# Devolutions Documentation

What can we help you with?

Devolutions Documentation
=========================

Need help? Here is the complete coverage for all Devolutions products, add-ons, and companion tools.

Remote access and connection management
---------------------------------------

# Profile - Devolutions Documentation

Profile
=======

In the [_**Profile**_](https://portal.devolutions.com/profile)
 section, you can manage the information and preferences of your Devolutions Account.

*   _**General**_: Set your name, your display language, your display theme, and the date format. Manage your profile image using the [Gravatar](https://gravatar.com/)
     system.
    
*   _**Contact information**_: Link an address and a phone number to your Devolutions Account.
    
*   _**Communication**_: Manage your Devolutions Newletters communication preferences.
    

You also have the option to permanently delete your Devolutions Account, but please note that **this action cannot be undone**. Once an account is deleted, it is irreversible. To understand the implications of this decision, we encourage you to read [How deleting Devolutions Accounts affects Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/kb/knowledge-base/deleting-devolutions-account-affect-hub/)
.

![Profile](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2011_2024_3.png)

Profile

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway
===================

Devolutions Gateway provides authorized just-in-time access to resources in segmented networks.

Key benefits of Devolutions Gateway include:

*   Reduced exposure to internal network resources with just-in-time RDP connections through the Devolutions Gateway.
    
*   Replaced static VPN and firewall rules with dynamic access rules controlled by Devolutions Server.
    
*   Enhanced security by giving remote access, or access to specific applications, in separate network segments on demand.
    
*   Improved productivity by eliminating the need to update VPN or firewall rules for temporary access.
    
*   Possible use of Devolutions Gateway with supported connection entry types (RDP, SSH, VNC, ARD, SCP, SFTP, PowerShell, Telnet, websites) in Remote Desktop Manager and supported data sources (Devolutions Server, Devolutions Hub Business).
    
*   Increased scalability by eliminating the need to use multiple VPNs to access many environments simultaneously. Devolutions Gateway can handle over 75 concurrent sessions, depending on the infrastructure.
    

![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/MARKETING_diagramme-gateway-instance2.png)

Learn more about [Devolutions Gateway](https://devolutions.net/gateway/)
.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Hub Business
===============================================================

On this page

*   [Steps for installing manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)
        

Devolutions Gateway allows for just-in-time connections at the session level, eliminating the need to change the system's global configuration. Devolutions Gateway provides a flexible and secure alternative to VPNs, offering easy access management and efficient use of network resources.

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure (Intermediate) Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate

Additionally, to [Launch an RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 with Devolutions Gateway only browsers that meet these minimal version requirements are compatible:

*   Chrome: 102
    
*   Firefox: 102
    
*   Safari: 16.4
    

Steps for installing manually
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)

The following instructions explain how to manually install Devolutions Gateway through Devolutions Hub Business.

As the installer is an MSI file, this method only works on Windows.

1.  Log in with an administrator Devolutions Hub Business account.
    
2.  Create an [application identity](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/application-users/manage-application-users/)
    .
    
3.  Once the application identity has been created, click on the _**Administration**_ tab.
    
    ![Administration tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Administration tab
    
4.  Click on Devolutions Gateway, which is under the _**Management**_ section.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0006_2024_1.png)
    
5.  Click on the _**More**_ button in the top right.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0007_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
6.  Click on _**Download public key**_. This key is unique to the Devolutions Hub Business account. It is automatically renamed to _provisioner.pem_. Keep track of where you saved this key, as it will be needed later.
    
    ![Gateway public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0009_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway public key
    
7.  Select _**Download MSI**_ from the dropdown.
    
    ![Download MSI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0008_2024_1.png)
    
    Download MSI
    
8.  Execute the installer.
    
    The installer should be run on the server hosting Devolutions Gateway.
    
9.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Setup Wizard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0010_2024_1.png)
    
    Setup Wizard
    
10.  Once the desired installation path is selected, click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Destination Folder](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0011_2024_1.png)
    
    Destination Folder
    
11.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Configure the Gateway installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0012_2024_1.png)
    
    Configure the Gateway installation
    
12.  Change the _**Ports**_ to the desired value and click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0013_2024_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
    HTTP(S) and TCP default ports are 7171 and 8181, respectively, but can be changed.
    
13.  Input the Devolutions Gateway access URI and click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Access URI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0014_2024_1.png)
    
    Access URI
    
14.  After clicking the top ellipsis button, select either a PFX file or a Certificate file, then enter the corresponding password. (If the listener is _**HTTP**_ this step is automatically skipped)
    
    ![Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0015_2024_1.png)
    
    Certificate
    
15.  Click on the ellipsis button and select the _**Provisioner Public Key**_ which was generated in Step 5.
    
    ![Public Key File](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0016_2024_1.png)
    
    Public Key File
    
16.  This screen shows a summary of the current paths/settings. It is possible to go _**Back**_ and modify them. If the settings are correct, click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Gateway setup summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0017_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway setup summary
    
17.  Click _**Install**_.
    
    ![Install button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0018_2024_1.png)
    
    Install button
    
18.  Click _**Finish**_ when the setup is complete.
    
    ![Finish button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0019_2024_1.png)
    
    Finish button
    
19.  Go back to the _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_ page in Devolutions Hub Business.
    
20.  Input the correct information.
    
    ![Information fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0020_2024_1.png)
    
    Information fields
    
    Once the Devolutions Gateway URL is entered, click on **_Auto-detect_** next to the **_TCP hostname_** to fill in the value automatically.
    
21.  By checking the _**Default**_ box, this Devolutions Gateway will be the one selected if none are specified or if _**Default**_ is chosen when connecting.
    
    ![Default option](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0021_2024_1.png)
    
    Default option
    
22.  Make certain the gateway can be reached by clicking _**Test Connection**_.
    
    ![Test Connection button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0022_2024_1.png)
    
    Test Connection button
    
23.  Click the _**Add**_ button to link your Devolutions Gateway installation to your Devolutions Hub Business.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0023_2024_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
24.  A rectangle will show the information for every Devolutions Gateway Hub link(s).
    
    ![Successful link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0024_2024_1.png)
    
    Successful link
    
25.  Enable [session recording](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/session-recording/)
    .
    

Visit [Remote Desktop Manager configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/rdm-configuration/)
 to learn more about linking Remote Desktop Manager and Devolutions Gateway.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway configuration  with Devolutions Server - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Server
=========================================================

On this page

*   [Differences between Side-by-side and Standard (managed) installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)
    
*   [Side-by-side installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
    
*   [Standard (managed) installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
    
*   [Enable Gateway recording](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)
    
*   [MSI installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
    
*   [Update Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)
    

This topic describes how to configure Devolutions Server to connect with Devolutions Gateway. There are three ways to install a Devolutions Gateway: the [_**Side-by-side installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
, the [_**Standard (managed) installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
 and the [_**MSI installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
.

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate

Additionally, to [Launch an RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 with Devolutions Gateway only browsers that meet these minimal version requirements are compatible:

*   Chrome: 102
    
*   Firefox: 102
    
*   Safari: 16.4
    

Differences between Side-by-side and Standard (managed) installation
--------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)

The _**Side-by-side installation**_ will be used if you need to install Devolutions Gateway on the same machine where Devolutions Server is hosted. It is a simplified installation process that will automatically configure the new Devolutions Gateway with information from the Devolutions Server instance (access URI and public key).

To install Devolutions Gateway on another machine than the one where Devolutions Server is hosted, you need to follow the _**Standard (managed) installation**_ process. The procedure is similar, but you will need to provide more information about your Devolutions Server instance to complete it.

Side-by-side installation
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)

This installation process is the easier of the two and is the recommended method for simpler network layouts.

1.  From the Devolutions Server Console, click on the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
    ![Companions tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp2083.png)
    
    Companions tab
    
2.  In the Devolutions Gateway section, click on _**Install**_.
    
3.  Choose _**Side-by-side installation**_.
    
    ![Side-by-side installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4047_2025_3.png)
    
    Side-by-side installation
    
    It is possible to download an [.msi](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     file to install Devolutions Gateway on an offline Devolutions Server.
    
4.  If default values do not work for your environment, enter the desired settings.
    
    *   _**HTTP Listener**_: HTTP(s) port to reach the Gateway. (7171 is default)
        
    *   _**TCP Listener**_: port used for the RDP sessions. (8181 is default)
        
5.  Click _**OK**_.
    
    ![OK button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0003_2025_1.png)
    
    OK button
    
6.  Go to the Devolutions Server web interface, connect with an administrator account.
    
7.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
8.  Click on the _**Ping**_ button for the desired gateway in the list to see if a connection can successfully be made. If the page was already open, refresh it first.
    
    ![Ping button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Ping button
    

Standard (managed) installation
-------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)

The _**Standard (managed)**_ method allows Devolutions Gateway to be installed on a separate server than Devolutions Server. It could be for performance purposes or access networks that Devolutions Server cannot access.

1.  From the Devolutions Server Console, click on the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
2.  In the Devolutions Gateway section, click on _**Install**_.
    
3.  Choose _**Standard installation**_.
    
    ![Standard installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4046_2025_3.png)
    
    Standard installation
    
4.  Choose between _**Download version**_ and _**Install from .msi file**_.
    
    It is possible to download an [_**.msi**_](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     file to install Devolutions Gateway on an offline Devolutions Server.
    
5.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Download version or Install from .msi file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0004_2025_1.png)
    
    Download version or Install from .msi file
    
6.  Enter the _**Access URI**_ information, for example https://gateway.example.com.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
7.  Choose the Devolutions Gateway _**Listeners**_ ports (by default they are 7171 and 8181). Devolutions Server will use the Access URI port (usually 443 or 7171) for health checks and initial configuration. Remote Desktop Manager will use ports 7171 and 8181 to connect to the Gateway. For instance, a web session using the Gateway will connect on port 7171, as will any registration via Devolutions Gateway. Port 8181 is used by sessions such as RDP.
    
    *   If HTTPS is chosen instead of HTTP in the step above, the _**Certificate configuration**_ will be needed.
        
    *   _**Certificate file**_: Needs to be a full chain certificate (.pfx, .p12, .pem, .crt).
        
    *   _**Certificate password**_: Only needed if a .pfx or .p12 certificate was used.
        
    *   _**Private key file**_: Only needed if a .pem or .crt was used as a certificate.
        
    
    Do not share the private key with other users, as it can be used to decrypt the communication between a user and Devolutions Gateway. Only the public key should be shared.
    
8.  Click _**Next**_.
    
9.  Choose between:
    
    *   _**Use public key from Devolutions Server instance 'Devolutions Server'**_: this option is used if the installed Devolutions Gateway is on the same server as the Devolutions Server;
        
    *   _**From file**_: If installing Devolutions Gateway on another computer, download the public key from the Devolutions Server you want to pair with that Devolutions Gateway. It is located under _**Administration – Devolutions Gateway**_.
        
    
    ![Download public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0007_2025_1.png)
    
    Download public key
    
10.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Key pair configuration](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0011.png)
    
    Key pair configuration
    
    If Devolutions Server is not installed locally, then check the _**From file**_ option, and select Devolutions Gateway's `.json` configuration file .See [Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)
     for a typical configuration file.
    
    [Devolutions' GitHub repository](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/?tab=readme-ov-file#configuration)
     also contains a list of the typical paths for the file, as well as all the stable options available to customize it.
    
11.  Click _**Install**_.
    
    ![Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0012.png)
    
    Summary
    
12.  Click _**Close**_.
    
    ![Installation Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0013.png)
    
    Installation Summary
    
13.  On the Devolutions Server web interface, connect with an administrator account.
    
14.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
15.  Click on the _**Add**_ button on the top right corner.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0006_2025_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
16.  Enter the following information.
    
    *   _**Name**_: Name of the gateway that will be displayed in Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**Description**_: Description of the gateway.
        
    *   _**Set as default**_: If enabled, this gateway will be selected by default when configuring Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**Devolutions Gateway URL**_: The Devolutions Gateway URL and Port that Devolutions Server will connect to, for example: **https://gateway.example.com:7171**.
        
    *   _**TCP Listening Port**_: Set the port with the same TCP port value configured in the Devolutions Server Console.
        
    *   _**TCP hostname**_: It should be resolvable by the machine initiating the connection (Remote Desktop Manager).
        
17.  Click _**Save**_.
    

![Gateway information](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0008_2025_1.png)

Gateway information

The gateway should now be visible in the list. It is possible to verify the status of the gateway with the _**Ping**_ button.

![Ping](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)

Ping

18.  Publish the _**Devolutions Gateway configuration**_.
    
19.  Publish the _**Revocation list**_. ![Publish the Gateway configuration and the Revocation list](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6066_2025_3.png)
    

Enable Gateway recording
------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)

Click [here](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/kb/how-to-articles/configure-recording-server/)
 to learn how to enable Devolutions Gateway recording in Devolutions Server.

MSI installation
----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)

It is possible to do an automated silent installation which will install a gateway with the default configuration. This is the recommended way to configure it through the [Devolutions.PowerShell module](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/devolutions-ecosystem/powershell/)
. Use the following command:

    msiexec.exe /i DevolutionsGateway-x86_64-VERSION.msi /quiet /norestart /log gateway_install.log
    

Update Devolutions Gateway
--------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)

Devolutions Gateway can be updated in three different ways depending on your needs:

*   Push updates via Devolutions Server web interface, in _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_. Using this method, instances can be updated singly or in bulk. The latter can be done quickly by toggling the _**Bulk update**_ option, selecting the gateways, and clicking on _**Update**_. Note that [Devolutions Agent](https://devolutions.net/agent/)
     is required to update from the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
*   Update manually through the Devolutions Server Console. To do so, head over the _**Companions**_ tab, select the Devolutions Gateway to update, click the _**Update**_ button, and follow the instructions then provided.
    
*   Run the [auto-updater PowerShell script](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/gateway-powershell/powershell-updater/)
    . This can be registered as a scheduled task to periodically check for updates.
    

#### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Workspace - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Workspace
=====================

On this page

*   [Workspace apps](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/overview/what-is-workspace/#workspace-apps)
    
*   [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/overview/what-is-workspace/#workspace-browser-extension)
    

Workspace apps
--------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/overview/what-is-workspace/#workspace-apps)

The Workspace apps are both mobile and desktop applications that bring together Devolutions Hub Business and Devolutions Server into a single, centralized, cloud-based location. Workspace simplifies and streamlines access and management in our solutions. It is the perfect companion tool for those who use our solutions.

The Workspace apps are available for iOS and Android devices as well as for Windows and macOS.

Workspace browser extension
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/overview/what-is-workspace/#workspace-browser-extension)

The Workspace browser extension is a web browser password plugin used in conjunction with Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub, which allows users to securely inject passwords into websites using credentials stored in their vaults.

It gives system administrators full control over the management of passwords, without affecting the user's productivity.

Advanced users, other browser extensions, or even JavaScript injection can all result in the password being read from the password edit control, even if it displays dots instead of the password. Any use of an external browser must be carefully weighed against your security requirements.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Installation - Devolutions Documentation

Installation
============

The Workspace browser extension is a free companion tool. It requires at least one of our Devolutions products to function at this time.

Click on one of the browser links below to start the installation of the Workspace browser extension:

*   [Chrome](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/chrome/)
    
*   [Firefox](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/firefox/)
    
*   [Edge](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/edge/)
    
*   [Opera](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/opera/)

Before using your application, you will have to complete a quick setup that involves selecting your Devolutions product(s), connecting to your account, and configuring security settings. The Workspace desktop app can be used with Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub Business.

Installing the Workspace desktop app
------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#installing-the-workspace-desktop-app)

The following steps detail how to install Workspace desktop app:

1.  [Download the Workspace desktop app](https://devolutions.net/workspace/)
     for Windows.
    
2.  Launch the installation wizard.
    
3.  Click on _**Install**_.
    

Setting up the Workspace desktop app
------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#setting-up-the-workspace-desktop-app)

Follow the steps below to perform the initial configuration of your Workspace desktop app:

1.  Once the installation is complete, in the _**Workspace apps setup**_ window, check the solution you wish to add, then click on _**Start setup**_.
    
2.  Next, enter the URL of the solution.
    
3.  Log in to your Devolutions Account.
    
    Adding a Devolutions Hub Business space requires the additional step of choosing which Hub to connect to.
    
4.  Choose a backup option (strongly recommended) and click on _**Next**_.
    
5.  Enable the use of a biometric lock (Windows Hello, Touch ID, etc.) or a master password (strongly recommended). The [Biometric lock setting](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/workspace-settings/biometric-lock-setting/)
     can be found later in _**File**_ – _**Settings**_ – _**Security and privacy**_.
    
    *   _**Use biometric lock**_: Your device will prompt you to authenticate using this method. It must first be configured on your device to work with Workspace.
        
    *   _**Use master password**_: Workspace will ask you to create a password of at least 8 characters.
        
6.  Click on _**Done**_ to complete the initial setup of your first space.
    

Adding more spaces can be done by clicking on the _**Add space**_ (cross icon), located either in the sidebar or the _**Home**_ section of Workspace, and following the same steps described above.

Before using your application, you will have to complete a quick setup that involves selecting your Devolutions product(s), connecting to your account, and configuring security settings. The Workspace desktop app can be used with Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub Business.

Installing the Workspace desktop app
------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#installing-the-workspace-desktop-app-1)

The following steps detail how to install Workspace desktop app:

1.  [Download the Workspace desktop app](https://devolutions.net/workspace/)
    for macOS.
    
2.  Launch the installation wizard.
    
3.  Click on _**Install**_.

    Adding a Devolutions Hub Business space requires the additional step of choosing which Hub to connect to.

     can be found later in _**File**_ – _**Settings**_ – _**Security and privacy**_.
    
    *   _**Use biometric lock**_: Your device will prompt you to authenticate using this method. It must first be configured on your device to work with Workspace.
        
    *   _**Use master password**_: Workspace will ask you to create a password of at least 8 characters.

Dependencies
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#dependencies)

In order to work properly on Linux, the Workspace desktop app is dependent on a few packages that must be downloaded and installed beforehand:

*   `libglib2.0-dev`
    
*   `libkeybinder-3.0-0`
    
*   `libwebkit2gtk-4.1-0`
    
*   `libsqlite3-dev`
    
*   `libcurl4t64`
    
*   `libayatana-appindicator3-1`
    
*   `libjpeg-turbo8`
    

The latest version of Workspace desktop app for Linux can be [downloaded from Cloudsmith](https://cloudsmith.io/~devolutions/repos/deb/packages/)
 or from [Devolution’ website](https://devolutions.net/workspace/)
, and is available for Ubuntu 2024.04 and up. The installation process is then the same as for the other operating systems.

Installing the Workspace desktop app
------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#installing-the-workspace-desktop-app-2)

The following steps detail how to install Workspace desktop app:

1.  [Download the Workspace desktop app](https://devolutions.net/workspace/)
    for Linux.
    
2.  Launch the installation wizard.
    
3.  Click on _**Install**_.

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#setting-up-the-workspace-desktop-app-2)

    *   _**Use biometric lock**_: Your device will prompt you to authenticate using this method. It must first be configured on your device to work with Workspace.
        
    *   _**Use master password**_: Workspace will ask you to create a password of at least 8 characters.

Custom installation
-------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/#custom-installation)

Custom installations can be created to facilitate data source deployment on multiple machines with the same preconfigured settings, similar to the [custom installer service](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/custom-installer-service/)
 for Remote Desktop Manager. Follow the steps below to create a `.cfg` configuration file which can then be imported into your users' Workspace app:

1.  In the Workspace desktop app, go to _**Help & Tools**_ – _**Custom installation**_.
    
2.  Click the _**Create configuration file**_ tab, and select an _**Active data source**_.
    
3.  Check the particular settings you wish to include in the custom installation, and toggle/define the options that best fit your needs.
    
4.  Once the settings have been configured, click the _**Create**_ button and choose a destination folder for the `.cfg` file.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# PAM with Remote Desktop Manager - Devolutions Documentation

PAM with Remote Desktop Manager
===============================

[Devolutions Privileged Access Management](https://devolutions.net/privileged-access-management/)
 provides all the following features. It is specifically designed to meet the needs of SMBs, providing enterprise-grade features to bring a level of protection usually only afforded to large organizations while at the same time being robust, easy to deploy, and affordable.

Here are some of its main features:

*   Ease of deployment and management
    
*   Secure password vault
    
*   Logging and reporting
    
*   Built-in multifactor authentication
    
*   Access brokering
    
*   Role-based access control
    

A license is required to enable the PAM module. Please contact our [sales department](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 for more information about the license.

The PAM features you have access to in Remote Desktop Manager will depend on the data source you are using.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Get started with SSO in Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Get started with SSO in Devolutions Hub Business
================================================

You can configure your Devolutions Hub Business users to log in using Single Sign-on (SSO) with Microsoft Entra ID or Okta credentials instead of using our Devolutions Account authentication. Follow the steps below to create and configure this feature in Devolutions Hub Business:

1.  Configure SSO authentication with:
    
    *   [Microsoft Azure](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-sso-hub-business/configure-sso-authentication-microsoft-azure/)
        
    *   [Okta](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-sso-hub-business/configure-sso-authentication-okta/)
        
2.  [Invite users for SSO in Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-sso-hub-business/invite-users-sso-hub-business/)
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-sso-hub-business/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Hub Business](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070846 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Hub Business")

# Devolutions Hub - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Hub
===============

Devolutions Hub is a highly secure team-based password manager that is part of our cloud services. It has been designed for both IT administrators and end users to store and share information across the whole organization, no matter the size. You can access and manage sensitive information from anywhere and with any supported web browser.

Your information is stored in entries of different types which are organized into vaults. Entries are managed directly from the web interface and no client application is required.

Security is at the core of Devolutions Hub since it is hosted by [Microsoft Azure](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/kb/knowledge-base/hosting-region-password-hub/)
, a highly trusted cloud services provider.

Devolutions Hub possesses powerful user management features, reports, and accessibility options. Users can be assigned roles and permissions and can also be members of user groups with predefined roles and permissions, streamlining the onboarding process.

Devolutions Hub can be used in combination with our Remote Desktop Manager as a data source as well as with other Devolutions products and companion tools, which you can find below.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/overview/what-is-hub/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Hub Business](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070846 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Hub Business")
    
*   [Devolutions Academy - Navigating Devolutions Hub](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/page/2633361-navigating-devolutions-hub?sid=4dd0e3d0-7c46-49cd-87a4-7785543da859&sid_i=0)
    
*   [Devolutions Academy – Introduction to Devolutions Hub](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/page/2813652-introduction-to-devolutions-hub?curriculum_activity_id=4268343&path_id=2543918&sid=5fb582e2-01ea-48ad-aa4b-28df6e2784e2&sid_i=0)

# Get started with Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Get started with Devolutions Hub Business
=========================================

On this page

*   [Setting up user groups and vaults](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#setting-up-user-groups-and-vaults)
    
*   [Inviting multiple users](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#inviting-multiple-users)
    
*   [Filling vaults with content](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#filling-vaults-with-content)
    
*   [Administration settings and reports](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#administration-settings-and-reports)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#see-also)
        

Here is a list of steps to help you get started with Devolutions Hub Business for your team environment.

Setting up _**user groups**_ and _**vaults**_
---------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#setting-up-user-groups-and-vaults)

In this video, we will demonstrate the proper configuration for Devolutions Hub Business as well as best practices for inviting an _**administrator**_, creating _**user groups**_, as well as setting up _**shared vaults**_, and assigning them _**roles**_ and _**permissions**_.

Inviting multiple _**users**_
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#inviting-multiple-users)

With this video, we will demonstrate how to add _**users**_ to your Devolutions Hub Business for both those who already have a Devolutions Account as well as those that do not.

Filling vaults with content
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#filling-vaults-with-content)

At this stage, we will show you four different ways to add and import _**entries**_ into your newly created Devolutions Hub Business. We will also cover the _**properties**_ and _**permissions**_ of _**entries**_. See also [9 secrets organizations should store in Devolutions Hub Business](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/02/spotlight-on-9-secrets-organizations-should-store-in-devolutions-hub-business/)
.

_**Administration settings**_ and _**reports**_
-----------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/get-started-hub-business/#administration-settings-and-reports)

In this final video, we will show you some of the administration _**management**_ settings, _**configuration**_, _**tools**_, and _**reports**_ that we think will benefit you as you finalize getting your Devolutions Hub Business all set up.

# Devolutions Launcher - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Launcher
====================

Devolutions Launcher is a companion tool for Devolutions Server. It can launch multiple remote sessions simultaneously, while giving system administrators full control. It is available on _**Windows only**_.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Download and installation - Devolutions Documentation

Download and installation
=========================

Once a [package](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/support-resources/getting-started-packages/)
 offering Devolutions Launcher has been purchased from the [Devolutions store](https://store.devolutions.net/package)
, you can follow these steps to download and install Devolutions Launcher:

1.  Download [Devolutions Launcher](https://devolutions.net/launcher/download)
     from our website and launch the executable file.
    
2.  Click _**Next**_ on the welcome page.
    
3.  Select a setup type:
    
    *   _**Typical**_: Installs the most common program features. Recommended for most users.
        
    *   _**Custom**_: Allows users to choose which program features will be installed and where they will be installed. Recommended for advanced users.
        
    *   _**Complete**_: All program features will be installed. (Requires most disk space) ![Choose a setup type](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/LAUNCHER2001_2024_3.png "Choose a setup type")
        
4.  Choose where to create Devolutions Launcher application shortcuts. Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Configure shortcuts](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB6030_2025_3.png)
    
    Configure shortcuts
    
5.  Read and accept the terms in the license agreement then click _**Next**_.
    
    ![End-user license agreement](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB6031_2025_3.png)
    
    End-user license agreement
    
6.  Click _**Install**_ to begin the installation.
    
    ![Ready to install](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB6032_2025_3.png)
    
    Ready to install
    
7.  Once done, click _**Finish**_ to complete the installation and launch Devolutions Launcher.
    
    ![Completed installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB6033_2025_3.png)
    
    Completed installation
    

#### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/installation/download-installation/#see-also)

*   [Licensing issues](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Server - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Server
==================

Devolutions Server is an self-hosted solution for storing and sharing information across your whole organization. Manage remote connections, credentials, and sensitive information with ease.

Use our _**user group-based access control**_ to grant permissions in a granular fashion. Advanced logging of all user activity is included to offer visibility in all aspects of the solution.

Because of its web architecture, you can offer Devolutions Server only from your intranet or publish it online.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/overview/what-is-server/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy – Devolutions Server path](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2942210-devolutions-server?sid_i=0)
    
*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Server](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2942210/activity/4899951)
    
*   [Devolutions Academy - Navigating Devolutions Server](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/page/2634255-navigating-devolutions-server?sid=e6228a6e-b1d0-46c2-ac20-70ede637d6aa&sid_i=0)

# Getting started - Devolutions Documentation

Getting started
===============

On this page

*   [Domain requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#domain-requirements)
    
*   [Installation steps](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#installation-steps)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#see-also)
        

A Devolutions Server instance is in itself a web server application which acts as a backend for our client applications. You can think of it as a specialized database for your data. All instances can be installed on the same physical server or spread across many. Devolutions Server can be installed through different [topologies](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/overview/topologies/)
.

Domain requirements
-------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#domain-requirements)

These requirements apply especially if you intend to use Automatic User Account Creation (see [Authentication](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/configuration/server-settings/general/authentication/)
) and/or User Groups to manage your instance.

1.  Create Active Directory groups to manage your instance. Typical examples are: Remote Desktop Manager Admins, Remote Desktop Manager Operators, Remote Desktop Manager Users.
    
2.  Add domain users to the Active Directory groups.
    
3.  Create a VaultDBOwner account that will be the owner of the database. Performing upgrades with this account will ensure the proper rights are held.
    
4.  Create a VaultDBRunner account that will be used as the identity of the website. This will allow you to harden the permissions to what is minimally required.
    

Installation steps
------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#installation-steps)

1.  Create a new instance of Devolutions Server (see [Create Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/)
    ).
    
2.  Create a Devolutions Server administrator account in the [User management](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/users/)
    .
    
3.  Create [User groups](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/user-groups/)
    .
    
4.  Add domain users or built-in users (see [User management](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/users/)
    ).
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy – Devolutions Server path](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2942210-devolutions-server?sid_i=0)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Installation - Devolutions Documentation

Installation
============

On this page

*   [Topology](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#topology)
    
*   [Installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#installation)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#see-also)
        

Topology
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#topology)

A Devolutions Server instance is a web application, allowing its services to be accessible over the Internet or an Intranet.

The recommended [topology](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/overview/topologies/)
 involves using two servers: one for the database and one for the web application. For smaller installations, a single server may be used; however, resources will be shared between both roles, which may impact performance.

Key points to consider:

*   Ensure that .NET 10.0 is installed on your machine before beginning the installation.
    
*   It is strongly recommended to enable SSL encryption to secure communication with the SQL Server instance. Follow Microsoft's guide: [Configure SQL Server Database Engine for encrypting connections](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-US/sql/database-engine/configure-windows/configure-sql-server-encryption)
    . We advise completing this step after the initial setup.
    
*   For full Active Directory integration, the application pool should use a domain identity, and both servers need to be joined to the domain.
    

Installation
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#installation)

*   [Installing web server prerequisites](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/installing-web-server-prerequisites/)
    
    After installing the prerequisites, test the IIS installation by navigating to `http://localhost`. If the IIS welcome screen does not appear, do not proceed. Any issues must be resolved before continuing.
    
*   [Database instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/database-setup/database-instance/)
    
*   [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/)
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Server](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070845 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Server")
    
*   [Devolutions Academy - Installing Devolutions Server](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/page/2942307-installing-devolutions-server?curriculum_activity_id=4493546&path_id=2942210&sid=1f0658ca-fdf5-4f74-a93f-a6a4b8853c09&sid_i=0)

# Remote Desktop Manager - Devolutions Documentation

Remote Desktop Manager
======================

On this page

*   [The Remote Desktop Manager ecosystem](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/overview/what-is-rdm/#the-remote-desktop-manager-ecosystem)
    
*   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/overview/what-is-rdm/#see-also)
    

Remote Desktop Manager is an application that integrates a comprehensive set of tools and managers to meet the needs of any IT team. It is designed to centralize remote connection technologies, credentials, and secure access to these resources. Most connections are established using either an external library or third-party software.

Remote Desktop Manager is compatible with over 200 relevant tools and technologies, including Apple Remote Desktop, Citrix, Dameware, FTP, Hyper-V, LogMeIn, Radmin, RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop), Remote Desktop Services, SSH Port Forward, SSH Shell, TeamViewer, Telnet, VMware, VNC, SCP, X Windows, and more!

The Remote Desktop Manager ecosystem
------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/overview/what-is-rdm/#the-remote-desktop-manager-ecosystem)

Remote Desktop Manager is available on **Windows**, **macOS**, **Linux**, **iOS**, and **Android**.

The solution is offered in **two editions**, regardless of the operating system:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Free** | For individual users who don't need to share remote connections and privileged passwords with other IT professionals. |
| **Team** | For MSPs, IT professionals & helpdesk technicians who need to share remote connections and privileged passwords with other team members. Purchasing a Team license grants the right to use Remote Desktop Manager on all available platforms. |

A desktop application is required to create a Team data source, which explains why the mobile applications are free. While they provide basic functionality similar to the Free edition for individual use, they can only access a Team data source, not manage it.

See also
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/overview/what-is-rdm/#see-also)

*   [Remote Desktop Manager FAQ: Overview edition](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/02/remote-desktop-manager-faq-overview-edition/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Getting started - Devolutions Documentation

Getting started
===============

Remote Desktop Manager offers great flexibility, making it suitable for both individuals and teams. Please refer to the checklist that best matches your environment:

*   [Checklist for **Solo (free)** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-individuals/)
    : Ideal for single users who do not wish to implement advanced security features.
    
*   [Checklist for **Native team** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/)
    : Designed for teams using Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub Business as their data source.
    
*   [Checklist for **Third-party team** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-small-teams/)
    : For environments intended to leverage Microsoft SQL Server or Microsoft Azure SQL as their data source.
    

Remote Desktop Manager macOS offers great flexibility, making it suitable for both individuals and teams. Please refer to the checklist that best matches your environment:

*   [Checklist for **Solo (free)** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-individuals/?tab=macos)
    : Ideal for single users who do not wish to implement advanced security features.
    
*   [Checklist for **Native team** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/?tab=macos)
    : Designed for teams using Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub Business as their data source.
    
*   [Checklist for **Third-party team** data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-small-teams/?tab=macos)
    : For environments intended to leverage Microsoft SQL Server or Microsoft Azure SQL as their data source.

# Client - Devolutions Documentation

Client
======

On this page

*   [Installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#installation)

*   [License](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#license-1)

    *   [Repo method](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#repo-method)

Remote Desktop Manager can be downloaded as setup files or as a binary compressed file (ZIP) via our [Devolutions website](https://devolutions.net/remote-desktop-manager/home/download)
. It can also be downloaded from the [Microsoft Store](https://apps.microsoft.com/store/detail/devolutions-remote-desktop-manager/XPFCXHF337W98S)
.

Installation
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#installation)

Depending on the downloaded media, either run the setup or extract the files from the archive in any folder and launch the executable.

If you wish to use a portable device or run multiple independent copies of the application, please consult [Portable (USB)](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/portable-usb/)
.

| OPTIONS | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Windows (.msi, x64)** | Download a Microsoft Software Installation package for 64-bit PCs (most desktops and laptops). |
| **Windows (.msi, arm64)** | Download a Microsoft Software Installation package for Windows devices using ARM. |
| **Windows (.msi, universal)** | Download a Microsoft Software Installation package containing binaries for both x64 and arm64 machines and devices. |
| **Windows (.exe, universal)** | Download a `.exe` package containing binaries for both x64 and arm64 machines and devices. |
| **Windows (.7z, x64)** | Download Remote Desktop Manager as a highly compressed, pre-optimized for x64, .7z file. Use [for better startup performance.](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/troubleshooting-articles/startup-performance/) |
| **Windows (.7z, arm64)** | Download Remote Desktop Manager as a highly compressed, pre-optimized for armx64, .7z file. Use for [better startup performance](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/troubleshooting-articles/startup-performance/)<br>. |
| **Windows (.zip, universal)** | Download Remote Desktop Manager as a compressed `.zip` file containing binaries for both x64 and arm 64 machines and devices. While `.7z` files are smaller, `.zip` files are more universally supported. |

License
-------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#license)

It is possible to try Remote Desktop Manager with a [Free trial](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/support-resources/getting-started-packages/free-trials/)
. If you possess a purchased license, please follow the instructions [Registration](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/registration/)
.

Data source
-----------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#data-source)

By default, a local data source is created using the SQLite format. You can add as many data sources as needed. Please consult [Data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/data-sources/)
 for more information.

To use an SQL Server or Azure SQL data source, refer to [Configure SQL Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/data-sources/data-sources-types/advanced-data-sources/microsoft-sql-server/configure/)
 or [Configure Azure SQL](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/data-sources/data-sources-types/advanced-data-sources/microsoft-azure-sql/configure/)
.

External applications
---------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#external-applications)

Configure your installation path for all external applications you intend to use such as RealVNC, Putty, Filezilla, etc. Set the paths in _**File**_ – _**Settings**_ – _**Application**_ – _**Paths**_.

-------------------------------------------

.

**Data source**
---------------

Installation
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#installation-2)

Depending on the downloaded media, either run the setup or extract the files from the archive in any folder and launch the executable. If this method of installation does not meet your needs, follow the instructions below.

### Repo method

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#repo-method)

Devolutions offer RDM through Cloudsmith for Debian and RedHat-based distributions. For Arch-based distributions, the package is available through AUR, and finally, Devolutions offers a Flatpak package that should cover most other platforms.

#### Debian and other Debian-based distributions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#debian-and-other-debian-based-distributions)

The repository must be set up before installing Remote Desktop Manager through Cloudsmith on any Debian-based distributions, including but not limited to Ubuntu, Pop!\_Os, and Kali Linux.

The following example showcases an Ubuntu system using APT as package manager.

1.  To set up the repositary, run the bash script that most fit your needs from the choices below:
    

###### Cloudsmith's automatic setup:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#cloudsmiths-automatic-setup)

    curl -1sLf \
      'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/setup.deb.sh' \
      | sudo -E bash
    

###### Forced specific distribution, release/version, architecture:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#forced-specific-distribution-releaseversion-architecture)

    curl -1sLf \
      'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/setup.deb.sh' \
      | sudo -E distro=some-distro codename=some-codename arch=some-arch bash
    

###### Manual configuration:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#manual-configuration)

    apt-get install -y debian-keyring  # debian only
    apt-get install -y debian-archive-keyring  # debian only
    apt-get install -y apt-transport-https
    # For Debian Stretch, Ubuntu 16.04 and later
    keyring_location=/usr/share/keyrings/devolutions-rdm-archive-keyring.gpg
    # For Debian Jessie, Ubuntu 15.10 and earlier
    keyring_location=/etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/devolutions-rdm.gpg
    curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/gpg.FE7407ECB26FD2FE.key' |  gpg --dearmor >> ${keyring_location}
    curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/config.deb.txt?distro=ubuntu&codename=xenial' > /etc/apt/sources.list.d/devolutions-rdm.list
    apt-get update
    

Be sure to replace **ubuntu** and **xenial** in the above with your actual operating system (distribution and distribution release/version).

2.  Install the package through your chosen package manager (APT here) by running the following script:
    

    sudo apt-get install remotedesktopmanager
    

#### RedHat and RedHat-based systems

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#redhat-and-redhat-based-systems)

The repository must be set up before installing Remote Desktop Manager through Cloudsmith on any RedHat-based distributions, including but not limited to RHEL, CentOS, SUSE, Fedora. For specific distribution based instructions please refer to [Cloudsmith’s guide](https://cloudsmith.io/~devolutions/repos/rdm/setup/#repository-setup-dnf)
.

The following example showcases a Fedora system using DNF as package manager.

1.  To set up the repositary, run the bash script that most fit your needs from the choices below:
    

##### Cloudsmith's automatic setup

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#cloudsmiths-automatic-setup-1)

    curl -1sLf \
      'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/setup.deb.sh' \
      | sudo -E bash
    

##### Forced specific distribution, release/version, architecture

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#forced-specific-distribution-releaseversion-architecture-1)

    curl -1sLf \
      'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/setup.deb.sh' \
      | sudo -E distro=some-distro codename=some-codename arch=some-arch bash
    

##### Manual configuration

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#manual-configuration-1)

    dnf install yum-utils pygpgme
    
    rpm --import 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/gpg.FE7407ECB26FD2FE.key'
    curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/devolutions/rdm/config.rpm.txt?distro=fedora&codename=29' > /tmp/devolutions-rdm.repo
    dnf config-manager --add-repo '/tmp/devolutions-rdm.repo'
    dnf -q makecache -y --disablerepo='*' --enablerepo='devolutions-rdm' --enablerepo='devolutions-rdm-source'
    

Be sure to replace **fedora** and **29** in the above with your actual operating system (distribution and distribution release/version).

2.   Install the package through your chosen package manager (DNF here) by running the following script:
    

    sudo dnf-get install remotedesktopmanager
    

#### Arch or Arch-based systems

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#arch-or-arch-based-systems)

For Arch-based distributions, including but not limited to Arch, Manjaro, EndeavourOS, Devolutions strongly recommends [Yay](https://github.com/Jguer/yay)
. The package can also be built from scratch.

##### Installing Remote Desktop Manager using Yay

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#installing-remote-desktop-manager-using-yay)

1.  If Yay is not already installed on the machine, do so by using this script:
    

    sudo pacman -Sy yay
    

2.  Install the remote-desktop-manager package:
    

    yay -Sy remote-desktop-manager
    

3.  Run a full system synchronization (recommended):
    

    yay -Syu
    

or only upgrade the remote-desktop-manager package (may cause dependency issues):

    yay -Sy remote-desktop-manager
    

##### Building the package using Pacman

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#building-the-package-using-pacman)

1.  Install base-devel with the following script:
    

    sudo pacman -S base-devel
    

2.  Clone the remote-desktop-manager repository in a particular location:
    

    git clone https://aur.archlinux.org/remote-desktop-manager.git
    

3.  Build and install the pack by running this script and replacing "path\_to\_the\_cloned\_repo":
    

    cd path_to_the_cloned_repo/
    makepkg -si
    

#### Flatpak-supported distributions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#flatpak-supported-distributions)

To install Remote Desktop Manager on Flatpak-supported distributions, start by setting up Flatpak on the machine according to Flatpak's [Quick Setup page](https://flatpak.org/setup/)
. Then, install the package using flathub by running these scripts:

    flatpak install flathub com.devolutions.remotedesktopmanager
    

    flatpak run com.devolutions.remotedesktopmanager
    

### **Manual installation on unsupported systems**

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/installation/client/#manual-installation-on-unsupported-systems)

Here is a simple guide to help installing Remote Desktop Manager Linux on an unsupported distro.

Here are required dependencies:

*   glibc 2.29
    
*   libwebkit2gtk-4.0 or libwebkit2gtk-4.1
    
*   ca-certificates
    
*   libsecret-1-0
    
*   gnome-keyring
    
*   libvte-2.91
    

Devolutions also suggests the following libraries:

*   libappindicator
    
*   xdotool
    
*   lsof
    

Install Remote Desktop Manager Linux using the following steps:

1.  Download the [latest .deb version of Remote Desktop Manager](https://devolutions.net/remote-desktop-manager/download/)
    .
    
2.  Make a directory:
    
    `mkdir ./extractedData/`
    
3.  Move the DEB file to the newly created folder and open that same folder:
    
    `mv ./RemoteDesktopManager_x.x.x.x_amd64.deb ./extractedData cd ./extractedData`
    
4.  Extract the DEB file's content:
    
    `ar -x RemoteDesktopManager_x.x.x.x_amd64.deb`
    
5.  Extract data.tar.xz content:
    
    `tar -xf data.tar.xz`
    
6.  Copy the extracted data’s bin/remotedesktopmananger to /bin:
    
    `cp -r /bin/remotedesktopmananger /bin`
    
7.  Copy the extracted data’s usr/lib/devolutions/RemoteDesktopManager to /usr/lib/devolutions/RemoteDesktopManager:
    
    `cp -r /usr/lib/devolutions/RemoteDesktopManager /usr/lib/devolutions/RemoteDesktopManager`
    

Remote Desktop Manager can then be launched using the remotedesktopmanager terminal command.

On the Apple Store, search for the Remote Desktop Manager application and install the application on your device.

When launching the application on your device, the _**Master password**_ window will appear, you can either decide to enter a password protecting Remote Desktop Manager, which will prompt you for your password every time you open the application or if you leave the field blank the application will open without prompting you for a password. You can also choose to use _**Touch ID**_ and _**Face ID**_. ![Master password window ](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMMOBILE6010.png)

Remote Desktop Manager iOS automatically creates an _**XML data source**_ the first time it is launched if you choose to skip the _**Setup Wizard**_. ![XML data source](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMMOBILE6011.png)

On the Google Play Store store, search for the Remote Desktop Manager application and install the application on your device.

When launching the application on your device, the _**Master Password**_ window will appear, you can either decide to enter a password protecting Remote Desktop Manager, which will prompt you for your password every time you open the application or if you leave the field blank the application will open without prompting your for a password.

Remote Desktop Manager Android will automatically create an XML data source upon first launch.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

 one for free. For help creating your account, check out [our guide](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/)
.

.

# Create your Devolutions Account - Devolutions Documentation

Create your Devolutions Account
===============================

On this page

*   [Devolutions Account creation](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/#devolutions-account-creation)
    
*   [Forgotten password](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/#forgotten-password)
    

To get started, create your free Devolutions Account by following the steps below.

Devolutions Account creation
----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/#devolutions-account-creation)

1.  Go to your [account login](https://portal.devolutions.com/)
    .
    
2.  Click on _**Create your account**_ to start the process.
    
    ![Create your account](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2013_2024_3.png)
    
    Create your account
    
3.  Fill in the fields with your information, then click _**Create account**_.
    
    By clicking on _**Create account**_ , you confirm that you have read and accepted our [Software License and Subscription Agreement](https://devolutions.net/legal/customer-agreements/)
     and [Privacy Policy](https://devolutions.net/legal/privacy/)
    .
    
    ![Account information](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2014_2024_3.png)
    
    Account information
    
4.  Go to your email inbox and open the activation email that was sent to you.
    
    The activation link email might be in your spam/junk folder. For Gmail accounts, also check the _**Promotions**_ folder.
    
    It may take some time to receive it. If you do not receive the email, follow the [Forgotten password](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/#forgotten-password)
     steps below.
    
5.  Click _**Activate**_ in the email to verify your account creation.
    
    ![Activate your account](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2015_2024_3.png)
    
    Activate your account
    

Your account has been created!

Forgotten password
------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/profile/create-devolutions-account/#forgotten-password)

If you did not receive the activation email or have forgotten your password, follow the steps below to resolve the issue:

1.  Go to the [Devolutions Account login page](https://portal.devolutions.com/)
    .
    
2.  Enter your _**Username**_ (Devolutions Account email address), then click _**Continue**_.
    
    ![Username](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2016_2024_3.png)
    
    Username
    
3.  Click _**Forgot your password?**_.
    
    ![Forgot your password?](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2017_2024_3.png)
    
    Forgot your password?
    
4.  Enter your username again if required, then click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Username](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2018_2024_3.png)
    
    Username
    
5.  Copy the code received in the email and paste it in the _**Code**_ field, then click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Email code](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD2019_2024_3.png)
    
    Email code
    
6.  Enter a new password that follows the security guidelines, then click _**Update my password**_.
    
    ![New password](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_cloud_Cloud4027.png)
    
    New password
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Send Standalone - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send Standalone
===========================

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)
    
*   [How to use Devolutions Send Standalone](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)
    
*   [How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)
    
*   [Technical details](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)
        

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 features a secure method to generate a link to share secrets instead of using insecure email to send sensitive data.

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)

The in-app version of Devolutions Send is currently under development and will be progressively deployed in Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub. More information will come in the future.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature set of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kb.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

How to use Devolutions Send Standalone
--------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)

1.  Go to the [Devolutions Send Standalone](https://send.devolutions.com/)
     website.
    
2.  Enter the _**Sender email**_, which is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    
3.  Enter your _**Secure message**_ to encrypt.
    
    *   A file of maximum 1 MB can be added to the secure message as well.
        
4.  Add a _**Passphrase**_ for extra security (mandatory if the recipient does not have a Devolutions Account, optional otherwise).
    
    *   _**Additional security options**_:
        
        *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days or 1 week.
            
        *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple views option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
            
        *   It is recommended to enable the _**Allow recipient to delete message**_ option.
            
5.  Read and agree to our online services terms.
    
6.  Click on _**Create secure link**_ to get the in-browser encrypted link. ![Interface](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0001_2024_3.png)
    
7.  Click on _**Copy to clipboard**_ and send it to the recipient(s).
    

How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret
---------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)

1.  Click on the received encrypted link.
    
    A Devolutions Send Standalone secret will always start with https://send.devolutions.com/receive/.
    
2.  Click on _**Unmask text**_.
    
    Make certain to be in a private setting before reading this message if it contains sensitive information.
    
    ![Unmask text](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0002_2024_3.png)
    
    Unmask text
    
3.  Enter the _**Passphrase**_ the sender provided (if necessary) and click on _**Decrypt**_. ![Decrypt button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0187.png)
    
4.  Once done, click on _**Delete Now**_.
    
5.  Click _**Yes**_. ![Yes button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0189.png) ![Deleted secure message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0190.png)
    

Technical details
-----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)

The core tenant of Devolutions Send is that Devolutions itself cannot decrypt the user's secret. This is accomplished via client-side (browser) encryption through a Rust program compiled to WASM (WebAssembly) in-browser. Therefore, Devolutions does not hold the encryption key and cannot decrypt the data.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/how-organizations-can-safely-share-confidential-information-with-devolutions-send/ "Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# PAM with Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

PAM with Devolutions Hub Business
=================================

[Devolutions Privileged Access Management](https://devolutions.net/privileged-access-management/)
 for Devolutions Hub Business takes care of Entra ID privileged accounts. It is specifically designed to meet the needs of SMBs, providing enterprise-grade features to bring a level of protection usually only afforded to large organizations while at the same time being robust, easy to deploy, and affordable.

Since Devolutions Hub Business is a cloud-based solution, you must download and install the [Devolutions Hub Services](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/pam-service/)
 to establish communication between your Devolutions Hub Business and your internal resources.

Here are some of its main features:

*   Secure PAM vault managing all your different privileged accounts
    
*   Checkout request approval
    
*   Automatic password reset
    
*   Secure password injection
    
*   Administration report
    

A license is required to enable the PAM module. Please contact our [sales department](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 for more information about the license.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)
