# Devolutions Send - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send
================

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)
    
*   [How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-hub-business)
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        
*   [Send copy of a password](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-copy-of-a-password)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#see-also)
        

Send a password through in-app secure messaging or email external contacts directly from an entry. Create a shareable link to send secrets outside your organization securely.

This feature needs the user to have _**Send messages with attachments**_ enabled. This option can be found under _**Administration**_ – _**Users**_. It is enabled by default for each user.

The _**External password sharing**_ option also needs to be enabled for this feature to work. The option can be found under _**Administration**_ – _**System settings**_ – _**Advanced**_. It is enabled by default.

![External sharing](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0015_2025_1.png)

External sharing

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 is an alternative for those who do not use our products.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature set of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kB.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Hub Business
---------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-hub-business)

1.  Open the Devolutions Hub Business web page.
    
2.  Click on _**Messages**_ next to the user's avatar.
    
    ![Messages](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_Hub0015.png)
    
    Messages
    
3.  Click _**New message**_.
    
    ![New message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_Hub0014.png)
    
    New message
    
4.  Select one of the three available options:
    
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        

### Send in-app

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)

![Send in-app](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0019_2025_1.png)

Send in-app

This feature is covered in [_**Secure messages**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/secure-messages/)
.

### Send by email

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)

![Send by email](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0020_2025_1.png)

Send by email

1.  Enter the _**Recipient(s) email**_.
    
2.  Enter the information in the _**Secure message**_ field.
    
    *   Files can be securely shared by clicking _**Upload file**_.
        
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks or 1 month.
        
    *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to _**Unlimited**, **Single view**_ or _**Multiple views**._ The latter is useful for setting an exact number of possible views.
        
    
3.  Click _**Submit**_.
    
    ![Submit](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0016_2025_1.png)
    
    Submit
    

### Create shareable link

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)

![Create shareable link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0021_2025_1.png)

Create shareable link

1.  Enter the information in the _**Secure Message**_ field.
    
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks or 1 month.
        
    *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
        
    
2.  Click on _**Create link**_.
    
    ![Create link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0017_2025_1.png)
    
    Create link
    
3.  Copy the link and send it to the intended individual(s).
    
    ![Copy to clipboard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0018_2025_1.png)
    
    Copy to clipboard
    

Send copy of a password
-----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-copy-of-a-password)

It is also possible to send a password directly to another user in-app or outside of Devolutions Hub Business by using Devolutions Send. The user needs to have [_**View**_ permission](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/configuration-security/system-permissions/roles-permissions/)
 on that entry to send it.

![Send copy](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0022_2025_1.png)

Send copy

The main difference with this option is that the password is automatically added and hidden as the message. The password can only be edited if the text is revealed (by clicking the eye icon).

![Editable only when revealed](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_Hub0022.png)

Editable only when revealed

To learn more about the _**Secure message**_ features, please refer to the above section on [How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-hub-business)
.

# Devolutions Send - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send
================

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)
    
*   [How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-server)
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        
*   [Send copy of a password](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-copy-of-a-password)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#see-also)
        

Send a password through in-app secure messaging or email external contacts directly from an entry. Create a shareable link to send secrets outside your organization securely.

This feature needs Devolutions Server to have _**SMTP**_ configured. This option can be found under _**Administration**_ – _**Server settings**_ – _**Email**_.

Additionally, _**Allow users to send password with Devolutions Send**_ needs to be enabled. This option can be found under _**Administration**_ – _**Server settings**_ – _**Features**_. It is enabled by default.

![Allow users to send password with](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0000_2025_1.png)

Allow users to send password with

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 is an alternative for those who do not use our products.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature set of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kB.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Server
---------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-server)

1.  Open the Devolutions Server web page.
    
2.  Click on _**Messages**_ next to the user's avatar. ![Messages](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0011_2024_1.png)
    
3.  Click _**New message**_. ![New message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0002_2024_1.png)
    
4.  Select one of the three available options:
    
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        

### Send in-app

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)

![Send in-app](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0009_2024_1.png) This feature is covered in [_**Secure messages**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/messages/)
.

### Send by email

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)

![Send by email](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0003_2024_1.png)

Send by email

1.  Enter the recipient(s) email in the _**To**_ field.
    
2.  Enter the information in the _**Secure message**_ field.
    
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks or 1 month.
        
    *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
        
    
3.  Click _**Send by email**_. ![Send by email](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0001_2025_1.png)
    

### Create shareable link

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)

![Create shareable link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0004_2024_1.png)

Create shareable link

1.  Enter the information in the _**Secure message**_ field.
    
    *   Files can be securely shared by clicking _**Attachment**_.
        
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks or 1 month.
        
    *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
        
    
2.  Click on _**Create link**_. ![Create link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0002_2025_1.png)
    
3.  Copy the link and send it to the intended individual(s). ![Copy to Clipboard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0003_2025_1.png)
    

Send copy of a password
-----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-copy-of-a-password)

It is also possible to send a password directly to another user in-app or outside of Devolutions Server by using Devolutions Send. The user needs to have [view permission](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/user-groups-based-security/permissions/)
 on that entry to send it. ![Send Copy](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0004_2025_1.png)

The main difference with this option is that the password is automatically added and hidden as the message in one of the three messaging option. The password can only be edited if the text is revealed (by clicking _**View**_).

To learn more about the _**Secure message**_ features, please refer to the above section on [How to use Devolutions Send with Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-with-devolutions-server)
.

*   [Devolutions Academy – Sending secure messages](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2942210/activity/4493544)

# Devolutions PowerShell - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions PowerShell
======================

On this page

*   [Getting started with the Devolutions.PowerShell module](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#getting-started-with-the-devolutionspowershell-module)
    *   [PowerShell Gallery (recommended)](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#powershell-gallery-recommended)
        
    *   [Cloudsmith](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#cloudsmith)
        
    *   [Offline](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#offline)
        
*   [Examples](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#examples)
    *   [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#remote-desktop-manager)
        
    *   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#devolutions-server)
        
    *   [Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#devolutions-hub)
        
*   [Uninstalling the Devolutions.PowerShell module](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#uninstalling-the-devolutionspowershell-module)
    

Devolutions products fully integrate Microsoft PowerShell, offering powerful scripting and automation capabilities. You can control Devolutions products themselves and, through Remote Desktop Manager, run PowerShell scripts across your environment. With that in mind, here is how PowerShell is used across the Devolutions ecosystem.

| Integration | Purpose | Reference |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Devolutions.PowerShell module | This PowerShell module is used to interact directly with Devolutions products. | *   [PowerShell Gallery](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/Devolutions.PowerShell/) |
| Remote Desktop Manager actions | You may define a PowerShell script to run as a batch action against one or more hosts. | *   [Custom PowerShell commands](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/rdm-powershell/powershell-scripting/custom-powershell-commands/)<br>    <br>*   [Batch edit with PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/rdm-powershell/batch-edit-folders-custom-powershell-commands/)<br>    <br>*   [Modifying a synchronizer source](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/rdm-powershell/powershell-scripting/custom-powershell-commands/change-synchronizer-source/) |
| Remote Desktop Manager reports | This entry type supports running a PowerShell script to generate a report. | *   [Custom PowerShell report](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/rdm-powershell/create-custom-field-report/) |
| Remote Desktop Manager entry types | Both the PowerShell local and PowerShell remote entry types support running scripts. |     |
| Privileged access management (PAM) providers and password propagation | Within Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub, PowerShell powers custom PAM providers and password propagation scripts. | *   [Devolutions Server custom PAM provider](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/server/getting-started/anyidentity/create-anyidentity-pam-provider-dvls/)<br>    <br>*   [Devolutions Server PAM password propagation scripts](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/server/propagation-scripts/) |

Getting started with the Devolutions.PowerShell module
------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#getting-started-with-the-devolutionspowershell-module)

The Devolutions.PowerShell module requires [PowerShell 7.4 or later](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/scripting/install/installing-powershell?view=powershell-7.4)
, and is supported on Windows, macOS, and Linux operating systems.

Windows PowerShell or earlier versions of PowerShell 7 are not supported because the PowerShell module is built from the same core as Remote Desktop Manager, and therefore requires a version of PowerShell using a compatible version of the .NET runtime (.NET 9).

### PowerShell Gallery (recommended)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#powershell-gallery-recommended)

The Devolutions.PowerShell module is available in the [PowerShell Gallery](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/Devolutions.PowerShell)
 and it is the recommended default installation method:

    Install-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -Force
    

Since the PowerShell Gallery is usually a repository marked as untrusted (packages are not curated or reviewed), using `-Force` is required to avoid the confirmation prompt.

### Cloudsmith

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#cloudsmith)

As an alternative to the PowerShell Gallery, we offer a [Devolutions PowerShell repository](https://cloudsmith.io/~devolutions/repos/powershell/packages/)
 hosted by [Cloudsmith](https://cloudsmith.com/)
.

1.  Register the Devolutions PowerShell repository, which can be marked as trusted:
    
        Register-PSRepository -Name 'Devolutions' -SourceLocation 'https://nuget.cloudsmith.io/devolutions/powershell/v2/' -InstallationPolicy Trusted
        
    
2.  Uninstall previous versions of the Devolutions.PowerShell module installed from the PowerShell Gallery:
    
        Uninstall-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -AllVersions
        
    
3.  Install the Devolutions.PowerShell module explicitly from the "Devolutions" repository:
    
        Install-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -Repository Devolutions
        
    
4.  Confirm that the installation source repository for the Devolutions.PowerShell module is "Devolutions" and not "PSGallery":
    
        Get-InstalledModule Devolutions.PowerShell | Select-Object -Property Name, Repository
        
        Name                   Repository
        ----                   ----------
        Devolutions.PowerShell Devolutions
        
    

Since the Devolutions.PowerShell module is available in more than one registered repository, the `-Repository` parameter becomes mandatory. However, if you've marked the "Devolutions" repository as trusted, `-Force` is unnecessary to avoid the confirmation prompt.

### Offline

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#offline)

If you need to install the Devolutions.PowerShell module on a system with limited or no Internet access, you can do so by following these steps:

1.  Create a new PowerShell repository called "local" in your chosen directory; the example below uses `C:\PSRepo`.
    
        $RepoPath = "C:\PSRepo"
        New-Item -Path $RepoPath -ItemType 'Directory' -Force | Out-Null
        Register-PSRepository -Name 'local' -SourceLocation $RepoPath -PublishLocation $RepoPath -InstallationPolicy Trusted
        
    
2.  Download the `.nupkg` file for the Devolutions.PowerShell module using the _**Download the raw nupkg file**_ button under _**Manual Download**_ in the [PowerShell Gallery](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/Devolutions.PowerShell)
    . Copy the `.nupkg` file to the previously created, local PowerShell repository directory.
    
3.  Uninstall previous versions of the Devolutions.PowerShell module installed from other sources.
    
        Uninstall-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -AllVersions
        
    
4.  Install the Devolutions.PowerShell module explicitly from the `local` repository.
    
        Install-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -Repository local
        
    
5.  Confirm that the installation source for the Devolutions.PowerShell module is `local`.
    
        Get-InstalledModule Devolutions.PowerShell | Select-Object -Property Name, Repository
        
        Name                   Repository
        ----                   ----------
        Devolutions.PowerShell local
        
    

Alternatively, a directory on a network share can be used instead of a local directory, making it easier to distribute the PowerShell module on a local network.

Examples
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#examples)

To quickly get started with some common Devolutions.PowerShell examples, read on below.

### Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#remote-desktop-manager)

    # [Import module]
    Import-Module Devolutions.PowerShell
    
    # [Load data source] Example for a local data source (SQLite) or SQL Server
    $DatasourceLocal = Get-RDMDataSource -Name "Local data source"; Set-RDMCurrentDataSource $DatasourceLocal
    
    $DatasourceSQL = Get-RDMDataSource -Name "SQL Server"; Set-RDMCurrentDataSource $DatasourceSQL
    
    # [Create vault] Only the SQL Server data source supports vaults (as do Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub)
    $Vault = New-RDMRepository -Name 'MyVault' -Description 'My vault description' -SetRepository | Set-RDMCurrentRepository | Update-RDMUI
    
    # [Retrieve vault]
    Get-RDMRepository -Name 'MyVault'
    
    # [Create entry] Example to create an RDP and Credential entry
    $Entry = New-RDMSession -Host 'MyHost' -Type RDPConfigured -Name 'MyHost'; Set-RDMSession -Session $Entry -Refresh; Update-RDMUI
    
    $Entry = New-RDMSession -Name 'MyCredential' -Type Credential; $Entry.Credentials.Username = 'Administrator'; Set-RDMSession $Entry -Refresh; Set-RDMSessionPassword -ID $Entry.ID -Password (ConvertTo-SecureString 'Test123$' -AsPlainText -Force)
    
    # [Retrieve entries]
    Get-RDMSession -GroupName 'MyFolder' -Name 'MyHost'
    
    # [Update entry]
    $Entry = Get-RDMSession -Name 'MyHost'; $Entry.Name = 'MyUpdatedHost'; Set-RDMSEssion $Entry | Update-RDMUI
    
    # [Export entries]
    $Entries = Get-RDMSession; $Entries | Select-Object * | Export-CSV 'C:\Export\FileName.csv' -NoTypeInformation
    
    # [Remove entry]
    Get-RDMSession -Name 'MyUpdatedHost' | Remove-RDMSession; Update-RDMUI
    

### Devolutions Server

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#devolutions-server)

    # [Import module]
    Import-Module Devolutions.PowerShell
    
    # [Load data source]
    New-DSSession -Credential (Get-Credential) -BaseURI 'https://MyServer/dvls/'
    
    # [Create vault]
    $Vault = New-DSVault -Name 'MyVault' -Description 'My vault description'
    
    # [Retrieve vault]
    Get-DSVault -All | Where-Object DisplayName -EQ 'MyVault'
    
    # [Create entry]
    New-DSRDPEntry -Name 'MyHost' -HostName 'MyHost' -Username 'Administrator' -Password 'Test123$' -Domain 'MyDomain' -VaultID 'VaultGUID'
    
    New-DSCredentialEntry -Name 'MyCredential' -Username 'Administrator' -Password 'Test123$' -Domain 'MyDomain' -VaultID 'VaultGUID'
    
    # [Retrieve entries]
    Get-DSEntry -FilterBy 'Name' -FilterMatch 'StartsWith' -FilterValue 'MyHost' -SearchAllVaults
    
    # [Update entry]
    $Entry = Get-DSEntry -EntryId 'EntryGUID'; $Entry.Name = 'MyUpdatedHost'; Update-DSEntryBase -JsonBody (ConvertTo-JSON -InputObject $Entry -Depth 10)
    
    # [Export entries]
    $Entries = Get-DSEntry -SearchAllVaults; $Entries | Select-Object * | Export-CSV 'C:\Export\FileName.csv' -NoTypeInformation
    
    # [Remove entry]
    Remove-DSEntry -EntryID 'EntryGUID'
    

### Devolutions Hub

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#devolutions-hub)

    # [Import module]
    Import-Module Devolutions.PowerShell
    
    # [Load data source]
    Connect-HubAccount -Url 'https://myhub.devolutions.app' -ApplicationKey 'ApplicationKey' -ApplicationSecret 'ApplicationSecret'
    
    # [Create vault]
    $Vault = New-HubVault -VaultName 'MyVault' -VaultDescription 'My vault description'
    
    # [Retrieve vault]
    Get-HubVault
    
    # [Create entry]
    $Entry = [Devolutions.Hub.PowerShell.Entities.Hub.PSDecryptedEntry]@{
        PsMetadata = [Devolutions.Hub.PowerShell.Entities.Hub.PSEntryMetadata]@{
            Name = 'MyHost'
            ConnectionType = [Devolutions.RemoteDesktopManager.ConnectionType]::Credential
        }
        Connection = [Devolutions.RemoteDesktopManager.Business.Connection]@{
            Credentials = [Devolutions.RemoteDesktopManager.Business.CredentialsConnection]@{
                CredentialType = [Devolutions.RemoteDesktopManager.CredentialResolverConnectionType]::Default
                UserName = 'Administrator'
                Password = 'Test123$'
            }
        }
    }
    
    New-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID' -PSDecryptedEntry $Entry
    
    # [Retrieve entries]
    Get-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID' | Where-Object { $PSItem.PSMetaData.Name -EQ 'MyHost' }
    
    # [Update entry]
    $Entry = Get-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID' -EntryId 'EntryGUID'; $Entry.PsMetadata.Name = 'MyUpdatedHost'; Set-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID' -EntryId $Entry.Entry.ID.Guid -PSDecryptedEntry $Entry
    
    # [Export entries]
    $Entries = Get-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID'; $Entries | Select-Object * | Export-CSV 'C:\Export\FileName.csv' -NoTypeInformation
    
    # [Remove entry]
    Remove-HubEntry -VaultId 'VaultGUID' -EntryId 'EntryGUID'
    

**Uninstalling** the Devolutions.PowerShell **module**
------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/overview/what-is-powershell/#uninstalling-the-devolutionspowershell-module)

Uninstall all versions of the Devolutions.PowerShell module:

    Uninstall-Module Devolutions.PowerShell -AllVersions
    

If the module is installed via Cloudsmith, you may unregister the "Devolutions" repository like so:

    Unregister-PSRepository Devolutions
    

Finally, if you have installed the module offline, you may unregister the "local" file-based repository and delete the associated directory (your directory name may be different):

    Unregister-PSRepository local
    Remove-Item "C:\PSRepo" -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Devolutions Send - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send
================

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)
    
*   [Using Devolutions Send with Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#using-devolutions-send-with-remote-desktop-manager)
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        
    *   [Send a password from a credential entry](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-a-password-from-a-credential-entry)
        
    *   [Disabling Devolutions Send in Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#disabling-devolutions-send-in-remote-desktop-manager)
        
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#see-also)
        

Devolutions Send features a secure method to generate a link to share secrets instead of using insecure email to send sensitive data. Send a password through in-app secure messaging or create a shareable link to send secrets outside your organization securely.

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#features)

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 is an alternative for those who do not use our products.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature sets of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kB.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

Using Devolutions Send with Remote Desktop Manager
--------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#using-devolutions-send-with-remote-desktop-manager)

These steps are valid for Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub Business data sources. Only the [Send a password from a credential entry](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-a-password-from-a-credential-entry)
 is available for SQL datasources.

1.  In the ribbon, navigate to the _**Window**_ tab.
    
2.  Click _**Messages**_.
    
    ![Messages button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0008_2025_1.png)
    
    Messages button
    
3.  Click _**Send message**_.
    
    ![Send message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0017_2024_1.png)
    
    Send message
    
4.  Select one of the three available options:
    
    *   [Send in-app](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)
        
    *   [Send by email](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)
        
    *   [Create shareable link](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)
        

### Send in-app

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-in-app)

![Send in-app](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0003_2025_1.png)

Send in-app

This feature is covered in [_**Secure messages**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/window/secure-messages/)
.

### Send by email

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-by-email)

![Send by email](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0004_2025_1.png)

Send by email

1.  Enter the recipient(s) email in the _**To**_ field.
    
2.  Enter the information in the _**Secure message**_ field.
    
    *   _**Attachments**_ such as user entries and files can be added.
        
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks, 1 month or custom.
        
    *   The _**View**_ limit can be set to _**Unlimited**_, _**Single view**_ or _**Multiple views**_. The latter is useful for setting an exact number of possible views.
        
    
3.  Click _**Send**_.
    
    ![Send](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6023_2025_3.png)
    
    Send
    

### Create shareable link

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#create-shareable-link)

![Create shareable link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0005_2025_1.png)

Create shareable link

1.  Enter the information in the _**Message**_ field.
    
    *   A _**Passphrase**_ may be added for additional security.
        
    *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days, 1 week, 2 weeks, 1 month or custom.
        
    *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to _**Unlimited**_, _**Single view**_ or _**Multiple views**_. The latter is useful for setting an exact number of possible views.
        
    
2.  Click on _**Create link**_.
    
    ![Create link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0016_2025_1.png)
    
    Create link
    
3.  Copy the link and send it to the intended individual(s).
    
    ![Copy and close](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0017_2025_1.png)
    
    Copy and close
    

### Send a password from a credential entry

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#send-a-password-from-a-credential-entry)

![Send via message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0007_2025_1.png)

Send via message

Sending a password from a credential entry on a Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub Business data source is possible with all three options showcased in the [Using Devolutions Send with Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#using-devolutions-send-with-remote-desktop-manager)
 section.

### Disabling Devolutions Send in Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#disabling-devolutions-send-in-remote-desktop-manager)

1.  In an SQL data source, go to the _**Administration**_ tab.
    
2.  Click on _**System settings**_.
    
    ![System settings](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0006_2025_1.png)
    
    System settings
    
3.  Under _**Application**_ – _**General**_ – _**General**_, enable _**Disable send message in dashboard**_.
    
    ![Disable send message in dashboard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW0002_2025_1.png)
    
    Disable send message in dashboard
    
4.  Click _**Save**_.
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/send/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/how-organizations-can-safely-share-confidential-information-with-devolutions-send/ "Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send")

# Licenses - Devolutions Documentation

Licenses
========

The _**Licenses**_ section of the Devolutions Portal lists all the licenses associated with its Devolutions Account. By default, only the main contact, i.e., the person who first communicated with our [sales team](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
, has the right to see and interact with the licenses. The main contact can share licenses with other users by clicking on the _**Share**_ button.

![The Licenses section of the Devolutions Portal](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD6000_2026_1.png)

The Licenses section of the Devolutions Portal

Additionally, this is where you can download `.lic` files for the licenses you own. These can then be used to import licenses in many different scenarios, such as [Remote Desktop Manager Offline registration](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/administration/licenses/#offline-registration)
.

The _**Licenses**_ section is a listing of your product licensing information only. You will be required to save the serial into the appropriate Devolutions application to register.

Communicate with Devolutions' [sales team](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 for assistance if you are the main contact but cannot see your purchased licenses.

#### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/licenses/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions store – Tailored packages for your IT needs](https://store.devolutions.net/package)
    
*   [Getting started with Devolutions packages](https://docs.devolutions.net/portal/support-resources/getting-started-packages/)
    
*   [Licensing issues](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

Remote access and connection management
---------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/devolutions-ecosystem/#remote-access-and-connection-management)

| PRODUCT | DESCRIPTION | INSTALLATION |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [**Remote Desktop Manager (RDM)**](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/overview/what-is-rdm/) | Remote Desktop Manager is an application used to manage and centralize remote access technologies, privileged passwords, documents and shared information. | Windows, macOS, Linux, iOS, Android |
| [**Devolutions Gateway**](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/) | Devolutions Gateway provides authorized just-in-time access to resources in segmented networks. | Windows, Linux |
| [**Devolutions Launcher**](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/) | Devolutions Launcher provides users with a simple method of launching remote sessions, while also giving system administrators full control of whether passwords and sensitive information are divulged or kept secret. All privileged account information is transmitted directly from the password vault into the remote session via Launcher's secure API, keeping with the latest security standards. | Windows |
| [**Workspace apps**](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/overview/what-is-workspace/) | The Workspace apps are both mobile and desktop applications that bring together Devolutions Hub Business and Devolutions Server into a single, centralized, cloud-based location. Workspace simplifies and streamlines access and management in our solutions. | Windows, macOS, Linux, iOS, Android |
| [**Workspace browser extension**](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/) | The Workspace browser extension is a free browser plugin used in conjunction with Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub, which allows users to securely inject passwords into websites using credentials stored in their vaults. | Windows, macOS, Linux |
| [**Remote Desktop Manager Agent**](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/rdm-agent/) | The Remote Desktop Manager Agent can run commands on remote hosts, but what is really useful is that it can send commands to multiple hosts at the same time. Since Remote Desktop Manager uses a secure RDP channel to communicate with the Remote Desktop Manager Agent, it can only operate against Windows-based hosts. | Windows |
| [**Remote Desktop Manager Jump**](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/rdm-jump/) | Remote Desktop Manager Jump connects to a remote host, often called a Jump Box, Service Host, or a Bastion Server, which in turn connects to other hosts. Remote Desktop Manager Jump is actually an RDP in an RDP. | Windows |

It deploys rapidly, implements easily, and delivers the core features of a comprehensive PAM solution. Devolutions Server is designed to meet the ever-expanding security requirements of SMBs, while remaining very affordable. | Windows, Linux |
| [**Devolutions Hub**](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/overview/what-is-hub/) | Devolutions Hub Business is a secure and cloud-based password manager for teams. It empowers your organization to easily and securely vault and manage business-user passwords, along with other sensitive information, through a user-friendly web interface that can be quickly, easily and securely accessed via any browser. | Cloud |

Toutes les informations de comptes privilégiés sont transmises directement du coffre de mots de passe dans la session à distance via l'API sécurisée du Launcher, conformément aux dernières normes de sécurité. | Windows |

| [**Remote Desktop Manager Agent**](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/rdm-agent/) | Remote Desktop Manager Agent peut exécuter des commandes sur des hôtes distants, mais il est vraiment utile car il peut envoyer des commandes à plusieurs hôtes en même temps. Étant donné que Remote Desktop Manager utilise un canal RDP sécurisé pour communiquer avec Remote Desktop Manager Agent, il ne peut fonctionner que sur des hôtes sous Windows. | Windows |
| [**Remote Desktop Manager Jump**](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/rdm-jump/) | Remote Desktop Manager Jump se connecte à un hôte distant, souvent appelé serveur de rebond, hôte de service, ou serveur Bastion, qui à son tour se connecte à d'autres hôtes. Remote Desktop Manager Jump est en réalité un RDP dans un RDP. | Windows |

# Devolutions Agent - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Agent
=================

Devolutions Agent is a versatile background process used by many Devolutions products to perform various remote management tasks.

Devolutions Agent can only operate against Windows-based hosts.

### Installation

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#installation)

Download Devolutions Agent from [Devolutions’ website](https://devolutions.net/agent/)
, and install it on the remote computer. Devolutions Agent must be configured to automatically start when a Windows session is established. Consult the documentation of your operating system for details.

New users using this technology may wonder why a full installation of Remote Desktop Manager is required. There are three factors that make this a good solution:

*   Remote Desktop Manager on the remote host does not require a data source, it’s an empty shell.
    
*   The logging of the activity is brought back to your data source.
    
*   Every technology supported by Remote Desktop Manager can be used remotely.
    

### Usage

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#usage)

#### Running commands on multiple remote hosts

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#running-commands-on-multiple-remote-hosts)

Devolutions Agent can be used to run scripts from another Remote Desktop Manager installation. Since it uses an RDP channel for communication, it saves you from remote management headaches such as opening various ports in your firewall.

#### Executing commands on remote hosts using RDM MCP server

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#executing-commands-on-remote-hosts-using-rdm-mcp-server)

Devolutions Agent allows users with access to RDM MCP server to run commands on remote hosts via text-based prompts. Read [MCP server (experimental)](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/tools/more-tools/mcp-server/)
 to learn about RDM MCP server.

#### Leveraging Remote Desktop Manager's PEDM module

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#leveraging-remote-desktop-managers-pedm-module)

With Devolutions Agent, users can obtain elevated privileges for specific actions as defined in Remote Desktop Manager's PEDM module. To use this method, someone with administrator privileges must first configure a PEDM profile and assign it to one or more users. From then on, they should be able to select the profile in Devolutions Agent, and use the _**Run elevated**_ option when attempting to access resources requiring admin rights (right-click context menu). See [Privileged elevation and delegation management](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/concepts/privilege-elevation-delegation-management/)
 for more details.

#### Updating remote Devolutions Gateways via Devolutions Agent

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/devolutions-agent/#updating-remote-devolutions-gateways-via-devolutions-agent)

The [Devolutions Hub Services](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/pam-service/)
 must be configured on the Devolutions Hub to enable Devolutions Gateway updates with the Devolutions Agent.

Devolutions Agent enables administrators on Devolutions Server to remotely update Devolutions Gateway instances and farms, provided the Agent is installed on the systems hosting them (with the _**Devolutions Gateway Updater**_ feature checked during installation).

The updating process can be initiated in a few clicks by toggling the _**Bulk update**_ option in _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_, selecting the desired gateways and/or farms, and clicking on _**Update**_. The _**Update version**_ and _**Bulk update**_ windows allow for further customization of the process, including options to defer updates, specify versions, etc.

![Updating a Gateway and its farms on Devolutions Server using the Devolutions Agent](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4222_2025_2.png)

Updating a Gateway and its farms on Devolutions Server using the Devolutions Agent

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions PowerShell - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions PowerShell
======================

The [Devolutions.PowerShell module](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/Devolutions.PowerShell/)
 provides administrators with a suite of of cmdlets for managing Devolutions Gateway through PowerShell.

Learn more about [Devolutions PowerShell with Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/gateway-powershell)
.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Fermes Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Fermes Devolutions Gateway
==========================

Le but de la fonctionnalité des fermes Devolutions Gateway est de regrouper plusieurs passerelles sous une seule ferme pour équilibrer la charge des sessions passant par chaque passerelle. En utilisant cette fonctionnalité, les sessions seront réparties entre elles selon la configuration de la ferme :

*   La distribution de la charge aide à éviter de surcharger une passerelle particulière. Auparavant, pour une entrée donnée, une passerelle pouvait être configurée, mais toutes les connexions pour cette session passeraient par elle, ce qui pourrait potentiellement conduire à une saturation. Avec les fermes, il est maintenant possible de distribuer cette charge pour éviter la surcharge du service et maintenir la performance.
    
*   Haute disponibilité, ce qui signifie que la ferme aide à maintenir la disponibilité continue du service. Auparavant, si une passerelle devenait indisponible pour une raison quelconque, il n'était pas possible d'établir une session. Avec une ferme, si une passerelle est indisponible, la session sera automatiquement dirigée vers l'une des autres passerelles disponibles dans la ferme. Cela peut également être utile pour la maintenance ou les mises à jour, car une passerelle peut être temporairement mise hors ligne tandis qu'une autre active continue de fournir le service.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway farms configuration - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway farms configuration
=======================================

On this page

*   [Configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#configuration)
    *   [Moving a gateway into a farm](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#moving-a-gateway-into-a-farm)
        
    *   [Removing a farm/gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#removing-a-farmgateway)
        
*   [Load balancing](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#load-balancing)
    *   [Weight](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#weight)
        
    *   [Drain](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#drain)
        
    *   [After configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#after-configuration)
        

This topic will cover how to configure a Devolutions Gateway farm through the web interface for Devolutions Hub Business.

The [PAM service](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/pam-service/)
 must be installed for Devolutions Gateway farms to work properly.

Configuration
-------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#configuration)

1.  In the web interface for Devolutions Hub Business, make sure you are connected to the right data source.
    
2.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
3.  Click _**Add**_ and click _**Gateway farm**_.
    
    ![Gateway Farm](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB6000_2025_1.png)
    
    Gateway Farm
    
4.  In the _**General**_ tab, provide a name and description for the farm. You can also choose to set this farm as the default.
    
    Only one default setting is allowed at a time, whether it is a gateway or a farm. If a farm is created and set as default while another gateway is the default, the farm becomes the new default. The same applies if a default gateway is moved into a farm, the farm becomes the new default.
    
5.  In the _**Members**_ tab, click _**Select Farm Members**_ to open a dialogue for selecting the gateways to include in the farm.
    
    A gateway can belong to only one farm at a time. If it is included in a new farm, it will be moved from the current farm.
    
6.  In the _**Vaults**_ tab, select the vaults that are going to be a part of the farm.
    
7.  In the _**Groups**_ tab, select which groups to add to the farm.
    
8.  In the _**Users**_ tab, select which users to add to the farm.
    
9.  The _**Farm information**_ tab contains information about the farm ID.
    
10.  Click _**Add**_ to save the farm.
    

### Moving a gateway into a farm

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#moving-a-gateway-into-a-farm)

To move a gateway into a farm, there are two ways:

*   Use the selection dialogue during the initial configuration; or
    
*   Directly _**Edit**_ a gateway and choose the farm in the _**General**_ tab.
    

### Removing a farm/gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#removing-a-farmgateway)

To remove a farm, you can choose to delete the gateways within it or only delete the farm. If you delete only the farm, the gateways within it become independent gateways.

Load balancing
--------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#load-balancing)

### Weight

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#weight)

In the _**Members**_ tab of the farm's _**Edit**_ dialogue, gateways appear in a table with two editable values. The first value is their relative weight. This weight affects load distribution, higher weight increases the chances of a gateway receiving the next session. If all gateways within the farm have the same weight, they have an equal chance of receiving sessions.

#### Weight calculations example 1:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#weight-calculations-example-1)

Gateway1 weight = 100 Gateway2 weight = 200 Gateway3 weight = 300 Total weight = 600

Gateway1 probability = 100/600 = 16.66% Gateway2 probability = 200/600 = 33.33% Gateway3 probability = 300/600 = 50%

The actual weight values do not matter, only their ratios. So, 1-2-3 is equivalent to 1000-2000-3000.

#### Weight calculations example 2:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#weight-calculations-example-2)

Gateway1 weight = 1 Gateway2 weight = 2 (UNAVAILABLE) Gateway3 weight = 3 Total weight = 4

In this example, since Gateway2 is unavailable, it is not considered for session distribution.

Gateway1 probability = 25% Gateway3 probability = 75%

These are probabilities, not certainties. For example, with 4 sessions, Gateway1 might receive 2 or 3 sessions, despite the 25% probability. Over time, probabilities tend to balance out according to the law of large numbers.

### Drain

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#drain)

The _**Drain**_ button is in the column with the same name. Clicking it makes a gateway unavailable for new sessions. Active sessions continue until completion. It is useful for planned maintenance or updates.

### After configuration

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/farms/farm-configuration/#after-configuration)

Selecting a farm for a session is similar to choosing a regular gateway (under _**Properties**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_ in the Devolutions Hub Business web interface). Farms are listed along with individual gateways. A gateway within a farm cannot be selected outside the farm.

The _**Check Health**_ button is available for farms. A positive response means at least one gateway in the farm is available. A negative response means no gateways in the farm are available.

Go to _**Reports**_ – _**Activity logs**_ – _**Log entry**_ – _**Details**_ to see exactly which _**Gateway**_ and _**Gateway farm**_ were used for the session.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway farms - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway farms
=========================

The purpose of the Devolutions Gateway farms feature is to group multiple gateways under a single farm to balance the load of sessions passing through each gateway. By using this feature, sessions will be distributed among them according to the farm's configuration:

*   Load distribution helps to avoid overloading a particular gateway. Previously, for a given entry, a gateway could be configured, but all connections for that session would pass through it, potentially leading to saturation. With farms, it is now possible to distribute this load to prevent service overload and maintain performance.
    
*   High availability, meaning that the farm helps maintain continuous service availability. Previously, if a gateway became unavailable for any reason, it was not possible to establish a session. With a farm, if one gateway is unavailable, the session will automatically be directed to one of the other available gateways in the farm. This can also be useful for maintenance or updates, as a gateway can be temporarily taken offline while an active one continues to provide service.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway farms - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway farms
=========================

The purpose of the Devolutions Gateway farms feature is to group multiple gateways under a single farm to balance the load of sessions passing through each gateway. By using this feature, sessions will be distributed among them according to the farm's configuration:

*   Load distribution helps to avoid overloading a particular gateway. Previously, for a given entry, a gateway could be configured, but all connections for that session would pass through it, potentially leading to saturation. With farms, it is now possible to distribute this load to prevent service overload and maintain performance.
    
*   High availability, meaning that the farm helps maintain continuous service availability. Previously, if a gateway became unavailable for any reason, it was not possible to establish a session. With a farm, if one gateway is unavailable, the session will automatically be directed to one of the other available gateways in the farm. This can also be useful for maintenance or updates, as a gateway can be temporarily taken offline while an active one continues to provide service.

# Configuration de Devolutions Gateway avec Devolutions Hub Business - Documentation Devolutions

Configuration de Devolutions Gateway avec Devolutions Hub Business
==================================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Étapes pour installer manuellement](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)
    *   [Voir aussi](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)
        

Devolutions Gateway permettre connexions juste-à-temps au niveau de la session, éliminant le besoin de changer la configuration globale du système. Devolutions Gateway fournir une alternative flexible et sécurisée aux VPN, offrant une gestion de l'accès facile et une utilisation efficace des ressources du réseau.

Si vos clients ne parviennent pas à se connecter avec Devolutions Gateway, assurez-vous que le certificat contient toute la chaîne. Cette chaîne de certificats inclut tous les certificats intermédiaires. Par exemple : Autorité de Certification Racine – Autorité de Certification (Intermédiaire) Sécurisée – Certificat XYZ Acheté

De plus, pour [lancer une session RDP](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 avec Devolutions Gateway, seuls les navigateurs répondant à ces exigences minimales de version sont compatibles :

*   Chrome : 102
    
*   Firefox : 102
    
*   Safari : 16.4
    

Étapes pour installer manuellement
----------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)

Les instructions suivantes expliquent comment installer manuellement Devolutions Gateway via Devolutions Hub Business.

Étant donné que l'installateur est un fichier MSI, cette méthode ne fonctionne que sous Windows.

1.  Se connecter avec un compte Devolutions Hub Business administrateur.
    
2.  Créer une [identité d'application](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/hub/web-interface/administration/management/application-users/manage-application-users/)
    .
    
3.  Une fois l'identité de l'application créée, cliquer sur l'onglet _**Administration**_.
    
    ![Administration tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Administration tab
    
4.  Cliquer sur Devolutions Gateway, qui se trouve sous la section _**Gestion**_.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0006_2024_1.png)
    
5.  Cliquer sur le bouton _**Plus**_ en haut à droite.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0007_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
6.  Cliquer sur _**Télécharger la clé publique**_. Cette clé est unique au compte Devolutions Hub Business. Elle est automatiquement renommée en _provisioner.pem_. Garder une trace de l'endroit où vous avez sauvegardé cette clé, car elle sera nécessaire plus tard.
    
    ![Gateway public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0009_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway public key
    
7.  Sélectionner _**Télécharger MSI**_ dans la liste déroulante.
    
    ![Download MSI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0008_2024_1.png)
    
    Download MSI
    
8.  Exécuter l'installateur.
    
    L'installateur doit être exécuté sur le serveur hébergeant Devolutions Gateway.
    
9.  Cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Setup Wizard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0010_2024_1.png)
    
    Setup Wizard
    
10.  Une fois le chemin d'installation souhaité sélectionné, cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Destination Folder](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0011_2024_1.png)
    
    Destination Folder
    
11.  Cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Configure the Gateway installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0012_2024_1.png)
    
    Configure the Gateway installation
    
12.  Changer les _**Ports**_ à la valeur désirée et cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0013_2024_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
    Les ports par défaut pour HTTP(S) et TCP sont respectivement 7171 et 8181, mais peuvent être changés.
    
13.  Saisir l'URI d'accès de Devolutions Gateway et cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Access URI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0014_2024_1.png)
    
    Access URI
    
14.  Après avoir cliqué sur le bouton supérieur des points de suspension, sélectionner soit un fichier PFX soit un fichier de certificat, puis saisir le mot de passe correspondant. (Si l'écouteur est _**HTTP**_ cette étape est automatiquement sautée)
    
    ![Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0015_2024_1.png)
    
    Certificate
    
15.  Cliquer sur le bouton des points de suspension et sélectionner la _**Clé publique du provisionneur**_ qui a été générée à l'Étape 5.
    
    ![Public Key File](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0016_2024_1.png)
    
    Public Key File
    
16.  Cet écran montre un résumé des chemins/paramètres actuels. Il est possible de revenir en arrière et de les modifier. Si les paramètres sont corrects, cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Gateway setup summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0017_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway setup summary
    
17.  Cliquer sur _**Installer**_.
    
    ![Install button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0018_2024_1.png)
    
    Install button
    
18.  Cliquer sur _**Terminer**_ une fois que l'installation est terminée.
    
    ![Finish button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0019_2024_1.png)
    
    Finish button
    
19.  Retourner à la page _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_ dans Devolutions Hub Business.
    
20.  Entrer les informations correctes.
    
    ![Information fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0020_2024_1.png)
    
    Information fields
    
    Une fois l'URL Devolutions Gateway saisie, cliquer sur **_Détection automatique_** à côté de **_nom d'hôte TCP_** pour remplir la valeur automatiquement.
    
21.  En cochant la case _**Par défaut**_, ce Devolutions Gateway sera celui sélectionné si aucun n'est spécifié ou si _**Par défaut**_ est choisi lors de la connexion.
    
    ![Default option](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0021_2024_1.png)
    
    Default option
    
22.  Assurez-vous que le gateway est accessible en cliquant sur _**Tester la connexion**_.
    
    ![Test Connection button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0022_2024_1.png)
    
    Test Connection button
    
23.  Cliquer sur le bouton _**Ajouter**_ pour lier votre installation Devolutions Gateway à votre Devolutions Hub Business.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0023_2024_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
24.  Un rectangle affichera les informations pour chaque lien(s) Devolutions Gateway Hub.
    
    ![Successful link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0024_2024_1.png)
    
    Successful link
    
25.  Activer [l'enregistrement de la session](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/pam/hub/session-recording/)
    .
    

Visiter [configuration du Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/rdm-configuration/)
 pour en savoir plus sur le lien entre Remote Desktop Manager et Devolutions Gateway.

### Voir aussi

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Aperçu de Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Aperçu de Devolutions Gateway")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Configuration de l'ensemble de règles Gateway dans Devolutions Hub Business - Documentation Devolutions

Configuration de l'ensemble de règles Gateway dans Devolutions Hub Business
===========================================================================

Restreindre l'accès au réseau et segmenter le trafic sans créer une nouvelle instance de Gateway sur une autre machine à l'aide des règles du Gateway. Configurer les règles pour autoriser ou refuser les connexions par IPs, sous-réseaux, plages IP ou domaines. De plus, appliquer des règles de sécurité pour autoriser ou refuser l'accès à des utilisateurs ou groupes d'utilisateurs spécifiques ou au niveau du coffre. Suivre les étapes ci-dessous pour configurer rapidement un ensemble de règles Gateway dans Devolutions Hub Business :

1.  Naviguer vers _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_,
    
2.  Cliquer sur _**Ajouter**_ (_**+**_) et sélectionner _**Ensemble de règles Gateway**_.
    
3.  Sélectionner un _**Gateway physique**_ depuis la liste des Gateways dans votre Devolutions Hub Business.
    
4.  Saisir un _**Nom**_ pour l'ensemble de règles Gateway.
    
5.  Cliquer sur _**Sauvegarder**_.
    

![Configure a new Gateway ruleset](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4258_2026_1.png)

Configure a new Gateway ruleset

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Gateway ruleset configuration in Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Gateway ruleset configuration in Devolutions Hub Business
=========================================================

Restrict network access and segment traffic without creating a new Gateway instance on a different machine with the help of Gateway rulesets. Rules can be configured to allow or deny connections by IPs, subnets, IP ranges, or domains. What's more, security rules can be enforced to allow or deny access to specific users or user groups or at vault level. Follow the steps below to quickly set up a Gateway ruleset in Devolutions Hub Business:

1.  Navigate to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_,
    
2.  Click on _**Add**_ (_**+**_ ) and select _**Gateway ruleset**_.
    
3.  Select a _**Physical Gateway**_ from the list of Gateway in your Devolutions Hub Business.
    
4.  Enter a _**Name**_ for the Gateway ruleset.
    
5.  Cick on _**Save**_.
    

![Configure a new Gateway ruleset](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4258_2026_1.png)

Configure a new Gateway ruleset

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Gateway ruleset configuration in Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Gateway ruleset configuration in Devolutions Hub Business
=========================================================

Restrict network access and segment traffic without creating a new Gateway instance on a different machine with the help of Gateway rulesets. Rules can be configured to allow or deny connections by IPs, subnets, IP ranges, or domains. What's more, security rules can be enforced to allow or deny access to specific users or user groups or at vault level. Follow the steps below to quickly set up a Gateway ruleset in Devolutions Hub Business:

1.  Navigate to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_,
    
2.  Click on _**Add**_ (_**+**_ ) and select _**Gateway ruleset**_.
    
3.  Select a _**Physical Gateway**_ from the list of Gateway in your Devolutions Hub Business.
    
4.  Enter a _**Name**_ for the Gateway ruleset.
    
5.  Cick on _**Save**_.
    

![Configure a new Gateway ruleset](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4258_2026_1.png)

Configure a new Gateway ruleset

# Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Hub Business - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Hub Business
===============================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Steps for installing manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)
        

Devolutions Gateway allows for just-in-time connections at the session level, eliminating the need to change the system's global configuration. Devolutions Gateway provides a flexible and secure alternative to VPNs, offering easy access management and efficient use of network resources.

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure (Intermediate) Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate

Additionally, to [Launch an RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 with Devolutions Gateway only browsers that meet these minimal version requirements are compatible:

*   Chrome: 102
    
*   Firefox: 102
    
*   Safari: 16.4
    

Steps for installing manually
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#steps-for-installing-manually)

The following instructions explain how to manually install Devolutions Gateway through Devolutions Hub Business.

As the installer is an MSI file, this method only works on Windows.

1.  Log in with an administrator Devolutions Hub Business account.
    
2.  Create an [application identity](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/application-users/manage-application-users/)
    .
    
3.  Once the application identity has been created, click on the _**Administration**_ tab.
    
    ![Administration tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Administration tab
    
4.  Click on Devolutions Gateway, which is under the _**Management**_ section.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0006_2024_1.png)
    
5.  Click on the _**More**_ button in the top right.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0007_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
6.  Click on _**Download public key**_. This key is unique to the Devolutions Hub Business account. It is automatically renamed to _provisioner.pem_. Keep track of where you saved this key, as it will be needed later.
    
    ![Gateway public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0009_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway public key
    
7.  Select _**Download MSI**_ from the dropdown.
    
    ![Download MSI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0008_2024_1.png)
    
    Download MSI
    
8.  Execute the installer.
    
    The installer should be run on the server hosting Devolutions Gateway.
    
9.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Setup Wizard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0010_2024_1.png)
    
    Setup Wizard
    
10.  Once the desired installation path is selected, click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Destination Folder](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0011_2024_1.png)
    
    Destination Folder
    
11.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Configure the Gateway installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0012_2024_1.png)
    
    Configure the Gateway installation
    
12.  Change the _**Ports**_ to the desired value and click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0013_2024_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
    HTTP(S) and TCP default ports are 7171 and 8181, respectively, but can be changed.
    
13.  Input the Devolutions Gateway access URI and click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Access URI](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0014_2024_1.png)
    
    Access URI
    
14.  After clicking the top ellipsis button, select either a PFX file or a Certificate file, then enter the corresponding password. (If the listener is _**HTTP**_ this step is automatically skipped)
    
    ![Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0015_2024_1.png)
    
    Certificate
    
15.  Click on the ellipsis button and select the _**Provisioner Public Key**_ which was generated in Step 5.
    
    ![Public Key File](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0016_2024_1.png)
    
    Public Key File
    
16.  This screen shows a summary of the current paths/settings. It is possible to go _**Back**_ and modify them. If the settings are correct, click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Gateway setup summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0017_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway setup summary
    
17.  Click _**Install**_.
    
    ![Install button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0018_2024_1.png)
    
    Install button
    
18.  Click _**Finish**_ when the setup is complete.
    
    ![Finish button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0019_2024_1.png)
    
    Finish button
    
19.  Go back to the _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_ page in Devolutions Hub Business.
    
20.  Input the correct information.
    
    ![Information fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0020_2024_1.png)
    
    Information fields
    
    Once the Devolutions Gateway URL is entered, click on **_Auto-detect_** next to the **_TCP hostname_** to fill in the value automatically.
    
21.  By checking the _**Default**_ box, this Devolutions Gateway will be the one selected if none are specified or if _**Default**_ is chosen when connecting.
    
    ![Default option](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0021_2024_1.png)
    
    Default option
    
22.  Make certain the gateway can be reached by clicking _**Test Connection**_.
    
    ![Test Connection button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0022_2024_1.png)
    
    Test Connection button
    
23.  Click the _**Add**_ button to link your Devolutions Gateway installation to your Devolutions Hub Business.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0023_2024_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
24.  A rectangle will show the information for every Devolutions Gateway Hub link(s).
    
    ![Successful link](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/HUBB0024_2024_1.png)
    
    Successful link
    
25.  Enable [session recording](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/session-recording/)
    .
    

Visit [Remote Desktop Manager configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/rdm-configuration/)
 to learn more about linking Remote Desktop Manager and Devolutions Gateway.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")

# Configuration de Devolutions Gateway dans Remote Desktop Manager - Documentation Devolutions

Configuration de Devolutions Gateway dans Remote Desktop Manager
================================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Étapes](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/rdm-configuration/#steps)
    

Les instructions suivantes expliquent comment utiliser Devolutions Gateway dans une session RDP.

Étapes
------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/rdm-configuration/#steps)

1.  Sélectionner une session RDP et ouvrir son dialogue _**Propriétés**_.
    
2.  Aller à _**Connexion**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_ – _**Général**_.
    
3.  Dans la section _**Général**_, définir l'option _**Type**_ sur Devolutions Gateway.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_DGW0008.png)
    
4.  Dans la même section, définir l'option _**Connecter**_ sur _**Toujours connecter**_.
    
    ![Always Connect](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_DGW0009.png)
    
    Always Connect
    
5.  Dans l'onglet _**Paramètres (Devolutions Gateway)**_ sélectionner le gateway configuré dans [configuration de Devolutions Hub Business.](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/)
    
    ![Settings](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_DGW0007.png)
    
    Settings
    

Pour supprimer le délai de cinq secondes lors de l'ouverture d'une connexion, définir la valeur **_Délai_** sur 0 dans l'onglet **_Avancé_**.

6.  Une fois la session RDP connectée, l’entrée du journal suivante devrait être dans _**Rapports**_ – _**Sessions Gateway**_, qui se trouvent dans l'interface web de Devolutions Hub.
    
    ![Reports – Gateway Sessions](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_hub_DGW0052.png)
    
    Reports – Gateway Sessions
    
7.  Toutes vos sessions, journaux et configurations peuvent être gérés depuis le ruban de Remote Desktop Manager en allant dans _**Administration**_ _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
    ![Administration – Devolutions Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW6001_2025_1.png)
    
    Administration – Devolutions Gateway
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)
