# Devolutions Gateway configuration on Linux - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration on Linux
==========================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Install Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#install-devolutions-gateway)
    *   [Update Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)
        
*   [Install the PowerShell gateway module](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#install-the-powershell-gateway-module)
    
*   [Configure certificates](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#configure-certificates)
    *   [Generate a LetsEncrypt certificate on Ubuntu 22.04 LTS via Certbot](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#generate-a-letsencrypt-certificate-on-ubuntu-2204-lts-via-certbot)
        
    *   [Generate a self-signed certificate on Ubuntu 22.04 LTS via OpenSSL](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#generate-a-self-signed-certificate-on-ubuntu-2204-lts-via-openssl)
        
    *   [Trust the self-signed certificate on Ubuntu](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#trust-the-self-signed-certificate-on-ubuntu)
        
    *   [Trust the self-signed certificate on Windows](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#trust-the-self-signed-certificate-on-windows)
        
*   [Open Ubuntu firewall ports](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-ubuntu-firewall-ports)
    
*   [Modify the Devolutions Gateway configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#modify-the-devolutions-gateway-configuration)
    *   [Restart Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#restart-devolutions-gateway)
        
*   [Connect Devolutions Gateway to Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#connect-devolutions-gateway-to-devolutions-server)
    *   [Copy the Public Key from Devolutions Server to Devolutions Gateway Linux](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#copy-the-public-key-from-devolutions-server-to-devolutions-gateway-linux)
        
    *   [Configure Devolutions Gateway in Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#configure-devolutions-gateway-in-devolutions-server)
        
*   [Resolve hosts in Ubuntu](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#resolve-hosts-in-ubuntu)
    
*   [Open a web-based RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-a-web-based-rdp-session)
    
*   [Open a Remote Desktop Manager RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-a-remote-desktop-manager-rdp-session)
    

Installing and running Devolutions Gateway on Linux is quick and easy, provided that several prerequisites are met. Ubuntu 22.04 LTS was used to demonstrate the installation and configuration.

Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub Business is needed for the configuration as well as a Devolutions Gateway license.

Install Devolutions Gateway
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#install-devolutions-gateway)

1.  Navigate to the [Devolutions Gateway GitHub Release](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/releases/ "https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/releases/")
     page and download the **.deb** file of the latest release.
    
2.  Input the following using the command-line: `wget https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/releases/download/v2024.3.2/devolutions-gateway_2024.3.2.0_amd64.deb`
    
    ![Command-line wget](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0027_2024_3.png)
    
    Command-line wget
    
3.  Install the package using the `dpkg` utility: `sudo dpkg -i devolutions-gateway_2024.3.2.0_amd64.deb`
    
    ![Command-line dpkg](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0028_2024_3.png)
    
    Command-line dpkg
    

The configuration and binary packages are in the following locations:

*   **Configuration**: `/etc/devolutions-gateway`
    
*   **Binary**: `/usr/bin/devolutions-gateway`
    

### Update Devolutions Gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)

To update Devolutions Gateway on Linux download the latest package as explained in the previous section and run the installation command. The package will install over the existing installation and preserve configurations.

Install the PowerShell gateway module
-------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#install-the-powershell-gateway-module)

It is recommended to use the PowerShell gateway module to configure and manage the Devolutions Gateway instance on Linux.

1.  Install PowerShell with this command:
    
        source /etc/os-release
        wget -q https://packages.microsoft.com/config/ubuntu/$VERSION_ID/packages-microsoft-prod.deb
        sudo dpkg -i packages-microsoft-prod.deb
        rm packages-microsoft-prod.deb
        sudo apt-get update
        sudo apt-get install -y powershell
        
    
2.  Install the Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module:
    
        Install-Module -Name DevolutionsGateway
        Import-Module -Name DevolutionsGateway
        
    

Once installed the Devolutions Gateway configuration can be started, stopped, viewed or modified.

Configure certificates
----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#configure-certificates)

Proper trust of certificates between systems is key to making Devolutions Gateway work. Functionalities such as WebSockets used in web dashboard views of RDP, SSH, etc., require a properly trusted certificate. A certificate from an official authority such as Let's Encrypt would be ideal for most production systems. Self-signed certificates, such as the example shown below, may be generated but require additional configuration for trust. You may generate certificates on any system and use them within Devolutions Gateway if it adheres to the certificate requirements.

### Generate a LetsEncrypt certificate on Ubuntu 22.04 LTS via Certbot

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#generate-a-letsencrypt-certificate-on-ubuntu-2204-lts-via-certbot)

One option is to generate a LetsEncrypt certificate with the Certbot utility. To install the latest version, you may use the snap package manager. Depending on the Ubuntu distribution, the default APT repositories may not contain the latest version of the software. In this example, the domain verification is used with Cloudflare as the DNS provider.

1.  The example below demonstrates running Certbot installed and running as the root user, but Devolutions Gateway as a different user.
    
        sudo snap install certbot --classic
        sudo snap set certbot trust-plugin-with-root=ok
        sudo snap install certbot-dns-cloudflare
        
    
2.  When using Cloudflare, generate either a user or account-scoped API token, using the **Edit zone DNS** template. Once you have the API token, create the containing folder and corresponding `.ini` file to contain the API token.
    
        sudo install -d -m 0700 /root/.secrets
        sudo nano /root/.secrets/cloudflare.ini
        sudo chmod 0600 /root/.secrets/cloudflare.ini
        
    
3.  Request a certificate for your Devolutions Gateway domain using the Cloudflare DNS plugin. Replace the `gateway.mydomain.com` value below with your own domain.
    
        certbot certonly --dns-cloudflare --dns-cloudflare-credentials /root/.secrets/cloudflare.ini -d gateway.mydomain.com --cert-name gateway
        
    
4.  Modify your `gateway.json` configuration file to add the following lines and use the newly generated certificate, using the Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module. The commands below modify the `TlsCertificateFile`, `TlsPrivateKeyFile`, and `Listeners` configuration variables.
    
        Import-Module DevolutionsGateway
        Set-DGatewayConfig -TlsCertificateFile "/etc/letsencrypt/live/gateway/fullchain.pem" -TlsPrivateKeyFile "/etc/letsencrypt/live/gateway/privkey.pem" -Listeners @(
        @{
                "InternalUrl" = "tcp://*:8181"
                "ExternalUrl" = "tcp://*:8181"
            }
            @{
                "InternalUrl" = "https://*:7171"
                "ExternalUrl" = "https://*:7171"
            }
        )
        
    
5.  Before you can restart Devolutions Gateway to use the new certificate, you must allow the user running Devolutions Gateway to read the certificate files. This assumes your user is named **devolutions** and that the certificate is named **gateway**. You are giving traversal rights to the directories and read rights to the certificate files themselves.
    
        sudo setfacl -R -m u:devolutions:x /etc/letsencrypt/live
        sudo setfacl -R -m u:devolutions:x /etc/letsencrypt/live/gateway
        sudo setfacl -R -m u:devolutions:x /etc/letsencrypt/archive
        sudo setfacl -R -m u:devolutions:x /etc/letsencrypt/archive/gateway
        sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/live/gateway/fullchain.pem
        sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/live/gateway/privkey.pem
        sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/archive/gateway/fullchain*.pem
        sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/archive/gateway/privkey*.pem
        
        # Reconfigure to add a deploy hook
        sudo certbot reconfigure --cert-name gateway --deploy-hook "sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/archive/gateway/fullchain*.pem; sudo setfacl -m u:devolutions:r /etc/letsencrypt/archive/gateway/privkey*.pem; systemctl restart devolutions-gateway.service"
        
    
6.  Restart Devolutions Gateway using either the `systemctl` command or the Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module.
    
        # Restart Gateway using systemctl
        systemctl restart devolutions-gateway.service
        
    
        # Restart Gateway using the Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module, assuming it is run in a pwsh shell.
        Import-Module DevolutionsGateway; Restart-DGateway
        
    

#### Renew LetsEncrypt certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#renew-letsencrypt-certificate)

By default, with the Snap installation method, a systemd timer is used (instead of a cron job), which runs twice a day (though only renews a certificate within 30 days of its expiration). To force a renewal, you can use the command below.

    sudo certbot renew
    # To perform a renewal dry run and force a restart of the service, you can use the following command:
    # sudo certbot renew --dry-run --run-deploy-hooks
    

### Generate a self-signed certificate on Ubuntu 22.04 LTS via OpenSSL

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#generate-a-self-signed-certificate-on-ubuntu-2204-lts-via-openssl)

Using the OpenSSL utility, generate a certificate directly from the command line. The certificate then needs to be placed directly into the configuration directory **/etc/devolutions-gateway**.

![Command-line openssl](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0029_2024_3.png)

Command-line openssl

    sudo openssl req -x509 -subj "/C=CA/ST=Quebec/L=Lavaltrie/O=Devolutions/CN=ubuntu-2204" -addext "subjectAltName = IP:10.10.0.20" -addext "extendedKeyUsage = serverAuth" -nodes -days 365 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /etc/devolutions-gateway/server.key -out /etc/devolutions-gateway/server.crt
    

The certificate request will look different for every configuration.

Note that the certificate **must** include a **Subject Alternative Name (SAN)** extension with either a **DNS name** or an **IP address**, and it should also contain the **Extended Key Usage (EKU)** extension with the **Server Authentication** purpose (`serverAuth`). This is required because modern operating systems and browsers, including **Google Chrome** and **macOS,** will reject certificates that are missing a SAN or the appropriate EKU, even if the Common Name (CN) is set. It’s possible to relax this requirement by setting the `TlsVerifyStrict` option to `false` if necessary, but this is not recommended.

| Customization options | Explanation |
| --- | --- |
| `req` | Create and process certificate requests including self-signed certificates in PKCS#10 format. |
| `-x509` | Output a self-signed certificate. |
| `-subj` | Define the certificate subject on the command-line. There must be no spaces between sections<br><br>*   `/C` - Country in 2-digit code such as “CA” for Canada or “US” for United States.<br>    <br>*   `/ST` - State or Province, such as Quebec or California.<br>    <br>*   `/L` - Locality, such as Lavaltrie or Sacramento.<br>    <br>*   `/O` - Organization, such as Devolutions or Microsoft.<br>    <br>*   `/CN` \- Common name, here `ubuntu-2204` (as shown via the `hostname` command). |
| `-addext` | To add a Subject Alternate Name (SAN), you can use this parameter to define either an IP or DNS entry.<br><br>*   `"subjectAltName = IP:10.10.0.20"`<br>    <br>*   `"subjectAltName = DNS:ubuntu-2204"` |
| `-nodes` | Do not encrypt the created private key. |
| `-days` | The number of days the certificate is valid. |
| `-newkey` | Define the algorithm and bit size, here `rsa:2048` is used. |
| `-keyout` | The location to create the private key file. |
| `-out` | The location to create the public key file. |

### Trust the self-signed certificate on Ubuntu

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#trust-the-self-signed-certificate-on-ubuntu)

The TLS certificate has two purposes:

1.  Secures the management API;
    
2.  Secures any client-to-Gateway tunnel in which gateway can inspect or filter traffic (websites, Gateway Tunnel, SCP/SFTP, etc.).  
    For opaque protocols such as RDP or SSH, Devolutions Gateway simply forwards already-encrypted bytes, but the certificate is still required for gateway health checks and future features.
    

Once the self-signed certificate is created the certificate within the Ubuntu system will need to be trusted. To trust system-wide use the following set of commands:

    cd /etc/devolutions-gateway
    sudo apt-get install -y ca-certificates
    sudo cp server.crt /usr/local/share/ca-certificates
    sudo update-ca-certificates
    

![Command-line update-ca-certificates](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0030_2024_3.png)

Command-line update-ca-certificates

The `ca-certificates` may already be installed. By running the `update-ca-certificates` command a symlink will be created in `/etc/ssl/certs` to the copied certificate file in **/usr/local/share/ca-certificates**.

![Creating a symlink](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0031_2024_3.png)

Creating a symlink

If this is done in Firefox multiple trust errors will appear as the browser does not use the system-wide certificate store. Their [documentation](https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox "https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox")
 offers a few solutions to this.

### Trust the self-signed certificate on Windows

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#trust-the-self-signed-certificate-on-windows)

After the self-signed certificate is created it will need to be trusted on Devolutions Server. The **server.crt** and **server.key** files will need to be transferred to the Windows system; or copy and paste the contents into files (i.e. **sudo cat server.crt** in Ubuntu and copy that into a text file on Windows).

Skip this section if Devolutions Server is not running on Windows.

1.  Copy the public key to Windows (in the example, **C:\\Gateway** is a temporary location):  
    `sudo cat server.crt`
    
    ![Command-line sudo cat server](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0032_2024_3.png)
    
    Command-line sudo cat server
    
2.  Copy the content into a **server.crt** file.
    
    ![Server.crt file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0064_2024_3.png)
    
    Server.crt file
    
3.  Copy private key to Windows:  
    `sudo cat server.key`
    
    ![Copying the key to Windows](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0034_2024_3.png)
    
    Copying the key to Windows
    
4.  Copy the content into a **server.key** file.
    
    ![Server.key file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0065_2024_3.png)
    
    Server.key file
    
5.  Create a PFX file using the Windows certutil command-line tool. For this to work, the key file must be named the same as the **crt** file, only differing in extension:  
    `certutil -mergepfx server.crt server.pfx`
    
    ![Create a PFX file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0036_2024_3.png)
    
    Create a PFX file
    
6.  Import the PFX file into the [Trusted Root Certification Authorities Certificate Store](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-hardware/drivers/install/trusted-root-certification-authorities-certificate-store)
    .
    
    1.  Double-click the **server.pfx** file to start the import wizard and choose _**Local Machine**_.
        
    2.  Click _**Next**_ and accept the prompt.
        
        ![Click Next](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0037_2024_3.png)
        
        Click Next
        
    3.  Click _**Next**_.
        
        ![Click Next](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0038_2024_3.png)
        
        Click Next
        
    4.  Enter the password that you entered with the `certutil` command.
        
        *   Optionally: choose to _**Mark this key as exportable**_.
            
        
        ![Enter the password](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0039_2024_3.png)
        
        Enter the password
        
    5.  Choose the option _**Place all certificates in the following store**_.
        
    6.  Select _**Trusted Root Certification Authorities**_ with the _**Browse...**_ button.
        
    7.  Click _**Next**_.
        
        ![Click Next](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0040_2024_3.png)
        
        Click Next
        
    8.  Click _**Finish**_ to complete the import.
        

Open Ubuntu firewall ports
--------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-ubuntu-firewall-ports)

If the Linux system uses UFW (Uncomplicated Firewall) to manage iptable-based firewall, perform the following commands to open the necessary ports:

    sudo ufw status
    sudo ufw allow 7171
    sudo ufw allow 8181
    sudo ufw status
    

![Opening Ubuntu firewall ports](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0041_2024_3.png)

Opening Ubuntu firewall ports

Modify the Devolutions Gateway configuration
--------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#modify-the-devolutions-gateway-configuration)

The default configuration of a gateway contained in the **/etc/devolutions-gateway/gateway.json** file needs the certificate directives added (the `InternalUrl` will need to use HTTPS):

    {
      "Id": "YOUR-UNIQUE-GUID",
      "ProvisionerPublicKeyFile": "provisioner.pem",
      "ProvisionerPrivateKeyFile": null,
      "Listeners": [\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "tcp://:8181",\
          "ExternalUrl": "tcp://:8181"\
        },\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "http://:7171",\
          "ExternalUrl": "https://:7171"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

Modify the above file to reflect the following, assuming that both **server.crt** and **server.key** are in the same directory as **gateway.json** (using the built-in file editor Nano is recommended):

    {
      "Id": "YOUR-UNIQUE-GUID",
      "ProvisionerPublicKeyFile": "provisioner.pem",
      "ProvisionerPrivateKeyFile": null,
      "TlsCertificateFile": "server.crt",
      "TlsPrivateKeyFile": "server.key",
      "Listeners": [\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "tcp://:8181",\
          "ExternalUrl": "tcp://:8181"\
        },\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "https://:7171",\
          "ExternalUrl": "https://:7171"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

![Modifying the configuration](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0042_2024_3.png)

Modifying the configuration

### Restart Devolutions Gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#restart-devolutions-gateway)

With the new configuration in place restart Devolutions Gateway. This can be done with the `systemctl` command:

    sudo systemctl restart devolutions-gateway.service
    sudo systemctl status devolutions-gateway.service
    

![Restart the gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0046_2024_3.png)

Restart the gateway

Alternatively the `Stop-DGateway` and `Start-DGateway` PowerShell commands can also be used.

Connect Devolutions Gateway to Devolutions Server
-------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#connect-devolutions-gateway-to-devolutions-server)

### Copy the Public Key from Devolutions Server to Devolutions Gateway Linux

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#copy-the-public-key-from-devolutions-server-to-devolutions-gateway-linux)

1.  Log into the Devolutions Server web console and navigate to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
2.  Click the _**More**_ button and choose the _**Download public key**_ option.
    
    ![Download public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0049_2024_3.png)
    
    Download public key
    
3.  Copy the contents of the downloaded **gateway\_public\_key.pem** file on Windows.
    
    ![Copy the contents](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0066_2024_3.png)
    
    Copy the contents
    
4.  Replace the contents of the **/etc/devolutions-gateway/provisioner.pem** (the Nano utility is recommended) file with the copied contents from Windows.
    
    ![Replace the contents](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0045_2024_3.png)
    
    Replace the contents
    
5.  Restart Devolutions Gateway with the command `sudo systemctl restart devolutions-gateway.service`.
    
    ![Restart Devolutions Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0046_2024_3.png)
    
    Restart Devolutions Gateway
    

### Configure Devolutions Gateway in Devolutions Server

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#configure-devolutions-gateway-in-devolutions-server)

Go to the Devolutions Server web interface where the newly configured Linux Devolutions Gateway will be added.

Skip this section if you are installing Devolutions Gateway with Devolutions Hub Business.

1.  Log into the Devolutions Server web console and navigate to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
2.  Click the _**Add**_ (_**+**_) button.
    
3.  Select _**Gateway**_.
    
    ![Select Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0047_2024_3.png)
    
    Select Gateway
    
4.  Enter the following (this will change depending on the configuration).
    
    1.  _**Name**_: Linux Gateway
        
    2.  _**Devolutions Gateway URL:**_ `https://10.10.0.20:7171`
        
    3.  _**TCP Hostname:**_ `Ubuntu-2204`
        
5.  Click _**Save**_.
    
    ![Click Save](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0050_2024_3.png)
    
    Click Save
    

Click the _**More**_ options menu for the gateway and choose the _**Publish revocation list**_ option if the revocation list is out of date.

![Revocation list is not in sync](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0051_2024_3.png)

Revocation list is not in sync

![Publish revocation list](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0048_2024_3.png)

Publish revocation list

Resolve hosts in Ubuntu
-----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#resolve-hosts-in-ubuntu)

The Linux-hosted Devolutions Gateway system must be able to resolve the addresses that are requested by Devolutions Server. The simplest method for testing is to modify the hosts file.

Connect to the following system:

*   **Hostname**: `it-help-dc`
    
*   **Fully-Qualified Domain Name (FQDN)**: `it-help-dc.ad.it-help.ninja`
    
*   **IP Address**: `10.10.0.3`
    

Open the hosts file for editing `sudo nano /etc/hosts` to add the host in Ubuntu.

![Add the host in Ubuntu](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0052_2024_3.png)

Add the host in Ubuntu

Open a web-based RDP session
----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-a-web-based-rdp-session)

The gateway can now to connect to hosts. Since the `it-help-dc` host was added as resolvable to Ubuntu, it can be used to connect in a web-based session.

Web-based sessions require an active gateway configured for the entry and the user launching will require an assigned Remote Desktop Manager Team edition license or Devolutions Launcher license.  
  
Additionally, if changes have been made to license assignments, logging out and back in may be needed to see the option to launch the web-based connection.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web UI click on _**Add**_. Select an _**RDP**_ session entry.
    
2.  Click _**Continue**_.
    
    ![Click Continue](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0053_2024_3.png)
    
    Click Continue
    
3.  Enter a _**Name**_ and _**Host**_ which must be resolvable by the Linux Devolutions Gateway install.
    
4.  Click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Click Add](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0054_2024_3.png)
    
    Click Add
    
5.  Enter or link any necessary credentials to the RDP session and click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Enter or link credentials](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0055_2024_3.png)
    
    Enter or link credentials
    
6.  Under the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ tab choose Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type.
    
7.  Set the _**Connect**_ option to _**Always connect**_.
    
8.  Choose the correct gateway.
    
9.  Click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Choose the correct gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0056_2024_3.png)
    
    Choose the correct gateway
    
10.  Click _**Open in web client**_.
    
    ![Open in web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0069_2024_3.png)
    
    Open in web client
    

Open a Remote Desktop Manager RDP session
-----------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/linux-configuration/#open-a-remote-desktop-manager-rdp-session)

If the entry is already configured from within the Devolutions Server web interface it can be launched from Remote Desktop Manager when connected to the Devolutions Server data source.

Skip this section if you are installing Devolutions Gateway with Devolutions Hub Business.

When creating a new entry from Remote Desktop Manager the process is similar to that of Devolutions Server.

1.  In Remote Desktop Manager click on _**New entry**_. Select an RDP session entry.
    
2.  Click on _**Select**_.
    
    ![Click on Select](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0058_2024_3.png)
    
    Click on Select
    
3.  Enter a _**Name**_ and _**Host**_ which must be resolvable by the Linux Devolutions Gateway install.
    
4.  Enter or link any necessary credentials to the RDP session.
    
    ![Fill in the necessary fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0067_2024_3.png)
    
    Fill in the necessary fields
    
5.  Set the _**Connect**_ option to _**Always connect**_.
    
6.  Under the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ tab choose Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type.
    
    ![Adjust the General settings](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0068_2024_3.png)
    
    Adjust the General settings
    
7.  Go to the _**Settings (Devolutions Gateway)**_ sub-tab.
    
8.  Choose the desired Devolutions Gateway.
    
9.  Click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Click Add](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0061_2024_3.png)
    
    Click Add
    
10.  Click on the _**Open session**_ button.
    

By hovering over the title bar a tooltip will appear and show that the RDP is connected via Devolutions Gateway.

![Tooltip](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0062_2024_3.png)

Tooltip

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway farms - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway farms
=========================

The purpose of the Devolutions Gateway farms feature is to group multiple gateways under a single farm to balance the load of sessions passing through each gateway. By using this feature, sessions will be distributed among them according to the farm's configuration:

*   Load distribution helps to avoid overloading a particular gateway. Previously, for a given entry, a gateway could be configured, but all connections for that session would pass through it, potentially leading to saturation. With farms, it is now possible to distribute this load to prevent service overload and maintain performance.
    
*   High availability, meaning that the farm helps maintain continuous service availability. Previously, if a gateway became unavailable for any reason, it was not possible to establish a session. With a farm, if one gateway is unavailable, the session will automatically be directed to one of the other available gateways in the farm. This can also be useful for maintenance or updates, as a gateway can be temporarily taken offline while an active one continues to provide service.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Configuration de Devolutions Gateway dans Remote Desktop Manager - Documentation Devolutions

Configuration de Devolutions Gateway dans Remote Desktop Manager
================================================================

Les instructions suivantes expliquent comment utiliser Devolutions Gateway dans une session RDP.

1.  Sélectionner une session RDP et ouvrir son dialogue des _**Propriétés**_.
    
2.  Aller à _**Connexion**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_.
    
3.  Définir l'option _**Connecter**_ sur _**Toujours connecter**_.
    
4.  Définir l'option _**Type**_ sur Devolutions Gateway.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6033_2026_1.png)
    
5.  Dans l'onglet _**Paramètres (Devolutions Gateway)**_, sélectionner la passerelle configurée dans [configuration de Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
    .
    
    ![Select the gateway configured](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6037_2026_1.png)
    
    Select the gateway configured
    
    Pour supprimer le délai de cinq secondes lors de l'ouverture d'une connexion, définir la valeur de **_Délai_** à 0 dans l'onglet **_Avancé_**.
    
6.  Une fois la session RDP connectée, l'entrée de journal suivante devrait se trouver dans _**Rapports**_ – _**Journaux de la source de données**_, qui se trouvent dans l'interface web de Devolutions Server.
    
    ![Reports – Data Source Logs](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6007_2026_1.png)
    
    Reports – Data Source Logs
    
7.  Toutes vos sessions, journaux et configurations peuvent être gérées à partir du ruban Remote Desktop Manager en allant à _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
    ![Administration -](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW6001_2025_1.png)
    
    Administration -
    

### Enregistrement de session

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/rdm-configuration/#session-recording)

Un [enregistrement de session](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/kb/how-to-articles/session-recording/)
 fournit un enregistrement de ce qu'un utilisateur a fait lors d'une connexion à distance ouverte dans Remote Desktop Manager.

1.  Ouvrir les propriétés de votre entrée RDP.
    
2.  Aller à _**Enregistrement de session**_.
    
3.  Dans le menu déroulant _**Mode**_, sélectionner votre réglage préféré.
    
4.  Dans le menu déroulant _**Enregistrement**_, choisir _**Distant**_.
    
5.  Cliquer sur _**Sauvegarder**_.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway configuration in Remote Desktop Manager - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration in Remote Desktop Manager
===========================================================

The following instructions explain how to use Devolutions Gateway in an RDP session.

1.  Select an RDP session and open its _**Properties**_ dialog.
    
2.  Go to _**Connection**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_.
    
3.  Set the _**Connect**_ option to _**Always connect**_.
    
4.  Set the _**Type**_ option to Devolutions Gateway.
    
    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6033_2026_1.png)
    
5.  In the _**Settings (Devolutions Gateway)**_ tab select the gateway configured in [Devolutions Server configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
    .
    
    ![Select the gateway configured](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6037_2026_1.png)
    
    Select the gateway configured
    
    To remove the five-second delay when opening a connection, set the **_Delay_** value to 0 in the **_Advanced_** tab.
    
6.  Once the RDP session is connected, the following log entry should be in _**Reports**_ – _**Data Source Logs**_, which are located in the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
    ![Reports – Data Source Logs](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6007_2026_1.png)
    
    Reports – Data Source Logs
    
7.  All of your sessions, logs, and configurations can be managed from the Remote Desktop Manager ribbon by going to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
    ![Administration -](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW6001_2025_1.png)
    
    Administration -
    

### Session recording

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/rdm-configuration/#session-recording)

A [session recording](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/how-to-articles/session-recording/)
 provides a record of what a user did while a remote connection was opened in Remote Desktop Manager.

1.  Open the properties of your RDP entry.
    
2.  Go to _**Session recording**_.
    
3.  From the _**Mode**_ dropdown menu, select your preferred setting.
    
4.  In the _**Recording**_ dropdown menu, choose _**Remote**_.
    
5.  Click _**Save**_.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

    ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/RDMW6033_2026_1.png)

# Configuration de Devolutions Gateway avec Devolutions Server - Documentation Devolutions

Configuration de Devolutions Gateway avec Devolutions Server
============================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Différences entre l'installation côte à côte et l'installation standard (gérée)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)
    
*   [Installation côte à côte](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
    
*   [Installation standard (gérée)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
    
*   [Activer l'enregistrement Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)
    
*   [Installation MSI](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
    
*   [Mettre à jour Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)
    

Cette rubrique décrit comment configurer Devolutions Server pour se connecter avec Devolutions Gateway. Il existe trois manières d'installer un Devolutions Gateway : [_**Installation côte à côte**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
, [_**Installation standard (gérée)**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
 et [_**Installation MSI**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
.

Si vos clients ne parviennent pas à se connecter avec Devolutions Gateway, veiller à ce que le certificat contienne toute la chaîne. Cette chaîne de certificat comprend tous les certificats intermédiaires. Par exemple : Autorité de Certification Racine – Autorité de Certification Sécurisée – Certificat XYZ Acheté

Pour [Lancer une session RDP](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 avec Devolutions Gateway uniquement les navigateurs qui répondent à ces exigences de version minimale sont compatibles:

*   Chrome : 102
    
*   Firefox : 102
    
*   Safari : 16.4
    

Différences entre l'installation côte à côte et l'installation standard (gérée)
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)

L'installation _**Côte à côte**_ sera utilisée si vous devez installer Devolutions Gateway sur la même machine où Devolutions Server est hébergé. Il s'agit d'un processus d'installation simplifié qui configurera automatiquement le nouveau Devolutions Gateway avec les informations de l'instance Devolutions Server (URI d'accès et clé publique).

Pour installer Devolutions Gateway sur une autre machine que celle où Devolutions Server est hébergé, suivre le processus _**Installation standard (gérée)**_. La procédure est similaire, mais il faudra fournir plus d'informations sur votre instance Devolutions Server pour la compléter.

Installation côte à côte
------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)

Ce processus d'installation est le plus facile des deux et est la méthode recommandée pour les configurations réseau plus simples.

1.  Depuis la console Devolutions Server, cliquer sur l'onglet _**Compagnons**_.
    
    ![Companions tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp2083.png)
    
    Companions tab
    
2.  Dans la section Devolutions Gateway, cliquer sur _**Installer**_.
    
3.  Choisir _**Installation côte à côte**_.
    
    ![Side-by-side installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4047_2025_3.png)
    
    Side-by-side installation
    
    Il est possible de télécharger un fichier [.msi](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     pour installer Devolutions Gateway sur un Devolutions Server hors ligne.
    
4.  Si les valeurs par défaut ne fonctionnent pas pour votre environnement, entrer les paramètres souhaités.
    
    *   _**Écouteur HTTP**_ : Port HTTP(s) pour atteindre la Gateway. (7171 par défaut)
        
    *   _**Écouteur TCP**_: port utilisé pour les sessions RDP. (8181 par défaut)
        
5.  Cliquer sur _**OK**_.
    
    ![OK button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0003_2025_1.png)
    
    OK button
    
6.  Aller à l'interface web de Devolutions Server, se connecter avec un compte administrateur.
    
7.  Aller dans _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
8.  Cliquer sur le bouton _**Ping**_ pour la passerelle désirée dans la liste pour voir si une connexion peut être établie avec succès. Si la page était déjà ouverte, l'actualiser d'abord.
    
    ![Ping button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Ping button
    

Installation standard (gérée)
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)

La méthode _**Standard (gérée)**_ permet à Devolutions Gateway d'être installé sur un serveur différent de Devolutions Server. Cela peut être pour des raisons de performance ou pour accéder aux réseaux que Devolutions Server ne peut pas atteindre.

1.  Depuis la console Devolutions Server, cliquer sur l'onglet _**Compagnons**_.
    
2.  Dans la section Devolutions Gateway, cliquer sur _**Installer**_.
    
3.  Choisir _**Installation standard**_.
    
    ![Standard installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4046_2025_3.png)
    
    Standard installation
    
4.  Choisir entre _**Télécharger la version**_ et _**Installer depuis un fichier .msi**_.
    
    Il est possible de télécharger un fichier [_**.msi**_](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     pour installer Devolutions Gateway sur un Devolutions Server hors ligne.
    
5.  Cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Download version or Install from .msi file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0004_2025_1.png)
    
    Download version or Install from .msi file
    
6.  Entrer les informations de l'_**URI d'accès**_, par exemple https://gateway.example.com.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
7.  Choisir les ports _**d'Écouteurs**_ de Devolutions Gateway (par défaut ils sont 7171 et 8181). Devolutions Server utilisera le port URI d'accès (généralement 443 ou 7171) pour les vérifications et la configuration initiale. Remote Desktop Manager utilisera les ports 7171 et 8181 pour se connecter à la Gateway. Par exemple, une session Web utilisant la Gateway se connectera sur le port 7171, tout comme toute inscription via Devolutions Gateway. Le port 8181 est utilisé par des sessions telles que RDP.
    
    *   Si HTTPS est choisi au lieu de HTTP à l'étape précédente, la _**Configuration du certificat**_ sera nécessaire.
        
    *   _**Fichier de certificat**_ : Doit être un certificat de chaîne complète (.pfx, .p12, .pem, .crt).
        
    *   _**Mot de passe du certificat**_: Nécessaire uniquement si un certificat .pfx ou .p12 a été utilisé.
        
    *   _**Fichier de clé privée**_ : Nécessaire seulement si un .pem ou .crt a été utilisé comme certificat.
        
    
    Ne pas partager la clé privée avec d'autres utilisateurs, car elle peut être utilisée pour déchiffrer la communication entre un utilisateur et Devolutions Gateway. Seule la clé publique doit être partagée.
    
8.  Cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
9.  Choisir entre :
    
    *   _**Utiliser la clé publique de l'instance Devolutions Server 'Devolutions Server'**_ : cette option est utilisée si Devolutions Gateway est installé sur le même serveur que le Devolutions Server ;
        
    *   _**Depuis un fichier**_ : Si l'installation de Devolutions Gateway est sur un autre ordinateur, télécharger la clé publique depuis le Devolutions Server avec lequel vouloir jumeler cette Devolutions Gateway. Elle se trouve sous _**Administration – Devolutions Gateway**_.
        
    
    ![Download public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0007_2025_1.png)
    
    Download public key
    
10.  Cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
    ![Key pair configuration](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0011.png)
    
    Key pair configuration
    
    Si Devolutions Server n'est pas installé localement, alors cocher l'option _**Depuis le fichier**_ et sélectionner le fichier de configuration `.json` de Devolutions Gateway. Voir [Configuration du magasin de certificats Windows via gateway.json](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)
     pour un fichier de configuration typique.
    
    [Le dépôt GitHub de Devolutions](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/?tab=readme-ov-file#configuration)
     contient également une liste des chemins typiques pour le fichier, ainsi que toutes les options stables disponibles pour le personnaliser.
    
11.  Cliquer sur _**Installer**_.
    
    ![Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0012.png)
    
    Summary
    
12.  Cliquer sur _**Fermer**_.
    
    ![Installation Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0013.png)
    
    Installation Summary
    
13.  Sur l'interface web de Devolutions Server, se connecter avec un compte administrateur.
    
14.  Aller dans _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
15.  Cliquer sur le bouton _**Ajouter**_ en haut à droite.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0006_2025_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
16.  Entrer les informations suivantes.
    
    *   _**Nom**_: Nom de la passerelle qui sera affiché dans Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**Description**_: Description de la passerelle.
        
    *   _**Définir par défaut**_ : Si activé, cette passerelle sera sélectionnée par défaut lors de la configuration de Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**URL Devolutions Gateway**_: L'URL et le Port du Devolutions Gateway auxquels Devolutions Server se connectera, par exemple : **https://gateway.example.com:7171**.
        
    *   _**Port d'écoute TCP**_: Définir le port avec le même numéro de port TCP configuré dans la console Devolutions Server.
        
    *   _**Nom d'hôte TCP**_: Il doit être résoluble par la machine initiant la connexion (Remote Desktop Manager).
        
17.  Cliquer sur _**Sauvegarder**_.
    

![Gateway information](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0008_2025_1.png)

Gateway information

La passerelle devrait maintenant être visible dans la liste. Il est possible de vérifier l'état de la passerelle avec le bouton _**Ping**_.

![Ping](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)

Ping

18.  Publier _**la configuration Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
19.  Publier _**la liste de révocation**_. ![Publish the Gateway configuration and the Revocation list](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6066_2025_3.png)
    

Activer l'enregistrement Gateway
--------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)

Cliquer [ici](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/kb/how-to-articles/configure-recording-server/)
 pour savoir comment activer l'enregistrement Devolutions Gateway dans Devolutions Server.

Installation MSI
----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)

Il est possible de faire une installation silencieuse automatisée qui installera une passerelle avec la configuration par défaut. C'est la manière recommandée de la configurer à travers le [module Devolutions.PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/devolutions-ecosystem/powershell/)
. Utiliser la commande suivante:

    msiexec.exe /i DevolutionsGateway-x86_64-VERSION.msi /quiet /norestart /log gateway_install.log
    

Mettre à jour Devolutions Gateway
---------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)

Devolutions Gateway peut être mis à jour de trois manières différentes selon vos besoins:

*   Transmettre les mises à jour via l'interface web de Devolutions Server, dans _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_. En utilisant cette méthode, les instances peuvent être mises à jour individuellement ou en masse. Cette dernière peut être effectuée rapidement en activant l'option _**Mise à jour en masse**_, en sélectionnant les passerelles, et en cliquant sur _**Mettre à jour**_. Noter que [Devolutions Agent](https://devolutions.net/agent/)
     est requis pour mettre à jour depuis l'interface web de Devolutions Server.
    
*   Mettre à jour manuellement via la console Devolutions Server. Pour le faire, aller sur l'onglet _**Compagnons**_, sélectionner Devolutions Gateway à mettre à jour, cliquer sur le bouton _**Mettre à jour**_, et suivre les instructions alors fournies.
    
*   Exécuter le [script PowerShell de mise à jour automatique](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/powershell/gateway-powershell/powershell-updater/)
    . Cela peut être enregistré comme une tâche planifiée pour vérifier périodiquement les mises à jour.
    

#### Voir aussi

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")

# Clear a browser's local storage - Devolutions Documentation

Clear a browser's local storage
===============================

Follow the steps to clear your browser's local storage.

1.  Open a Google Chrome browser page.
    
2.  Use your keyboard's F12 key to open the Google Chrome Developer Tools Console.
    
    ![Google Chrome Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4759.png)
    
    Google Chrome Developer Tools Console
    
3.  Click _**Application**_ in the console's top menu.
    
    ![Console – Application](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4760.png)
    
    Console – Application
    
4.  Expand the _**Local storage**_ list located under the _**Storage**_ section in the console's left menu.
    
    ![Console – Application – Local storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4761.png)
    
    Console – Application – Local storage
    
5.  Right-click your site(s) and click _**Clear**_ to delete the local storage.
    
    ![Local storage – Clear](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4762.png)
    
    Local storage – Clear
    

1.  Open a Microsoft Edge browser page.
    
2.  Use your keyboard's F12 key to open the Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console.
    
    ![Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4869.png)
    
    Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console
    
3.  Click _**Application**_ in the console's top menu.
    
    ![Console – Application](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4870.png)
    
    Console – Application
    
4.  Expand the _**Local Storage**_ list located in the _**Storage**_ section of the console's left menu.
    
    ![Console – Application – Local storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4871.png)
    
    Console – Application – Local storage
    
5.  Right-click your site(s) and click _**Clear**_ to delete the local storage.
    
    ![Local storage – Clear](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4872.png)
    
    Local storage – Clear

    ![Firefox Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4865.png)
    
    Firefox Developer Tools Console

    ![Console – Storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4866.png)
    
    Console – Storage

    ![Console – Storage – Local Storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4867.png)
    
    Console – Storage – Local Storage

    ![Local Storage – Delete All](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4868.png)
    
    Local Storage – Delete All

# Devolutions Gateway with Devolutions Server - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway with Devolutions Server
===========================================

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway farms configuration - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway farms configuration
=======================================

On this page

*   [Configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#configuration)
    *   [Moving a gateway into a farm](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#moving-a-gateway-into-a-farm)
        
    *   [Removing a farm/gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#removing-a-farmgateway)
        
*   [Load balancing](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#load-balancing)
    *   [Weight](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#weight)
        
    *   [Drain](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#drain)
        
    *   [After configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#after-configuration)
        

This topic will cover how to configure a Devolutions Gateway farm through the web interface for Devolutions Server.

Configuration
-------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#configuration)

1.  In the web interface for Devolutions Server, make sure you are connected to the right data source.
    
2.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Modules**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
3.  Click _**Add**_ and click _**Gateway Farm**_.
    
    ![Gateway Farm](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0032.png)
    
    Gateway Farm
    
4.  In the _**General**_ tab, provide a name and description for the farm. You can also choose to set this farm as the default.
    
    Only one default setting is allowed at a time, whether it is a gateway or a farm. If a farm is created and set as default while another gateway is the default, the farm becomes the new default. The same applies if a default gateway is moved into a farm, the farm becomes the new default.
    
5.  In the _**Members**_ tab, click _**Select Farm Members**_ to open a dialogue for selecting the gateways to include in the farm.
    
    A gateway can belong to only one farm at a time. If it is included in a new farm, it will be moved from the current farm.
    
6.  In the _**Security**_ tab, configure who can use the farm and in which vault it can be used. Permissions and rights are the same as those for a regular gateway.
    
    If gateways within the farm have specific restrictions or permissions, they will be overridden by the farm's settings. A warning message in the **_Security_** tab of a gateway within a farm informs the user that modifying restrictions/permissions here will not have an impact as long as it remains in the farm.
    

### Moving a gateway into a farm

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#moving-a-gateway-into-a-farm)

To move a gateway into a farm, there are two ways:

*   Use the selection dialogue during the initial configuration; or
    
*   Directly _**Edit**_ a gateway and choose the farm in the _**General**_ tab.
    

### Removing a farm/gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#removing-a-farmgateway)

To remove a farm, you can choose to delete the gateways within it or only delete the farm. If you delete only the farm, the gateways within it become independent gateways.

Load balancing
--------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#load-balancing)

### Weight

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#weight)

In the _**Members**_ tab of the farm's _**Edit**_ dialogue, gateways appear in a table with two editable values. The first value is their relative weight. This weight affects load distribution, higher weight increases the chances of a gateway receiving the next session. If all gateways within the farm have the same weight, they have an equal chance of receiving sessions.

#### Weight calculations example 1:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#weight-calculations-example-1)

Gateway1 weight = 100 Gateway2 weight = 200 Gateway3 weight = 300 Total weight = 600

Gateway1 probability = 100/600 = 16.66% Gateway2 probability = 200/600 = 33.33% Gateway3 probability = 300/600 = 50%

The actual weight values do not matter, only their ratios. So, 1-2-3 is equivalent to 1000-2000-3000.

#### Weight calculations example 2:

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#weight-calculations-example-2)

Gateway1 weight = 1 Gateway2 weight = 2 (UNAVAILABLE) Gateway3 weight = 3 Total weight = 4

In this example, since Gateway2 is unavailable, it is not considered for session distribution.

Gateway1 probability = 25% Gateway3 probability = 75%

These are probabilities, not certainties. For example, with 4 sessions, Gateway1 might receive 2 or 3 sessions, despite the 25% probability. Over time, probabilities tend to balance out according to the law of large numbers.

### Drain

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#drain)

The _**Drain**_ button is in the column with the same name. Clicking it makes a gateway unavailable for new sessions. Active sessions continue until completion. It is useful for planned maintenance or updates.

### After configuration

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/farm/farm-configuration/#after-configuration)

Selecting a farm for a session is similar to choosing a regular gateway (under _**Properties**_ – _**VPN/SSH/Gateway**_ in the Devolutions Server web interface). Farms are listed along with individual gateways. A gateway within a farm cannot be selected outside the farm.

The _**Check Health**_ button is available for farms. A positive response means at least one gateway in the farm is available. A negative response means no gateways in the farm are available.

Go to _**Reports**_ – _**Activity Logs**_ – _**Log Entry**_ – _**Details**_ to see exactly which _**Gateway**_ and _**Gateway Farm**_ were used for the session.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Récupération du compte Devolutions - Documentation Devolutions

Récupération du compte Devolutions
==================================

Les utilisateurs qui ont perdu l'accès à leur compte Devolutions peuvent les récupérer rapidement en suivant la procédure de récupération décrite ci-dessous :

1.  Ouvrir un navigateur Web et se diriger vers le [site Web Devolutions Portal](https://portal.devolutions.com/)
    .
    
2.  Entrer votre _**Nom d'utilisateur**_ et cliquer sur l'option _**Mot de passe oublié**_ pour réinitialiser votre mot de passe. Cela envoie automatiquement un code de vérification à votre adresse courriel.
    
3.  De retour sur l'écran de connexion du Devolutions Portal, entrer le code qui vous a été fourni et choisir une méthode pour récupérer votre clé privée. Si vous n'en avez configuré aucune, cliquer sur _**Je n'ai aucun de ceux-ci**_.
    
    S'assurer d’avoir votre [kit de récupération](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/hub/kb/how-to-articles/emergency-kit-business/#emergency-kit-reset)
     à portée de main si vous êtes le propriétaire des sources de données Devolutions Hub Business. Le kit de récupération est généré lors de la création du hub. Sans lui, perdre l’accès indéfiniment.
    
4.  Choisir un nouveau _**Mot de passe**_ pour votre compte Devolutions. Une fois le mot de passe modifié, se connecter au Devolutions Portal et se rendre à la section _**Connexion & Sécurité**_.
    
5.  Configurer un nouvel ensemble de clés de récupération. L'authentification à deux facteurs est fortement recommandée comme méthode pour récupérer les clés privées (_**Authentification à deux facteurs**_, _**Récupération de compte**_, et _**Codes de récupération**)._
    
6.  Si cette récupération concernait un utilisateur du Devolutions Hub, il peut être réinvité dans le hub et son coffre utilisateur restauré.
    

#### Voir aussi

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-account-recovery/#see-also)

*   [Academie Devolutions – Récupérer votre compte Devolutions](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/activity/2930847-recover-your-devolutions-account)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway configuration  with Devolutions Server - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Server
=========================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Differences between Side-by-side and Standard (managed) installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)
    
*   [Side-by-side installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
    
*   [Standard (managed) installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
    
*   [Enable Gateway recording](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)
    
*   [MSI installation](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
    
*   [Update Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)
    

This topic describes how to configure Devolutions Server to connect with Devolutions Gateway. There are three ways to install a Devolutions Gateway: the [_**Side-by-side installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)
, the [_**Standard (managed) installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)
 and the [_**MSI installation**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)
.

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate

Additionally, to [Launch an RDP session](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
 with Devolutions Gateway only browsers that meet these minimal version requirements are compatible:

*   Chrome: 102
    
*   Firefox: 102
    
*   Safari: 16.4
    

Differences between Side-by-side and Standard (managed) installation
--------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#differences-between-side-by-side-and-standard-managed-installation)

The _**Side-by-side installation**_ will be used if you need to install Devolutions Gateway on the same machine where Devolutions Server is hosted. It is a simplified installation process that will automatically configure the new Devolutions Gateway with information from the Devolutions Server instance (access URI and public key).

To install Devolutions Gateway on another machine than the one where Devolutions Server is hosted, you need to follow the _**Standard (managed) installation**_ process. The procedure is similar, but you will need to provide more information about your Devolutions Server instance to complete it.

Side-by-side installation
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#side-by-side-installation)

This installation process is the easier of the two and is the recommended method for simpler network layouts.

1.  From the Devolutions Server Console, click on the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
    ![Companions tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp2083.png)
    
    Companions tab
    
2.  In the Devolutions Gateway section, click on _**Install**_.
    
3.  Choose _**Side-by-side installation**_.
    
    ![Side-by-side installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4047_2025_3.png)
    
    Side-by-side installation
    
    It is possible to download an [.msi](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     file to install Devolutions Gateway on an offline Devolutions Server.
    
4.  If default values do not work for your environment, enter the desired settings.
    
    *   _**HTTP Listener**_: HTTP(s) port to reach the Gateway. (7171 is default)
        
    *   _**TCP Listener**_: port used for the RDP sessions. (8181 is default)
        
5.  Click _**OK**_.
    
    ![OK button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0003_2025_1.png)
    
    OK button
    
6.  Go to the Devolutions Server web interface, connect with an administrator account.
    
7.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
8.  Click on the _**Ping**_ button for the desired gateway in the list to see if a connection can successfully be made. If the page was already open, refresh it first.
    
    ![Ping button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Ping button
    

Standard (managed) installation
-------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#standard-installation)

The _**Standard (managed)**_ method allows Devolutions Gateway to be installed on a separate server than Devolutions Server. It could be for performance purposes or access networks that Devolutions Server cannot access.

1.  From the Devolutions Server Console, click on the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
2.  In the Devolutions Gateway section, click on _**Install**_.
    
3.  Choose _**Standard installation**_.
    
    ![Standard installation](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4046_2025_3.png)
    
    Standard installation
    
4.  Choose between _**Download version**_ and _**Install from .msi file**_.
    
    It is possible to download an [_**.msi**_](https://devolutions.net/gateway/download/)
     file to install Devolutions Gateway on an offline Devolutions Server.
    
5.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Download version or Install from .msi file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0004_2025_1.png)
    
    Download version or Install from .msi file
    
6.  Enter the _**Access URI**_ information, for example https://gateway.example.com.
    
    ![Listeners](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE0005_2025_1.png)
    
    Listeners
    
7.  Choose the Devolutions Gateway _**Listeners**_ ports (by default they are 7171 and 8181). Devolutions Server will use the Access URI port (usually 443 or 7171) for health checks and initial configuration. Remote Desktop Manager will use ports 7171 and 8181 to connect to the Gateway. For instance, a web session using the Gateway will connect on port 7171, as will any registration via Devolutions Gateway. Port 8181 is used by sessions such as RDP.
    
    *   If HTTPS is chosen instead of HTTP in the step above, the _**Certificate configuration**_ will be needed.
        
    *   _**Certificate file**_: Needs to be a full chain certificate (.pfx, .p12, .pem, .crt).
        
    *   _**Certificate password**_: Only needed if a .pfx or .p12 certificate was used.
        
    *   _**Private key file**_: Only needed if a .pem or .crt was used as a certificate.
        
    
    Do not share the private key with other users, as it can be used to decrypt the communication between a user and Devolutions Gateway. Only the public key should be shared.
    
8.  Click _**Next**_.
    
9.  Choose between:
    
    *   _**Use public key from Devolutions Server instance 'Devolutions Server'**_: this option is used if the installed Devolutions Gateway is on the same server as the Devolutions Server;
        
    *   _**From file**_: If installing Devolutions Gateway on another computer, download the public key from the Devolutions Server you want to pair with that Devolutions Gateway. It is located under _**Administration – Devolutions Gateway**_.
        
    
    ![Download public key](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0007_2025_1.png)
    
    Download public key
    
10.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Key pair configuration](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0011.png)
    
    Key pair configuration
    
    If Devolutions Server is not installed locally, then check the _**From file**_ option, and select Devolutions Gateway's `.json` configuration file .See [Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)
     for a typical configuration file.
    
    [Devolutions' GitHub repository](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway/?tab=readme-ov-file#configuration)
     also contains a list of the typical paths for the file, as well as all the stable options available to customize it.
    
11.  Click _**Install**_.
    
    ![Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0012.png)
    
    Summary
    
12.  Click _**Close**_.
    
    ![Installation Summary](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_server_ServerOp0013.png)
    
    Installation Summary
    
13.  On the Devolutions Server web interface, connect with an administrator account.
    
14.  Go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
15.  Click on the _**Add**_ button on the top right corner.
    
    ![Add button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0006_2025_1.png)
    
    Add button
    
16.  Enter the following information.
    
    *   _**Name**_: Name of the gateway that will be displayed in Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**Description**_: Description of the gateway.
        
    *   _**Set as default**_: If enabled, this gateway will be selected by default when configuring Remote Desktop Manager.
        
    *   _**Devolutions Gateway URL**_: The Devolutions Gateway URL and Port that Devolutions Server will connect to, for example: **https://gateway.example.com:7171**.
        
    *   _**TCP Listening Port**_: Set the port with the same TCP port value configured in the Devolutions Server Console.
        
    *   _**TCP hostname**_: It should be resolvable by the machine initiating the connection (Remote Desktop Manager).
        
17.  Click _**Save**_.
    

![Gateway information](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0008_2025_1.png)

Gateway information

The gateway should now be visible in the list. It is possible to verify the status of the gateway with the _**Ping**_ button.

![Ping](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS0005_2025_1.png)

Ping

18.  Publish the _**Devolutions Gateway configuration**_.
    
19.  Publish the _**Revocation list**_. ![Publish the Gateway configuration and the Revocation list](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6066_2025_3.png)
    

Enable Gateway recording
------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#enable-gateway-recording)

Click [here](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/kb/how-to-articles/configure-recording-server/)
 to learn how to enable Devolutions Gateway recording in Devolutions Server.

MSI installation
----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#msi-installation)

It is possible to do an automated silent installation which will install a gateway with the default configuration. This is the recommended way to configure it through the [Devolutions.PowerShell module](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/devolutions-ecosystem/powershell/)
. Use the following command:

    msiexec.exe /i DevolutionsGateway-x86_64-VERSION.msi /quiet /norestart /log gateway_install.log
    

Update Devolutions Gateway
--------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#update-devolutions-gateway)

Devolutions Gateway can be updated in three different ways depending on your needs:

*   Push updates via Devolutions Server web interface, in _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_. Using this method, instances can be updated singly or in bulk. The latter can be done quickly by toggling the _**Bulk update**_ option, selecting the gateways, and clicking on _**Update**_. Note that [Devolutions Agent](https://devolutions.net/agent/)
     is required to update from the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
*   Update manually through the Devolutions Server Console. To do so, head over the _**Companions**_ tab, select the Devolutions Gateway to update, click the _**Update**_ button, and follow the instructions then provided.
    
*   Run the [auto-updater PowerShell script](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/gateway-powershell/powershell-updater/)
    . This can be registered as a scheduled task to periodically check for updates.
    

#### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy - Overview of Devolutions Gateway](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/path/2007290/activity/3070847 "Devolutions Academy - Overview of the Devolutions Gateway")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Account recovery - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Account recovery
============================

Users who have lost access to their Devolutions Account can recover them quickly by following the recovery procedure described below:

1.  Open a web browser and navigate to the [Devolutions Portal website](https://portal.devolutions.com/)
    .
    
2.  Enter your _**Username**_ and click on the _**Forgot my password**_ option to reset your password. This automatically sends a verification code to your email address.
    
3.  Back on the Devolutions Portal login screen, enter the code provided to you and select a method to retrieve your private key. If you have not configured any, click on _**I have none of these**_.
    
    Make sure you have your [recovery kit](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/kb/how-to-articles/emergency-kit-business/#emergency-kit-reset)
     on hand if you are the owner of Devolutions Hub Business data sources. The recovery kit is generated during the hub's creation. Without it, you will lose access indefinitely.
    
4.  Choose a new _**Password**_ for your Devolutions Account. Once the password has been changed, log in to Devolutions Portal and head over to the _**Sign-In & Security**_ section.
    
5.  Configure a new set of recovery keys. Two-step verification is highly recommended as a method of recovering private keys (_**Two-step verification**_, _**Account recovery**_, and _**Recovery codes**)._
    
6.  If this recovery was for a Devolutions Hub user, he can safely be reinvited to the hub and his user vault restored.
    

#### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-account-recovery/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Academy – Recover your Devolutions Account](https://academy.devolutions.net/student/activity/2930847-recover-your-devolutions-account)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# La page de connexion Devolutions ne s'ouvre pas dans le navigateur - Documentation Devolutions

La page de connexion Devolutions ne s'ouvre pas dans le navigateur
==================================================================

Lors de la tentative de connexion à un produit Devolutions tel que Devolutions Hub ou Devolutions Server, une page de connexion devrait s'ouvrir dans votre navigateur pour vous permettre d'entrer vos informations d'identification. Cette fenêtre peut parfois être bloquée par votre navigateur ou une extension installée dessus. Dans ce cas, aucun message d'erreur n'est affiché dans le produit Devolutions puisque le problème provient du navigateur.

### Solution

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-login-page-does-not-open-browser/#solution)

D'abord, modifier les paramètres de votre navigateur ou de l'extension de navigateur pour supprimer ou désactiver le paramètre qui a bloqué la fenêtre d'invite d'identification. Essayer de se connecter à nouveau.

Si cela ne fonctionne pas, désactiver ou supprimer l'extension qui cause le problème ou changer de navigateur. Essayer de se connecter à nouveau.

Si vous rencontrez toujours des problèmes, [contactez notre équipe de support client](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---
