# Clear a browser's local storage - Devolutions Documentation

Clear a browser's local storage
===============================

Follow the steps to clear your browser's local storage.

1.  Open a Google Chrome browser page.
    
2.  Use your keyboard's F12 key to open the Google Chrome Developer Tools Console.
    
    ![Google Chrome Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4759.png)
    
    Google Chrome Developer Tools Console
    
3.  Click _**Application**_ in the console's top menu.
    
    ![Console – Application](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4760.png)
    
    Console – Application
    
4.  Expand the _**Local storage**_ list located under the _**Storage**_ section in the console's left menu.
    
    ![Console – Application – Local storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4761.png)
    
    Console – Application – Local storage
    
5.  Right-click your site(s) and click _**Clear**_ to delete the local storage.
    
    ![Local storage – Clear](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4762.png)
    
    Local storage – Clear
    

1.  Open a Microsoft Edge browser page.
    
2.  Use your keyboard's F12 key to open the Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console.
    
    ![Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4869.png)
    
    Microsoft Edge Developer Tools Console
    
3.  Click _**Application**_ in the console's top menu.
    
    ![Console – Application](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4870.png)
    
    Console – Application
    
4.  Expand the _**Local Storage**_ list located in the _**Storage**_ section of the console's left menu.
    
    ![Console – Application – Local storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4871.png)
    
    Console – Application – Local storage
    
5.  Right-click your site(s) and click _**Clear**_ to delete the local storage.
    
    ![Local storage – Clear](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4872.png)
    
    Local storage – Clear
    

1.  Open a Firefox browser page.
    
2.  Use your keyboard's F12 key to open the Firefox Developer Tools Console.
    
    ![Firefox Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4865.png)
    
    Firefox Developer Tools Console
    
3.  Click _**Storage**_ in the console's top menu.
    
    ![Console – Storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4866.png)
    
    Console – Storage
    
4.  Expand the _**Local Storage**_ list located in the console's left menu.
    
    ![Console – Storage – Local Storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4867.png)
    
    Console – Storage – Local Storage
    
5.  Right-click your site(s) and click _**Delete All**_ to delete the local storage.
    
    ![Local Storage – Delete All](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4868.png)
    
    Local Storage – Delete All

    ![Opera Developer Tools Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4873.png)
    
    Opera Developer Tools Console

    Console – Application

    ![Console – Application – Local Storage](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4875.png)

    ![Local Storage – Clear](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4876.png)
    
    Local Storage – Clear

# Devolutions login page does not open in the browser - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions login page does not open in the browser
===================================================

When trying to connect to a Devolutions product such as Devolutions Hub or Devolutions Server, a connection page should open in your browser to allow you to enter your credentials. This window can sometimes be blocked by your browser or an extension installed on it. In this case, no error message is shown in the Devolutions product since the issue comes from the browser.

### Solution

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-login-page-does-not-open-browser/#solution)

First, change your browser or browser extension settings to remove or disable the setting that blocked the credentials prompt window. Try connecting again.

If that does not work, disable or delete the extension that causes the issue or change browser. Try connecting again.

If you still encouter issues, please [contact our customer support team](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Send Standalone - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send Standalone
===========================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)
    
*   [How to use Devolutions Send Standalone](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)
    
*   [How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)
    
*   [Technical details](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)
        

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 features a secure method to generate a link to share secrets instead of using insecure email to send sensitive data.

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)

The in-app version of Devolutions Send is currently under development and will be progressively deployed in Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub. More information will come in the future.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature set of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kb.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

How to use Devolutions Send Standalone
--------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)

1.  Go to the [Devolutions Send Standalone](https://send.devolutions.com/)
     website.
    
2.  Enter the _**Sender email**_, which is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    
3.  Enter your _**Secure message**_ to encrypt.
    
    *   A file of maximum 1 MB can be added to the secure message as well.
        
4.  Add a _**Passphrase**_ for extra security (mandatory if the recipient does not have a Devolutions Account, optional otherwise).
    
    *   _**Additional security options**_:
        
        *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days or 1 week.
            
        *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple views option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
            
        *   It is recommended to enable the _**Allow recipient to delete message**_ option.
            
5.  Read and agree to our online services terms.
    
6.  Click on _**Create secure link**_ to get the in-browser encrypted link. ![Interface](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0001_2024_3.png)
    
7.  Click on _**Copy to clipboard**_ and send it to the recipient(s).
    

How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret
---------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)

1.  Click on the received encrypted link.
    
    A Devolutions Send Standalone secret will always start with https://send.devolutions.com/receive/.
    
2.  Click on _**Unmask text**_.
    
    Make certain to be in a private setting before reading this message if it contains sensitive information.
    
    ![Unmask text](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0002_2024_3.png)
    
    Unmask text
    
3.  Enter the _**Passphrase**_ the sender provided (if necessary) and click on _**Decrypt**_. ![Decrypt button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0187.png)
    
4.  Once done, click on _**Delete Now**_.
    
5.  Click _**Yes**_. ![Yes button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0189.png) ![Deleted secure message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0190.png)
    

Technical details
-----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)

The core tenant of Devolutions Send is that Devolutions itself cannot decrypt the user's secret. This is accomplished via client-side (browser) encryption through a Rust program compiled to WASM (WebAssembly) in-browser. Therefore, Devolutions does not hold the encryption key and cannot decrypt the data.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/how-organizations-can-safely-share-confidential-information-with-devolutions-send/ "Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Prévenir les problèmes en faisant correspondre les versions majeures et mineures - Documentation Devolutions

Prévenir les problèmes en faisant correspondre les versions majeures et mineures
================================================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Version majeure](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)
    
*   [Version mineure](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#minor-version)
    
*   [Maintenance prolongée et dernières versions (Devolutions Server)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)
    
*   [Gestion des versions](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)
    

Toujours correspondre les versions majeures et mineures à travers les produits Devolutions (par exemple, 2025.1 avec 2025.1) pour éviter les erreurs et les problèmes de compatibilité.

Version majeure
---------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)

Une version majeure fait référence à une publication qui introduit des changements significatifs, de nouvelles fonctionnalités ou des améliorations majeures. La version majeure est identifiée par le premier chiffre après l'année. Par exemple, dans _**2024.3.27.0**_, la version majeure est _**3**_.

Version mineure
---------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#minor-version)

Une version mineure consiste en des mises à jour incrémentielles au sein d'une version majeure. Ces mises à jour incluent souvent des corrections de bogues, des correctifs de sécurité et des améliorations mineures mais n'introduisent pas de nouvelles fonctionnalités majeures ou de changements qui altèrent significativement la fonctionnalité. Par exemple, dans _**2024.3.27.0**_, la version mineure est _**27**_.

Maintenance prolongée et dernières versions (Devolutions Server)
----------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)

En plus de comprendre les versions majeures et mineures, il est important de distinguer entre maintenance prolongée et dernières versions. Cette distinction s'applique uniquement à Devolutions Server.

*   **Maintenance prolongée** : Se réfère à la dernière version mineure de la version majeure précédente (par ex., 2023.3.16).
    
*   **Dernier**: Fait référence à la version la plus récente disponible, qui comprend toutes les dernières fonctionnalités, améliorations, [correctifs de sécurité](https://devolutions.net/security/advisories/)
     et corrections de bogues (par exemple, 2024.1.11).
    

Chaque fois qu'une nouvelle version majeure est publiée (par ex., 2024.2.x), la dernière version (2024.1.x) devient la nouvelle version de maintenance prolongée. Aucune mise à jour de sécurité ou correctif n'est fourni pour les versions de maintenance prolongée précédentes (par ex., 2023.3.x ou antérieures). Ce cycle se répète pour chaque nouvelle version majeure.

Gestion des versions
--------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)

La _**Gestion de version**_ permet aux administrateurs de gérer la disponibilité de la source de données dans d'autres versions de Remote Desktop Manager pour Windows, Mac et Linux.

*   [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/commands/administration/system-settings/application-specific/version-management/)
    
*   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/web-interface/administration/configuration/system-settings/#vault-management)
      
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Connaissance générale - Documentation Devolutions

Connaissances générales
=======================

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Send Standalone - Documentation Devolutions

Devolutions Send Standalone
===========================

Sur cette page

*   [Fonctionnalités](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)
    
*   [Comment utiliser Devolutions Send Standalone](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)
    
*   [Comment recevoir un secret Devolutions Send Standalone](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)
    
*   [Détails techniques](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)
    *   [Voir aussi](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)
        

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 propose une méthode sécurisée pour générer un lien afin de partager des secrets au lieu d'utiliser des courriels non sécurisés pour envoyer des données sensibles.

Fonctionnalités
---------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)

La version in-app de Devolutions Send est actuellement en cours de développement et sera progressivement déployée dans Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server et Devolutions Hub. Plus d'informations à venir dans le futur.

Bien qu'ils partagent la même architecture sous-jacente, de légères différences existent entre l'ensemble des fonctionnalités des versions autonome et in-app de Devolutions Send.

*   Lien unique chiffré côté client.
    
*   Valable pour une durée personnalisable.
    
*   Protection optionnelle via une phrase secrète fournie par le client.
    
*   Les utilisateurs peuvent être des utilisateurs non-Devolutions (non liés à un compte Devolutions).
    
*   Limite de caractères de 10 Ko.
    
*   Un courriel de l'expéditeur est requis et stocké avec le GUID dans le cadre de la « charge utile » stockée dans la base de données.
    

Comment utiliser Devolutions Send Standalone
--------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)

1.  Aller sur le site [Devolutions Send Standalone](https://send.devolutions.com/)
    .
    
2.  Saisir le _**courriel de l'expéditeur**_, qui est requis et stocké avec le GUID comme partie de la “charge utile” stockée dans la base de données.
    
3.  Entrer votre _**Message sécurisé**_ à chiffrer.
    
    *   Un fichier d'une taille maximale de 1 Mo peut aussi être ajouté au message sécurisé.
        
4.  Ajouter une _**Phrase secrète**_ pour une sécurité supplémentaire (obligatoire si le destinataire n'a pas de compte Devolutions, facultatif sinon).
    
    *   _**Options de sécurité supplémentaires**_:
        
        *   La _**Durée du lien**_ peut être fixée à 1 heure, 24 heures, 3 jours ou 1 semaine.
            
        *   La _**Limite de vues**_ peut être réglée sur Illimité, Vue unique ou Vues multiples. L'option Vues multiples est utile pour définir un nombre exact de vues possibles.
            
        *   Il est recommandé d'activer l'option _**Autoriser le destinataire à supprimer le message**_.
            
5.  Lire et accepter nos conditions de service en ligne.
    
6.  Cliquer sur _**Créer un lien sécurisé**_ pour obtenir le lien chiffré dans le navigateur. ![Interface](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0001_2024_3.png)
    
7.  Cliquer sur _**Copier dans le presse-papiers**_ et l'envoyer au(x) destinataire(s).
    

Comment recevoir un secret Devolutions Send Standalone
------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)

1.  Cliquer sur le lien chiffré reçu.
    
    Un secret Devolutions Send Standalone commencera toujours par https://send.devolutions.com/receive/.
    
2.  Cliquer sur _**Faire apparaître le texte**_.
    
    S'assurer d'être dans un environnement privé avant de lire ce message s'il contient des informations sensibles.
    
    ![Unmask text](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0002_2024_3.png)
    
    Unmask text
    
3.  Entrer la _**Phrase secrète**_ fournie par l'expéditeur (si nécessaire) et cliquer sur _**Déchiffrer**_. ![Déchiffrer bouton](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0187.png)
    
4.  Une fois terminé, cliquer sur _**Supprimer maintenant**_.
    
5.  Cliquer sur _**Oui**_. ![Oui bouton](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0189.png) ![Message sécurisé supprimé](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0190.png)
    

Détails techniques
------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)

Le principe fondamental de Devolutions Send est que Devolutions elle-même ne peut pas déchiffrer le secret de l'utilisateur. Cela est accompli via un chiffrement côté client (navigateur) grâce à un programme Rust compilé en WASM (WebAssembly) dans le navigateur. Par conséquent, Devolutions ne détient pas la clé de chiffrement et ne peut pas déchiffrer les données.

### Voir aussi

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)

*   [Blog Devolutions - Comment les organisations peuvent partager en toute sécurité des informations confidentielles avec Devolutions Send](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/how-organizations-can-safely-share-confidential-information-with-devolutions-send/ "Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Prevent issues by matching major and minor versions - Devolutions Documentation

Prevent issues by matching major and minor versions
===================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Major version](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)
    
*   [Minor version](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#minor-version)
    
*   [Extended maintenance and latest versions (Devolutions Server)](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)
    
*   [Version management](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)
    

Always match major and minor versions across Devolutions products (e.g., 2025.1 with 2025.1) to avoid errors and compatibility issues.

Major version
-------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)

A major version refers to a release that introduces significant changes, new features, or major enhancements. The major version is identified by the first number after the year. For example, in _**2024.3.27.0**_, the major version is _**3**_.

Minor version
-------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#minor-version)

A minor version consists of incremental updates within a major version. These updates often include bug fixes, security patches, and minor enhancements but do not introduce major new features or changes that significantly alter functionality. For example, in _**2024.3.27.0**_, the minor version is _**27**_.

Extended maintenance and latest versions (Devolutions Server)
-------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)

In addition to understanding major and minor versions, it is important to distinguish between extended maintenance and latest versions. This distinction applies only to Devolutions Server.

*   **Extended maintenance**: Refers to the latest minor version of the previous major release (e.g., 2023.3.16).
    
*   **Latest**: Refers to the most recent version available, which includes all the latest features, improvements, [security patches](https://devolutions.net/security/advisories/)
    , and bug fixes (e.g., 2024.1.11).
    

Each time a new major version is released (e.g., 2024.2.x), the latest version (2024.1.x) becomes the new extended maintenance version. No security updates or patches are provided for previous extended maintenance versions (e.g., 2023.3.x or earlier). This lifecycle is repeated for each new major release.

Version management
------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)

The _**Version management**_ allows administrators to manage the data source availability in other versions of Remote Desktop Manager for Windows, Mac, and Linux.

*   [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/administration/system-settings/application-specific/version-management/)
    
*   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/configuration/system-settings/#vault-management)
      
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions login page does not open in the browser - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions login page does not open in the browser
===================================================

When trying to connect to a Devolutions product such as Devolutions Hub or Devolutions Server, a connection page should open in your browser to allow you to enter your credentials. This window can sometimes be blocked by your browser or an extension installed on it. In this case, no error message is shown in the Devolutions product since the issue comes from the browser.

### Solution

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-login-page-does-not-open-browser/#solution)

First, change your browser or browser extension settings to remove or disable the setting that blocked the credentials prompt window. Try connecting again.

If that does not work, disable or delete the extension that causes the issue or change browser. Try connecting again.

If you still encouter issues, please [contact our customer support team](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Installer des certificats racines - Documentation Devolutions

Installer des certificats racines
=================================

Voici la procédure pour installer des certificats racines sur Windows.

Firefox ne fait pas confiance aux mêmes certificats que Windows et un réglage doit être appliqué pour l'activer.

Veuillez consulter [l'article de la base de connaissances de Mozilla](https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox)
.

1.  Ouvrir la console de gestion Microsoft en recherchant _**MMC**_ dans le menu _**Démarrer**_. Une autre façon est d'appuyer sur les touches Windows+R sur votre clavier et, dans la fenêtre _**Exécuter**_, rechercher _**MMC**_.
    
2.  Sélectionner _**Fichier – Ajouter/Supprimer un module complémentaire**_.
    
3.  Dans la boîte _**Modules complémentaires disponibles**_, sélectionner _**Certificats**_.
    
4.  Cliquer sur le bouton _**Ajouter**_.
    
5.  Dans l'assistant, sélectionner _**Compte de l'ordinateur**_, puis cliquer sur _**Suivant**_.
    
6.  Sélectionner _**Ordinateur local**_, puis cliquer sur _**Terminer**_ pour terminer l'assistant.
    
7.  Cliquer sur _**OK**_ pour enregistrer vos modifications. Cette action fermera également le _**Ajouter ou supprimer un module complémentaire**_ dialogue.
    
8.  Dans la console, sélectionner _**Certificats (Ordinateur Local)**_.
    
9.  Dans la boîte _**Nom du magasin logique**_, faire un clic droit sur _**Autorités de certification racines de confiance**_ et sélectionner _**Toutes les tâches – Importer**_.
    
10.  Suivre les instructions dans l'_**Assistant d'importation de certificats**_ et fournir le fichier de certificat que vous avez.
    

Voici la procédure pour installer des certificats racines sous Linux (Ubuntu et Debian).

Firefox ne fait pas confiance aux mêmes certificats que Windows et un réglage doit être appliqué pour l'activer.

Veuillez consulter [l'article de la base de connaissances de Mozilla](https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox)
.

1.  sudo mkdir /usr/local/share/ca-certificates/extra
    
2.  sudo cp ca.crt /usr/local/share/ca-certificates/extra/ca.crt
    
3.  sudo update-ca-certificates
    

Guetter un "1" ajouté dans les messages de sortie.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Send Standalone - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Send Standalone
===========================

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)
    
*   [How to use Devolutions Send Standalone](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)
    
*   [How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)
    
*   [Technical details](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)
        

[Devolutions Send Standalone](https://devolutions.net/devolutions-send/)
 features a secure method to generate a link to share secrets instead of using insecure email to send sensitive data.

Features
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#features)

The in-app version of Devolutions Send is currently under development and will be progressively deployed in Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub. More information will come in the future.

Despite sharing the same underlying architecture, slight differences exist between the feature set of the standalone and in-app versions of Devolutions Send.

*   Unique link encrypted on the client side.
    
*   Valid for a customizable amount of time.
    
*   Optional protection via a client-provided passphrase.
    
*   Users may be non-Devolutions users (not linked to a Devolutions Account).
    
*   Character limit of 10 kb.
    
*   A sender email is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    

How to use Devolutions Send Standalone
--------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-use-devolutions-send-standalone)

1.  Go to the [Devolutions Send Standalone](https://send.devolutions.com/)
     website.
    
2.  Enter the _**Sender email**_, which is required and stored with the GUID as part of the “payload” stored in the database.
    
3.  Enter your _**Secure message**_ to encrypt.
    
    *   A file of maximum 1 MB can be added to the secure message as well.
        
4.  Add a _**Passphrase**_ for extra security (mandatory if the recipient does not have a Devolutions Account, optional otherwise).
    
    *   _**Additional security options**_:
        
        *   The _**Link duration**_ can be set to 1 hour, 24 hours, 3 days or 1 week.
            
        *   The _**View limit**_ can be set to Unlimited, Single view or Multiple views. The Multiple views option is useful for setting an exact amount of possible views.
            
        *   It is recommended to enable the _**Allow recipient to delete message**_ option.
            
5.  Read and agree to our online services terms.
    
6.  Click on _**Create secure link**_ to get the in-browser encrypted link. ![Interface](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0001_2024_3.png)
    
7.  Click on _**Copy to clipboard**_ and send it to the recipient(s).
    

How to receive a Devolutions Send Standalone secret
---------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#how-to-receive-a-devolutions-send-standalone-secret)

1.  Click on the received encrypted link.
    
    A Devolutions Send Standalone secret will always start with https://send.devolutions.com/receive/.
    
2.  Click on _**Unmask text**_.
    
    Make certain to be in a private setting before reading this message if it contains sensitive information.
    
    ![Unmask text](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/CLOUD0002_2024_3.png)
    
    Unmask text
    
3.  Enter the _**Passphrase**_ the sender provided (if necessary) and click on _**Decrypt**_. ![Decrypt button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0187.png)
    
4.  Once done, click on _**Delete Now**_.
    
5.  Click _**Yes**_. ![Yes button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0189.png) ![Deleted secure message](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0190.png)
    

Technical details
-----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#technical-details)

The core tenant of Devolutions Send is that Devolutions itself cannot decrypt the user's secret. This is accomplished via client-side (browser) encryption through a Rust program compiled to WASM (WebAssembly) in-browser. Therefore, Devolutions does not hold the encryption key and cannot decrypt the data.

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/devolutions-send-standalone/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/how-organizations-can-safely-share-confidential-information-with-devolutions-send/ "Devolutions Blog - How organizations can safely share confidential information with Devolutions Send")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Prevent issues by matching major and minor versions - Devolutions Documentation

Prevent issues by matching major and minor versions
===================================================

On this page

*   [Major version](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)
    
*   [Minor version](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#minor-version)
    
*   [Extended maintenance and latest versions (Devolutions Server)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)
    
*   [Version management](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)
    

Always match major and minor versions across Devolutions products (e.g., 2025.1 with 2025.1) to avoid errors and compatibility issues.

-------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#major-version)

-------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#extended-maintenance-and-latest-versions-devolutions-server)

In addition to understanding major and minor versions, it is important to distinguish between extended maintenance and latest versions. This distinction applies only to Devolutions Server.

*   **Extended maintenance**: Refers to the latest minor version of the previous major release (e.g., 2023.3.16).

    , and bug fixes (e.g., 2024.1.11).

------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/difference-major-minor-versions/#version-management)

*   [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/administration/system-settings/application-specific/version-management/)

# Install root certificates - Devolutions Documentation

Install root certificates
=========================

Here is the procedure to install root certificates on Windows.

Firefox does not trust the same certificates as Windows and a setting must be applied to enable this.

Please consult [Mozilla's knowledge base article](https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox)
.

1.  Open the Microsoft Management Console by searching for _**MMC**_ in the _**Start**_ menu. Another way is to press the Windows+R keys on your keyboard and, in the _**Run**_ window, search for _**MMC**_.
    
2.  Select _**File – Add/Remove Snap-in**_.
    
3.  In the _**Available snap-ins**_ box, select _**Certificates**_.
    
4.  Click the _**Add**_ button.
    
5.  In the wizard, select _**Computer Account**_, then click _**Next**_.
    
6.  Select _**Local computer**_, then click _**Finish**_ to end the wizard.
    
7.  Click _**OK**_ to save your changes. This action will also close the _**Add or Remove Snap-ins**_ dialog.
    
8.  In the console, select _**Certificates (Local Computer)**_.
    
9.  In the _**Logical Store Name**_ box, right-click _**Trusted Root Certification Authorities**_ and select _**All Tasks – Import**_.
    
10.  Follow the instructions in the _**Certificate Import Wizard**_ and provide the certificate file you have.
    

Here is the procedure to install root certificates on Linux (Ubuntu and Debian).

Firefox does not trust the same certificates as Windows and a setting must be applied to enable this.

Please consult [Mozilla's knowledge base article](https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/setting-certificate-authorities-firefox)
.

1.  sudo mkdir /usr/local/share/ca-certificates/extra
    
2.  sudo cp ca.crt /usr/local/share/ca-certificates/extra/ca.crt
    
3.  sudo update-ca-certificates
    

Watch for a "1" added in the output messages.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Life cycle policies - Devolutions Documentation

Life cycle policies
===================

Auf dieser Seite

# Vault privacy for administrators and users - Devolutions Documentation

Vault privacy for administrators and users
==========================================

The connection and password management solutions provided by Devolutions (Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub Business) offer a robust system that empowers administrators with complete and secure control over user vault management. However, it is natural for some customers to have concerns regarding the potential access to their "private" vaults by a malicious administrator. It is crucial to clarify the intended purpose of these "private" or "user" vaults, as they are primarily designed for personal corporate usage rather than personal private usage.

The distinction lies in the fact that these vaults are created within the context of a corporate environment, where administrators need to ensure continuous access to critical information stored within them. This necessity arises from various scenarios such as managing incidents, addressing employee terminations, and other operational requirements. By maintaining administrative access to these vaults, organizations can effectively safeguard against potential disruptions and ensure the smooth functioning of their operations.

While administrators do possess the ability to access these vaults, it is important to emphasize that this access is granted within the framework of their administrative responsibilities, and they are logged normally for visibility and traceability. Devolutions recognize the importance of privacy and understand that users may require an additional layer of security for their personal information. To address this concern and provide users with absolute privacy, Devolutions offers a free solution called Devolutions Hub Business Free.

Devolutions Hub Business Free is specifically designed to cater to the individual needs of users who seek heightened privacy and control over their personal data. This solution ensures that personal information remains entirely private, without any administrative access or intervention. Users can securely store and manage their sensitive data within their personal vaults, maintaining complete ownership and exclusive control over their information.

By recommending Devolutions Hub Business Free for users seeking absolute privacy, Devolutions acknowledge the importance of differentiating between the corporate and personal usage of their connection and password management solution. This approach provides a comprehensive suite of options, catering to both the administrative requirements of organizations and the individual privacy needs of users, thereby offering a well-rounded and versatile solution for diverse user scenarios.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Confidentialité des coffres pour les administrateurs et les utilisateurs - Documentation Devolutions

Confidentialité des coffres pour les administrateurs et les utilisateurs
========================================================================

Les solutions de gestion des connexions et des mots de passe proposées par Devolutions (Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server et Devolutions Hub Business) offrent un système robuste permettant aux administrateurs de disposer d’un contrôle complet et sécurisé sur la gestion du coffre des utilisateurs. Cependant, il est naturel que certains clients aient des préoccupations concernant l'accès éventuel à leur coffre « privé » par un administrateur malveillant. Il est essentiel de clarifier l’objectif prévu de ces coffres « privés » ou « utilisateur », car ils sont principalement conçus pour un usage professionnel personnel et non pour un usage privé personnel.

La distinction réside dans le fait que ces coffres sont créés dans le cadre d'un environnement corporatif, où les administrateurs doivent assurer un accès continu aux informations critiques qui y sont stockées. Cette nécessité découle de divers scénarios tels que la gestion des incidents, la gestion des départs d'employés et d'autres exigences opérationnelles. En maintenant un accès administratif à ces coffres, les organisations peuvent efficacement se protéger contre les perturbations potentielles et assurer le bon fonctionnement de leurs opérations.

Même si les administrateurs possèdent la capacité d’accéder à ces coffres, il est important de souligner que cet accès est accordé dans le cadre de leurs responsabilités administratives, et tout accès est consigné normalement pour assurer la visibilité et la traçabilité. Devolutions reconnaît l’importance de la confidentialité et comprend que les utilisateurs peuvent exiger une couche supplémentaire de sécurité pour leurs informations personnelles. Pour répondre à cette préoccupation et offrir aux utilisateurs une confidentialité absolue, Devolutions propose une solution gratuite dénommée Devolutions Hub Business Free.

Devolutions Hub Business Free est spécialement conçu pour répondre aux besoins individuels des utilisateurs recherchant une plus grande confidentialité et un meilleur contrôle sur leurs données personnelles. Cette solution garantit que les informations personnelles restent entièrement privées, sans aucun accès ni intervention administrative. Les utilisateurs peuvent stocker et gérer de façon sécurisée leurs données sensibles dans leurs coffres personnels, en conservant la pleine propriété et le contrôle exclusif de leurs informations.

En recommandant Devolutions Hub Business Free aux utilisateurs cherchant une confidentialité absolue, Devolutions reconnaît l’importance de différencier l’utilisation professionnelle et personnelle de leur solution de gestion des connexions et des mots de passe. Cette approche offre une suite complète d’options, répondant à la fois aux exigences administratives des organisations et aux besoins de confidentialité individuelle des utilisateurs, offrant ainsi une solution polyvalente et complète pour divers scénarios d’utilisation.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# How to renew your license - Devolutions Documentation

How to renew your license
=========================

Licenses can be renewed directly through the [Devolutions Portal](https://portal.devolutions.com/)
, provided the renewal is for the same product(s) and number of users. To switch products or modify the number of users, please contact our [sales team](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 for further assistance.

1.  Log in to the Devolutions Portal using the account that purchased the previous license.
    
2.  Once logged in, go to the _**Licenses**_ section. You will see a list of your active and expired licenses.
    
3.  Find the license you wish to renew and click the _**Renew now**_ button.
    
4.  You will be able to adjust the **license term** (e.g., 1 year, 3 years). No other modifications can be made at this stage.
    
5.  Click on _**Pay now**_ to confirm your renewal.
    
6.  Complete the payment.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Générer des certificats serveur et client auto-signés avec OpenSSL - Documentation Devolutions

Générer des certificats serveur et client auto-signés avec OpenSSL
==================================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Procédure](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)
    *   [Autorité de certification racine (AC)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
        
    *   [Certificat serveur](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
        
    *   [Certificat client](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
        
    *   [Traiter une demande de signature de certificat (CSR) sur l'autorité de certification racine (AC)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
        

Ceci est le guide définitif pour créer des certificats sécurisés, à la fois pour les serveurs et les clients, en utilisant OpenSSL.

Procédure
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)

Sur Windows, il est recommandé d'utiliser Chocolatey pour installer OpenSSL et ses dépendances. La ligne de commande est simplement \`choco install openssl\`.

*   [Créer l'AC racine](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
    
*   [Générer une demande de signature de certificat (CSR) – Serveur](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
    
*   [Générer une demande de signature de certificat (CSR) – Client](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
    
*   [Traiter une demande de signature de certificat (CSR) sur l'autorité de certification (CA) racine](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    

### Autorité de certification racine (AC)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)

1.  Générer la _**clé privée de l'AC racine**_ en utilisant la ligne de commande suivante :`openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out ca.key`. Chaque certificat doit avoir une clé privée correspondante.
    
2.  Générer le _**Certificat AC racine**_ (Autorité de Certification) en utilisant la ligne de commande suivante: `openssl req -new -x509 -sha256 -key ca.key -out ca.crt`.
    
3.  Entrer les informations sur l'AC (le certificat sera généré dans le fichier ca.crt):
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  [Installer le certificat](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/install-root-certificates/)
    .
    

Noter que le certificat doit être installé sur le serveur et sur tous les clients pour valider la légitimité des certificats émis. Certains navigateurs ont également des particularités qui sont décrites dans la rubrique.

### Certificat serveur

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)

Ces étapes sont généralement effectuées sur chaque serveur ou appareil pour lequel vous avez l'intention de demander un certificat. Installer OpenSSL s'il n'est pas présent. L'alternative est de déployer en toute sécurité la clé privée sur le serveur de destination en même temps que le certificat. Il est recommandé d'utiliser cette dernière approche uniquement si vous devez adhérer à des déploiements scriptés pour suivre les pratiques CloudOps/DevOps.

1.  Générer la _**clé privée du certificat serveur**_ en utilisant la ligne de commande suivante : `openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out server.key` (clé privée de 256 bits dans le fichier server.key). Chaque certificat doit avoir une clé privée correspondante.
    
2.  Générer la _**demande de signature de certificat**_ (CSR) du serveur en utilisant la ligne de commande suivante : `openssl req -new -sha256 -key server.key -out server.csr`. Cette demande sera ensuite traitée sur le serveur de l'AC racine.
    
3.  Entrer les informations sur le certificat du serveur (le FQDN exact utilisé par le serveur doit être spécifié). Par exemple:
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:vault.acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  Entrer un mot de passe dans l'invite, utiliser un gestionnaire de mots de passe ainsi qu'un générateur de mots de passe fort est essentiel.
    
5.  Transférer le fichier server.csr à l'AC racine.
    
6.  Traiter la demande en suivant les instructions [ci-dessous](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    .
    
7.  Déployer le certificat.
    

### Certificat client

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)

Suivre la même procédure que pour le [certificat serveur](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
, mais vous devez adapter deux attributs des informations que vous entrez à vos besoins, à savoir le _**Nom commun**_ et l'_**Adresse courriel**_.

    Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:John Doe
    Email Address []:JohnDoe@acme.com
    

### Traiter une demande de signature de certificat (CSR) sur l'autorité de certification racine (AC)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)

Traiter la CSR en générant un certificat.

Générer en utilisant la ligne de commande suivante, où le server.csr a été généré sur le serveur: `openssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 1000 -sha256`

Cela se traduit par le certificat généré dans le fichier server.crt. Vous devez le déployer sur le serveur où vous avez généré le CSR.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Licensing issues  - Devolutions Documentation

Licensing issues
================

On this page

*   [Invalid license (Product: RDM)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#invalid-license-product-rdm)

*   [Unable to save – License is invalid](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#unable-to-save-license-is-invalid)
    
*   [License not supported or not valid](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#license-not-supported-or-not-valid)

*   [This account does not have an assigned license or the license is expired. Ask your administrator to assign you a license](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#this-account-does-not-have-an-assigned-license-or-the-license-is-expired-ask-your-administrator-to-assign-you-a-license)
    
*   [Importing license key (.lic)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#importing-license-key-lic)
    
*   [License already exists](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#license-already-exists)
    
*   [About the .lic file](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#lic-file)
    

This article provides solutions to licensing issues encountered across Devolutions products. If none of the solutions resolve the issue, please contact our customer support team at [service@devolutions.net](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
.

Licenses cannot be manually added in the [Devolutions Portal](https://portal.devolutions.com/serials)
. For any issues or irregularities related to license display, please contact our sales team at [sales@devolutions.net](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
.

Removing expired licenses is a recommended best practice that can help resolve current issues and prevent future ones.

Invalid license (Product: RDM)
------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#invalid-license-product-rdm)

Licenses for Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Launcher, and integration module are not assigned in Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub.

#### Solutions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solutions)

*   Confirm that old licenses have been removed.
    
*   Verify that the new license has been added.
    
*   Check that the license is properly assigned to the user(s).
    

* * *

Invalid license – Not found
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#invalid-license-not-found)

OSC key is used in a version older than 2025.2.

#### Solutions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solutions-1)

*   Confirm that old licenses have been removed.
    
*   Verify that the new license has been added.
    
*   Check that the license is properly assigned to the user(s).
    

If the above solutions do not resolve the issue, contact our [sales team](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 to get a licorice key type.

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solutions-6)

*   Confirm that old licenses have been removed.
    
*   Add the new license via the [`.lic` file](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#lic-file)
    .
    
*   Verify that the new license has been added.
    
*   Refresh cache using CTRL + F5.
    

* * *

This account does not have an assigned license or the license is expired. Ask your administrator to assign you a license
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#this-account-does-not-have-an-assigned-license-or-the-license-is-expired-ask-your-administrator-to-assign-you-a-license)

#### Solutions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solutions-7)

Confirm that a license has been assigned to the user.

* * *

Importing license key (.lic)
----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#importing-license-key-lic)

The `.lic` file cannot be found.

#### Solutions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solutions-8)

*   Confirm that old licenses have been removed.
    
*   Add the new license via the [`.lic` file](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#lic-file)
    .
    
*   Check that the license is properly assigned to the user(s).
    

If the above solutions do not resolve the issue, contact our [sales team](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 so they can provide you with the `.lic` file.

* * *

License already exists
----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#license-already-exists)

A key was provided as part of an older package purchase, but it is no longer compatible and cannot be added.

#### Solution

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#solution)

The key is no longer necessary.

* * *

About the .lic file
-------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#lic-file)

The person who communicated with our [sales team](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 (main contact) is the one who received the `.lic` file via email. This file contains a JSON Web Token (JWT). You can import and register the license while offline using the `.lic` file.

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/license/licensing-issues/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions store – Tailored packages for your IT needs](https://store.devolutions.net/package)

# Generate a self-signed server and client certificates with OpenSSL - Devolutions Documentation

Generate a self-signed server and client certificates with OpenSSL
==================================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Procedure](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)
    *   [Root Certification authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
        
    *   [Server certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
        
    *   [Client certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
        
    *   [Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
        

This is the definitive guide to create secure certificates, for both servers and clients, using OpenSSL.

Procedure
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)

On Windows, it is recommended to use Chocolatey to install OpenSSL and its dependencies. The command line is simply \`choco install openssl\`.

*   [Create the Root Certification Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
    
*   [Generate a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) – Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
    
*   [Generate a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) – Client](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
    
*   [Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    

### Root Certification authority (CA)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)

1.  Generate the _**Root CA Private Key**_ using the following command line:`openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out ca.key`. Every certificate must have a corresponding private key.
    
2.  Generate the _**Root CA Certificate**_ (Certificate Authority) using the following command line: `openssl req -new -x509 -sha256 -key ca.key -out ca.crt`.
    
3.  Enter the information about the CA (the certificate will be generated in the ca.crt file):
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  [Install the certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/install-root-certificates/)
    .
    

Note that the certificate must be installed on the server and on all of the clients to validate the legitimacy of issued certificates. Some browsers also have particularities which are described in the topic.

### Server certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)

These steps are usually performed on each server or device for which you intend to request a certificate. Install OpenSSL if it is not present. The alternative is to securely deploy the private key to the destination server at the same time as the certificate. It is recommended to use this last approach only if you must adhere to scripted deployments to follow CloudOps/DevOps practices.

1.  Generate the _**Server Certificate Private Key**_ using the following command line: `openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out server.key` (256bit private key in the server.key file). Every certificate must have a corresponding private key.
    
2.  Generate the server _**Certificate Signing Request**_ (CSR) using the following command line: `openssl req -new -sha256 -key server.key -out server.csr`. This request will later be processed on the Root CA server.
    
3.  Enter the information about the server certificate (the exact FQDN that is used by the server must be specified). For Example:
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:vault.acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  Enter a password into the prompt, using a password manager as well as a strong password generator is essential.
    
5.  Transfer the server.csr file to the Root CA.
    
6.  Process the request by following the instructions [below](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    .
    
7.  Deploy the certificate.
    

### Client certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)

Follow the same procedure as for the [Server certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
, but you must adapt two attributes of the information you enter to your needs, namely the _**Common Name**_ and the _**Email Address**_.

    Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:John Doe
    Email Address []:JohnDoe@acme.com
    

### Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)

Process the CSR by generating a certificate.

Generate it using the following command line, where the server.csr has been generated on the server: `openssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 1000 -sha256`

This results in the certificate being generated in the server.crt file. You must deploy it to the server where you generated the CSR.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Qu'est-ce que SHA-256 ? - Documentation Devolutions

Qu'est-ce que SHA-256 ?
=======================

La famille des Algorithmes de Hachage Sécurisés (SHA) englobe plusieurs fonctions de hachage cryptographique, avec SHA-256 étant une variante largement utilisée. Les hachages cryptographiques agissent comme des signatures numériques pour les données, permettant la comparaison de grands ensembles de données par leurs valeurs de hachage plutôt que par leur contenu intégral. Cette méthode est similaire à l'utilisation des empreintes digitales pour l'identification—chaque ensemble de données a un hachage unique, et même une modification mineure des données change la valeur du hachage.

SHA-256 génère un hachage distinctif et de taille fixe de 256 bits (32 octets), fonctionnant comme un processus à sens unique qui le rend excellent pour les vérifications de l'intégrité des données, les défis d'authentification, les mesures anti-falsification, les signatures numériques et les applications blockchain.

Par exemple, lors du téléchargement d'applications telles que celles de Devolutions, SHA-256 aide à vérifier que les données reçues correspondent à l'original, garantissant qu'elles n'ont pas été altérées en raison d'erreurs réseau ou d'attaques de maliciels. Pour vérifier le hachage d'un fichier, cliquez simplement sur l'icône SHA-256 sur la page de téléchargement du site Web de Devolutions.

Pour des instructions supplémentaires sur la manière d'obtenir le hachage SHA-256 d'un fichier, consultez la documentation de Microsoft sur la [commande Get-FileHash](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/module/microsoft.powershell.utility/get-filehash?view=powershell-7.2)
. Voici comment l'utiliser :

    Get-FileHash C:\Users\user1\Downloads\Setup.RemoteDesktopManager.exe -Algorithm SHA256 | Format-List.
    

Cette commande fournit une sortie structurée de la valeur du hachage, facilitant ainsi la vérification de l'intégrité de votre fichier.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# What is SHA-256? - Devolutions Documentation

What is SHA-256?
================

The Secure Hash Algorithm (SHA) family encompasses several cryptographic hash functions, with SHA-256 being a widely-used variant. Cryptographic hashes act as digital signatures for data, enabling the comparison of large data sets by their hash values rather than their full content. This method is similar to using fingerprints for identification—each data set has a unique hash, and even a minor alteration to the data changes the hash value.

SHA-256 generates a distinctive, fixed-size 256-bit (32-byte) hash, functioning as a one-way process that makes it excellent for data integrity checks, authentication challenges, anti-tampering measures, digital signatures, and blockchain applications.

For instance, when downloading applications like those from Devolutions, SHA-256 helps verify that the data received matches the original, ensuring it has not been altered due to network errors or malware attacks. To check a file's hash, simply click on the SHA-256 icon on the download page of the Devolutions website.

For additional guidance on how to obtain the SHA-256 hash of a file, refer to Microsoft's documentation on the [Get-FileHash](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/module/microsoft.powershell.utility/get-filehash?view=powershell-7.2)
 command. Here is how you can use it:

    Get-FileHash C:\Users\user1\Downloads\Setup.RemoteDesktopManager.exe -Algorithm SHA256 | Format-List.
    

This command provides a structured output of the hash value, aiding in easy verification of your file's integrity.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Change Devolutions Gateway certificate - Devolutions Documentation

Change Devolutions Gateway certificate
======================================

Devolutions Gateway certificates can be changed quickly and easily in the Devolutions Server Console. Follow the instructions below:

1.  Open the Devolutions Server Console, and click on the _**Edit**_ button located in the _**Devolutions Gateway**_ section of the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
    ![Edit the Devolutions Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4043_2025_2.png)
    
    Edit the Devolutions Gateway
    
2.  Then, change the _**HTTP listener**_ to _**https**_, and click on the ellipsis button (_**…**_) in the _**Certificate file**_ field under the _**Certificate configuration**_ heading.
    
    ![Change the HTTP listener and choose a different certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4045_2025_3.png)
    
    Choose a different certificate
    
3.  Choose the certificate `.pfx` file to switch to, and click _**Ok**_ to save the changes.
    
4.  Wait until the service restarts or do it manually in the Windows Services console.
    
5.  Finally, verify the health of the Devolutions Gateway as described in [Troubleshooting Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-a-gateways-health)
    .
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Changer le certificat Devolutions Gateway - Documentation Devolutions

Changer le certificat Devolutions Gateway
=========================================

Les certificats Devolutions Gateway peuvent être changés rapidement et facilement dans la console Devolutions Server. Suivre les instructions ci-dessous :

1.  Ouvrir la console Devolutions Server, et cliquer sur le bouton _**Modifier**_ situé dans la section _**Devolutions Gateway**_ de l'onglet _**Compagnons**_.
    
    ![Edit the Devolutions Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4043_2025_2.png)
    
    Edit the Devolutions Gateway
    
2.  Ensuite, changer le _**HTTP listener**_ à _**https**_, et cliquer sur le bouton des points de suspension (_**…**_) dans le champ_**fichier de certificat**_ sous le titre _**configuration du certificat**_.
    
    ![Change the HTTP listener and choose a different certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4045_2025_3.png)
    
    Choose a different certificate
    
3.  Choisir le fichier de certificat `.pfx` à utiliser, et cliquer sur _**Ok**_ pour enregistrer les modifications.
    
4.  Attendre que le service redémarre ou le faire manuellement dans la console des Services Windows.
    
5.  Enfin, vérifier la santé du Devolutions Gateway comme décrit dans [Dépannage Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-a-gateways-health)
    .
