# Vault privacy for administrators and users - Devolutions Documentation

Vault privacy for administrators and users
==========================================

The connection and password management solutions provided by Devolutions (Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub Business) offer a robust system that empowers administrators with complete and secure control over user vault management. However, it is natural for some customers to have concerns regarding the potential access to their "private" vaults by a malicious administrator. It is crucial to clarify the intended purpose of these "private" or "user" vaults, as they are primarily designed for personal corporate usage rather than personal private usage.

The distinction lies in the fact that these vaults are created within the context of a corporate environment, where administrators need to ensure continuous access to critical information stored within them. This necessity arises from various scenarios such as managing incidents, addressing employee terminations, and other operational requirements. By maintaining administrative access to these vaults, organizations can effectively safeguard against potential disruptions and ensure the smooth functioning of their operations.

While administrators do possess the ability to access these vaults, it is important to emphasize that this access is granted within the framework of their administrative responsibilities, and they are logged normally for visibility and traceability. Devolutions recognize the importance of privacy and understand that users may require an additional layer of security for their personal information. To address this concern and provide users with absolute privacy, Devolutions offers a free solution called Devolutions Hub Business Free.

Devolutions Hub Business Free is specifically designed to cater to the individual needs of users who seek heightened privacy and control over their personal data. This solution ensures that personal information remains entirely private, without any administrative access or intervention. Users can securely store and manage their sensitive data within their personal vaults, maintaining complete ownership and exclusive control over their information.

By recommending Devolutions Hub Business Free for users seeking absolute privacy, Devolutions acknowledge the importance of differentiating between the corporate and personal usage of their connection and password management solution. This approach provides a comprehensive suite of options, catering to both the administrative requirements of organizations and the individual privacy needs of users, thereby offering a well-rounded and versatile solution for diverse user scenarios.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Generate a self-signed server and client certificates with OpenSSL - Devolutions Documentation

Generate a self-signed server and client certificates with OpenSSL
==================================================================

On this page

*   [Procedure](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)
    *   [Root Certification authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
        
    *   [Server certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
        
    *   [Client certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
        
    *   [Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
        

This is the definitive guide to create secure certificates, for both servers and clients, using OpenSSL.

Procedure
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#procedure)

On Windows, it is recommended to use Chocolatey to install OpenSSL and its dependencies. The command line is simply \`choco install openssl\`.

*   [Create the Root Certification Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)
    
*   [Generate a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) – Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
    
*   [Generate a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) – Client](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)
    
*   [Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    

### Root Certification authority (CA)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#root-certification-authority-ca)

1.  Generate the _**Root CA Private Key**_ using the following command line:`openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out ca.key`. Every certificate must have a corresponding private key.
    
2.  Generate the _**Root CA Certificate**_ (Certificate Authority) using the following command line: `openssl req -new -x509 -sha256 -key ca.key -out ca.crt`.
    
3.  Enter the information about the CA (the certificate will be generated in the ca.crt file):
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  [Install the certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/install-root-certificates/)
    .
    

Note that the certificate must be installed on the server and on all of the clients to validate the legitimacy of issued certificates. Some browsers also have particularities which are described in the topic.

### Server certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)

These steps are usually performed on each server or device for which you intend to request a certificate. Install OpenSSL if it is not present. The alternative is to securely deploy the private key to the destination server at the same time as the certificate. It is recommended to use this last approach only if you must adhere to scripted deployments to follow CloudOps/DevOps practices.

1.  Generate the _**Server Certificate Private Key**_ using the following command line: `openssl ecparam -name prime256v1 -genkey -noout -out server.key` (256bit private key in the server.key file). Every certificate must have a corresponding private key.
    
2.  Generate the server _**Certificate Signing Request**_ (CSR) using the following command line: `openssl req -new -sha256 -key server.key -out server.csr`. This request will later be processed on the Root CA server.
    
3.  Enter the information about the server certificate (the exact FQDN that is used by the server must be specified). For Example:
    
        Country Name (2 letter code) [AU]:US
        State or Province Name (full name) [Some-State]:CA
        Locality Name (eg, city) []:Toontown
        Organization Name (eg, company) [Internet Widgits Pty Ltd]:Acme inc.
        Organizational Unit Name (eg, section) []:Security
        Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:vault.acme.com
        Email Address []:security@acme.com
        
    
4.  Enter a password into the prompt, using a password manager as well as a strong password generator is essential.
    
5.  Transfer the server.csr file to the Root CA.
    
6.  Process the request by following the instructions [below](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)
    .
    
7.  Deploy the certificate.
    

### Client certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#client-certificate)

Follow the same procedure as for the [Server certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#server-certificate)
, but you must adapt two attributes of the information you enter to your needs, namely the _**Common Name**_ and the _**Email Address**_.

    Common Name (e.g. server FQDN or your name) []:John Doe
    Email Address []:JohnDoe@acme.com
    

### Process a Certificate Signing Request (CSR) on the Root Certificate Authority (CA)

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/general-knowledge/secure-self-signed-certificates/#process-a-certificate-signing-request-csr-on-the-root-certificate-authority-ca)

Process the CSR by generating a certificate.

Generate it using the following command line, where the server.csr has been generated on the server: `openssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 1000 -sha256`

This results in the certificate being generated in the server.crt file. You must deploy it to the server where you generated the CSR.

# What is SHA-256? - Devolutions Documentation

What is SHA-256?
================

The Secure Hash Algorithm (SHA) family encompasses several cryptographic hash functions, with SHA-256 being a widely-used variant. Cryptographic hashes act as digital signatures for data, enabling the comparison of large data sets by their hash values rather than their full content. This method is similar to using fingerprints for identification—each data set has a unique hash, and even a minor alteration to the data changes the hash value.

SHA-256 generates a distinctive, fixed-size 256-bit (32-byte) hash, functioning as a one-way process that makes it excellent for data integrity checks, authentication challenges, anti-tampering measures, digital signatures, and blockchain applications.

For instance, when downloading applications like those from Devolutions, SHA-256 helps verify that the data received matches the original, ensuring it has not been altered due to network errors or malware attacks. To check a file's hash, simply click on the SHA-256 icon on the download page of the Devolutions website.

For additional guidance on how to obtain the SHA-256 hash of a file, refer to Microsoft's documentation on the [Get-FileHash](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/module/microsoft.powershell.utility/get-filehash?view=powershell-7.2)
 command. Here is how you can use it:

    Get-FileHash C:\Users\user1\Downloads\Setup.RemoteDesktopManager.exe -Algorithm SHA256 | Format-List.
    

This command provides a structured output of the hash value, aiding in easy verification of your file's integrity.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Configurer l'injection des identifiants basée sur un proxy - Documentation Devolutions

Configurer l'injection des identifiants basée sur un proxy
==========================================================

Devolutions Gateway offre une fonctionnalité pour l'injection des identifiants via un proxy, permettant aux utilisateurs de se connecter à des sessions distantes sans jamais avoir accès à ses identifiants sur leur machine. Suivre les étapes ci-dessous pour configurer l'injection d'identifiants basée sur un proxy sur une entrée :

1.  Configurer Devolutions Gateway dans [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     ou [Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/)
    .
    
2.  Modifier une entrée RDP et [la lier à un ensemble de règles Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/configure-proxy-based-credential-injection/)
     (ces étapes sont identiques quel que soit la source de données).
    
3.  Se rendre sur l’interface Web de la source de données choisie, accéder à _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_, puis cliquer sur le bouton _**Modifier**_ de l’ensemble de règles Gateway lié.
    
4.  Puis, cocher l'option _**Activer l’injection d’identifiants basée sur un proxy**_ sous _**Sécurité**_.
    

Dès lors, lancer la session sans exposer ses identifiants sur la machine de l'utilisateur.

Pour une sécurité maximale lors de la gestion des utilisateurs externes, créer un [_**utilisateur Contractor**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/user-groups-based-security/#contractors)
 avec la permission _**Exécuter**_ mais PAS la permission _**Afficher mot de passe**_.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Change Devolutions Gateway certificate - Devolutions Documentation

Change Devolutions Gateway certificate
======================================

Devolutions Gateway certificates can be changed quickly and easily in the Devolutions Server Console. Follow the instructions below:

1.  Open the Devolutions Server Console, and click on the _**Edit**_ button located in the _**Devolutions Gateway**_ section of the _**Companions**_ tab.
    
    ![Edit the Devolutions Gateway](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4043_2025_2.png)
    
    Edit the Devolutions Gateway
    
2.  Then, change the _**HTTP listener**_ to _**https**_, and click on the ellipsis button (_**…**_) in the _**Certificate file**_ field under the _**Certificate configuration**_ heading.
    
    ![Change the HTTP listener and choose a different certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4045_2025_3.png)
    
    Choose a different certificate
    
3.  Choose the certificate `.pfx` file to switch to, and click _**Ok**_ to save the changes.
    
4.  Wait until the service restarts or do it manually in the Windows Services console.
    
5.  Finally, verify the health of the Devolutions Gateway as described in [Troubleshooting Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-a-gateways-health)
    .
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Configure proxy-based credential injection - Devolutions Documentation

Configure proxy-based credential injection
==========================================

Devolutions Gateway offers a feature for the injection of credentials through a proxy, allowing users to connect to remote sessions without ever having access to its credentials on their machine. Follow the steps below to configure proxy-based credential injection on an entry:

1.  Configure Devolutions Gateway in [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     or [Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/)
    .
    
2.  Edit an RDP entry, and [link it to a Gateway ruleset](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/configure-proxy-based-credential-injection/)
     (these steps are the same regardless of the data source).
    
3.  Head over to your chosen data source's web interface, go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_, and click to _**Edit**_ button on the linked Gateway ruleset.
    
4.  Then, check the _**Enable proxy-based credential injection**_ option under _**Security**_.
    

From then on, launching the session will not expose its credentials on the user's machine.

For maximum security when dealing with external users, create a [_**Contractor**_ user](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/user-groups-based-security/#contractors)
 with the _**Execute**_ permission but NOT the _**View password**_ permission.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Lancer une session SSH dans un client Web - Documentation Devolutions

Lancer une session SSH dans un client Web
=========================================

Sur cette page

*   [Exigences](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Entrées de session prises en charge](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [Configuration de la session terminal SSH](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)
    
*   [Voir également](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)
    

Lancer la session SSH directement depuis votre navigateur web préféré via l'interface web Devolutions Server ou Devolutions Hub.

Exigences
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)

Pour utiliser cette fonctionnalité, certaines exigences doivent être respectées, à savoir :

*   Windows 10 ou 11.
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     version 2023.1 ou ultérieure.
    
*   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     version 2023.1 ou ultérieure.
    
*   Une entrée de [session de terminal SSH](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
     avec un type de VPN Devolutions Gateway configuré doit être créée.
    
*   Une licence Remote Desktop Manager ou Devolutions Launcher doit être assignée à l'utilisateur lançant la session.
    

Entrées de session prises en charge
-----------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

D'autres types de sessions peuvent être lancés via l'interface web Devolutions Server :

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (à distance)
    
*   [RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   Terminal SSH
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

Configuration de la session terminal SSH
----------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)

Suivre les étapes ci-dessous pour configurer correctement votre session de terminal SSH afin de la lancer dans un navigateur :

Les étapes ci-dessous supposent que vous avez déjà une entrée de session terminal SSH. Si vous ne l'avez pas encore créée et souhaitez savoir comment, voir [Créer des entrées manuellement](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  Dans l'interface web du Devolutions Server, aller aux _**Propriétés...**_ de votre entrée de session terminal SSH.
    
2.  Dans la section _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_, sélectionner _**Devolutions Gateway**_ dans la liste déroulante _**Type de VPN**_.
    

!\[Définir Devolutions Gateway comme le type de VPN pour votre connexion\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4191\_2025\_1.png "Définir Devolutions Gateway comme le type de VPN pour votre connexion")

3.  Dans le menu déroulant _**Connecter**_, sélectionner _**Toujours connecter**_.
    

!\[Mode de connexion Devolutions Gateway\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4192\_2025\_1.png "Mode de connexion Devolutions Gateway")

4.  Sous _**Paramètres**_, sélectionner le Devolutions Gateway à utiliser pour cette connexion, puis cliquer sur _**Vérifier la santé**_ pour s'assurer que le Gateway est fonctionnel. Sa version doit être 2023.1 ou ultérieure pour que cela fonctionne. Cliquer sur _**Mettre à jour**_ pour enregistrer vos modifications.
    

!\[Sélectionner la bonne instance Devolutions Gateway et tester si la connexion fonctionne correctement\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4193\_2025\_1.png "Sélectionner la bonne instance Devolutions Gateway et tester si la connexion fonctionne correctement")

5.  Une fois toutes les conditions remplies, vous pouvez appuyer sur le bouton _**Ouvrir dans le client Web**_.
    

![Launch the SSH terminal connection](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4194_2025_1.png)

Launch the SSH terminal connection

Voir également
--------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Démarrer une session RDP dans un client web](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   [Options d'entrée du terminal SSH](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Démarrer une session RDP dans un client web - Documentation Devolutions

Démarrer une session RDP dans un client web
===========================================

Sur cette page

*   [Exigences](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Entrées de session prises en charge](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [Configuration de la session RDP](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
    
*   [Lancement de la connexion](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)
    *   [Fonctionnalités prises en charge](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)
        
    *   [Espionnage de session](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)
        
    *   [Voir aussi](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)
        

Lancer les connexions RDP et d'autres types de sessions directement depuis le navigateur via l'interface web de Devolutions Server.

Basé sur [IronRDP](https://github.com/Devolutions/IronRDP)
 (implémentation Rust du protocole RDP) et son composant web assembly, le client web, passant par un Devolutions Gateway, garantit une communication sécurisée en utilisant directement le protocole. Contrairement à Apache Guacamole, aucun protocole intermédiaire n'est utilisé et contrairement à RD Web Access, il n'y a pas de couche TLS supplémentaire redondante. Cela garantit de bonnes performances.

Exigences
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)

Pour utiliser cette fonctionnalité, certaines exigences doivent être remplies, à savoir :

*   Le navigateur doit répondre à ces exigences minimales de version :
    
    *   Chrome : 102
        
    *   Firefox: 102
        
    *   Safari : 16.4
        
*   Windows 10 ou 11.
    
*   Windows Server 2016 et versions ultérieures.
    
*   Avoir une version [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     2023.1 ou ultérieure.
    
*   Avoir une version [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     2023.1.3 ou ultérieure.
    
*   Avoir une [connexion de type RDP](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
     avec un type de _VPN_ passerelle configuré.
    
*   Avoir l'autorisation _**Voir le mot de passe**_ si vous êtes celui qui utilise la session.
    
    *   Lors de l'utilisation d'IronRDP, un appel est généré vers l'outil, et le mot de passe peut être vu lorsque les outils de développement sont activés.
        
*   Avoir une licence Remote Desktop Manager ou Devolutions Launcher assignée à l'utilisateur qui lancera la session.
    

Si HTTPS est utilisé pour les communications de Devolutions Gateway, il est fortement recommandé d'utiliser le Subject Alternative Name (SAN). Dans la plupart des cas, un Common Name (CN) est uniquement utilisé comme solution de secours et généralement ignoré lorsque SAN est défini. Toutefois, pour des raisons de meilleures pratiques de sécurité et de compatibilité, il est préférable que le CN corresponde à l'une des entrées SAN.

Entrées de session prises en charge
-----------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

D'autres types d'entrées de session peuvent être lancées via l'interface web de Devolutions Server:

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (à distance)
    
*   RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)
    
*   Terminal SSH
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

Configuration de la session RDP
-------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)

Suivre les étapes ci-dessous pour configurer correctement votre session RDP pour la lancer dans un navigateur :

Les étapes ci-dessous supposent que vous avez déjà une entrée de session RDP. Si vous ne l'avez pas encore créée et souhaitez savoir comment procéder, voir [Créer des entrées manuellement](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  Dans l'interface web de Devolutions Server, aller aux _**Propriétés**_ de votre _entrée RDP_.
    
2.  Dans la section _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_, sélectionner _**Devolutions Gateway**_ dans la _**liste déroulante**_ de type de VPN.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2046_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type
    
3.  Dans la _**liste déroulante**_ Connexion, sélectionner _**Connecter si incapacité à ping/sanner des ports**_.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2047_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan
    
4.  Sous _**Paramètres**_, sélectionner le _**Devolutions Gateway**_ à utiliser pour cette connexion, puis cliquer sur _**Vérifier la santé**_ pour s'assurer que le Gateway est fonctionnel. Sa version doit être 2023.1 ou ultérieure.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2048_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health
    
5.  Dans la section _**Enregistrement de session**_, définir le _**Mode**_ d'enregistrement.
    
    ![Session recording – Mode](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2049_2024_3.png)
    
    Session recording – Mode
    
6.  Cliquer sur _**Mettre à jour**_ pour enregistrer vos modifications.
    

Lancement de la connexion
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)

Une fois toutes les conditions remplies, vous pouvez appuyer sur le bouton _**Ouvrir dans le client web**_ pour lancer la connexion depuis le client web.

![Open in web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0069_2024_3.png)

Open in web client

Si le mode d'enregistrement de la session a été défini sur _**Optionnel**_ dans les propriétés de l'entrée, il vous sera demandé si vous souhaitez enregistrer cette session.

![Do you want to record your session?](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2052_2024_3.png)

Do you want to record your session?

Un nouvel onglet de navigateur devrait s'ouvrir et votre session devrait commencer.

![RDP session opened in a web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2053_2024_3.png)

RDP session opened in a web client

Si la connexion ne fonctionne pas, vérifier à nouveau les [exigences](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
 ou visiter [RDP Web client not showing](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/ "RDP web client not showing")
.

### Fonctionnalités prises en charge

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)

Le menu des outils dans l'interface web RDP contient ce qui est actuellement pris en charge. Notez que la fonctionnalité de copier-coller (y compris le presse-papiers) est également prise en charge.

![Supported features](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2051_2024_3.png)

Supported features

| Icône | Option | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_fullscreen.png) | Plein écran | Afficher le contenu de la session en s'assurant d'occuper toujours l'espace maximum de l'écran. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_smallscreen.png) | Adapter à l'écran (par défaut) | Adapter la taille pour s'ajuster au mieux à l'espace disponible afin que toute la session soit toujours visible. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_screen.png) | Taille réelle | Se conformer à la résolution de l'hôte cible. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_windows.png) | Touche Windows | Envoyer le signal de la touche Windows (cependant, la touche doit également fonctionner). |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_gear.png) | Ctrl + Alt + Del | Envoie la commande au système hôte. |

### Espionnage de session

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)

Avec le support de suivi de session Devolutions Gateway, il est possible de regarder un enregistrement de session en cours pour assister ou auditer le travail en cours. Accédez à l'onglet d'enregistrement d'une entrée pour voir une icône clignotante indiquant un enregistrement en cours, puis cliquez pour regarder en temps réel.

1.  Lancer une session RDP basée sur le Web dans l'interface web de Devolutions Server.
    
2.  Le Gateway commence automatiquement à enregistrer la session en arrière-plan.
    
3.  Exécuter un script de chronométrage pour montrer le temps écoulé.
    
4.  Retourner à l'interface web de Devolutions Server.
    
5.  Sélectionner l' _entrée RDP_.
    
6.  Ouvrir l'onglet d'enregistrement de l'entrée RDP pour voir la session en temps réel.
    

### Voir aussi

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/spotlight-on-web-based-rdp-ard-ssh-in-devolutions-server-and-hub/ "Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub")

# Quickly deploy Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Quickly deploy Devolutions Gateway
==================================

Learn how to quickly deploy Devolutions Gateway in the following environments:

*   [Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway configuration with Devolutions Hub Business](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/hub/hub-business-configuration/)
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway configuration in Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/rdm-configuration/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Launch an SSH session in a web client - Devolutions Documentation

Launch an SSH session in a web client
=====================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Supported session entries](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [SSH terminal session configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)
    
*   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)
    

Launch SSH session directly from your favorite web browser via the Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub web interface.

Requirements
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)

To use this feature, certain requirements must be met, namely:

*   Windows 10 or 11.
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   An [SSH terminal session](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
     entry with a Devolutions Gateway VPN type configured must be created.
    
*   A Remote Desktop Manager or Devolutions Launcher license must be assigned to the user launching the session.
    

Supported session entries
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

Other session types can be launched via the Devolutions Server web interface:

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (remote)
    
*   [RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   SSH terminal
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

SSH terminal session configuration
----------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)

Follow the steps below to properly configure your SSH terminal session to launch it in a browser:

The steps below assume that you already have an SSH terminal session entry. If you have not yet created it and want to learn how, see [Create entries manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web interface, go to the _**Properties...**_ of your SSH terminal entry.
    
2.  In the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ section, select _**Devolutions Gateway**_ in the _**VPN type**_ drop-down list.
    

!\[Set Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type for your connection\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4191\_2025\_1.png "Set Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type for your connection")

3.  In the _**Connect**_ drop-down menu, select _**Always connect**_.
    

!\[Devolutions Gateway connect mode\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4192\_2025\_1.png "Devolutions Gateway connect mode")

4.  Under _**Settings**_, select the Devolutions Gateway to use for this connection, then click on _**Check health**_ to make sure the Gateway is functional. Its version must be 2023.1 or later for this to work. Click on _**Update**_ to save your changes.
    

!\[Select the correct Devolutions Gateway instance and test if the connection functions properly\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4193\_2025\_1.png "Select the correct Devolutions Gateway instance and test if the connection functions properly")

5.  Once all the conditions are met, you can press the _**Open in web client**_ button.
    

![Launch the SSH terminal connection](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4194_2025_1.png)

Launch the SSH terminal connection

See also
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Launch an RDP session in a web client](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   [SSH terminal entry options](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Launch an RDP session in a web client - Devolutions Documentation

Launch an RDP session in a web client
=====================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Supported session entries](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [RDP session configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
    
*   [Launching the connection](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)
    *   [Supported features](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)
        
    *   [Session shadowing](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)
        
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)
        

Launch RDP connections and other session types directly from the browser via the Devolutions Server web interface.

Based on [IronRDP](https://github.com/Devolutions/IronRDP)
 (Rust implementation of the RDP protocol) and its web assembly component, the web client, passing through a Devolutions Gateway, ensures a secure communication using the protocol directly. Unlike Apache Guacamole, no intermediate protocol is used and unlike RD Web Access, there is no redundant extra TLS layer. This ensures good performance.

Requirements
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)

To use this feature, certain requirements must be met, namely:

*   The browser must meet these minimal version requirements:
    
    *   Chrome: 102
        
    *   Firefox: 102
        
    *   Safari: 16.4
        
*   Windows 10 or 11.
    
*   Windows Server 2016 and later.
    
*   Have a [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   Have a [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     version 2023.1.3 or later.
    
*   Have an [RDP type connection](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
     with a gateway type VPN configured.
    
*   Have the _**View password**_ permission if you are the one to use the session.
    
    *   When using IronRDP, a call is generated to the tool, and the password can be seen when the developer tools are enabled.
        
*   Have a Remote Desktop Manager or Devolutions Launcher license assigned to the user who will launch the session.
    

If HTTPS is used for Devolutions Gateway communications, it is highly recommended to use Subject Alternative Name (SAN). In most cases, a Common Name (CN) is only used as fallback and typically ignored when SAN is set. It is best security and compatibility practice, however, to make the CN match one of the SAN entries.

Supported session entries
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

Other session entry types can be launched via the Devolutions Server web interface:

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (remote)
    
*   RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)
    
*   SSH terminal
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

RDP session configuration
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)

Follow the steps below to properly configure your RDP session to launch it in a browser:

The steps below assume that you already have an RDP session entry. If you have not yet created it and want to learn how, see [Create entries manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web interface, go to the _**Properties**_ of your RDP entry.
    
2.  In the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ section, select _**Devolutions Gateway**_ in the _**VPN type**_ drop-down list.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2046_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type
    
3.  In the _**Connect**_ drop-down list, select _**Connect if unable to ping/port scan**_.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2047_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan
    
4.  Under _**Settings**_, select the _**Devolutions Gateway**_ to use for this connection, then click on _**Check health**_ to make sure the Gateway is functional. Its version must be 2023.1 or later.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2048_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health
    
5.  In the _**Session recording**_ section, set the recording _**Mode**_.
    
    ![Session recording – Mode](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2049_2024_3.png)
    
    Session recording – Mode
    
6.  Click _**Update**_ to save your changes.
    

Launching the connection
------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)

Once all the conditions are met, you can press the _**Open in web client**_ button to launch the connection from the web client.

![Open in web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0069_2024_3.png)

Open in web client

If the session recording mode was set to _**Optional**_ in the entry properties, you will be asked if you want to record this session.

![Do you want to record your session?](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2052_2024_3.png)

Do you want to record your session?

A new browser tab should open and your session should start.

![RDP session opened in a web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2053_2024_3.png)

RDP session opened in a web client

If the connection does not work, check the [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
 again or visit [RDP Web client not showing](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/ "RDP web client not showing")
.

### Supported features

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)

The tools menu in the RDP web interface contains what is currently supported. Note that the copy/paste feature (including the clipboard) is also supported.

![Supported features](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2051_2024_3.png)

Supported features

| Icon | Option | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_fullscreen.png) | Full screen | Displays the content of the session, making sure to always occupy the maximum space on the screen. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_smallscreen.png) | Fit to screen (default) | Adapts the size to best fit the available space so that the entire session is always visible. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_screen.png) | Real size | Conforms to the resolution of the target host. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_windows.png) | Windows key | Sends the signal of the Windows key (however, the key must also work). |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_gear.png) | Ctrl + Alt + Del | Sends the command to the host system. |

### Session shadowing

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)

With Devolutions Gateway session shadowing support, it is possible to watch an in-progress session recording to assist or audit in-process work. Navigate to the recording tab of an entry to see a pulsing icon indicating an in-progress recording, then click to watch in real-time.

1.  Launch a web-based RDP session in the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
2.  The Gateway automatically starts recording the session in the background.
    
3.  Run a stopwatch script to show the elapsed time.
    
4.  Go back to the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
5.  Select the RDP entry.
    
6.  Open the RDP entry's recording tab to view the session in real time.
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/spotlight-on-web-based-rdp-ard-ssh-in-devolutions-server-and-hub/ "Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Use Devolutions Gateway with an external browser - Devolutions Documentation

Use Devolutions Gateway with an external browser
================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Workaround to set up without having to close Chrome](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)
    
*   [PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#powershell)
    *   [Batch edit using PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#batch-edit-using-powershell)
        
    *   [Temporary edit with Before Open](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#temporary-edit-with-before-open)
        
    *   [Deleting the folder](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#deleting-the-folder)
        

It is possible to use Devolutions Gateway with an external browser, but at the moment there are a few limitations to be aware of because of the browser design:

*   It only works with Google Chrome.
    
*   Google Chrome must be closed when opening a website from Remote Desktop Manager. A solution to this can be found in the [workaround](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)
    .
    
*   In case there are other proxy settings with Chrome (by GPO, command line, settings, etc.), they might conflict with each other and Devolutions Gateway will not work.
    
*   In case Google Chrome is closed and does not have any other proxy settings, set up the entry to open externally like any other entries in Remote Desktop Manager. No additional installations/addons are needed for this to work.
    

Workaround to set up without having to close Chrome
---------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)

1.  Right-click to go into the _**Properties**_ of the _**Web Browser**_ entry that has the Devolutions Gateway set.
    
2.  In the _**General**_ section, set the _**Display**_ to _**External**_.
    
    ![Common – General – Display – External](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0019.png)
    
    Common – General – Display – External
    
3.  Go to the _**Advanced**_ tab.
    
    ![Advanced Tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0020.png)
    
    Advanced Tab
    
4.  Check _**User Data Path**_.
    
    ![User Data Path Option](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0021.png)
    
    User Data Path Option
    
5.  Enter a path for a new Chrome user data to be stored.
    
6.  Click _**Ok**_ to save the changes.
    

PowerShell
----------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#powershell)

This section will showcase multiple solutions by using PowerShell.

### Batch edit using PowerShell

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#batch-edit-using-powershell)

It is possible to [batch edit](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/commands/edit/batch-edit/)
 the entries with a custom PowerShell command to make all of them use a different path (can be the temp or any place users are allowed to use it):

    $connection.Web.UseUserDataPath = $true;
    $connection.Web.UserDataPath  = "C:\MyPath\" + $connection.ID;
    $RDM.Save();
    

### Temporary edit with Before Open

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#temporary-edit-with-before-open)

It is also possible to [temporarily use the properties](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/how-to-articles/execute-powershell-connection)
 'Web.UseUserDataPath' set to true and 'Web.UserDataPath' set the path to the temp or any place users are allowed to use it that can be dynamic with a Before Open Event (using PowerShell Script).

    $RDM.Connection.Web.UseUserDataPath = $true
    $RDM.Connection.Web.UserDataPath = "C:\MyPath\" + $RDM.Connection.ID
    

### Deleting the folder

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#deleting-the-folder)

This code is used to delete the folder on the onClose Event:

    $connectionID = $RDM.Connection.ID
    Remove-Item -Path "C:\MyPath\$connectionID" -Recurse -Force
    

It is not possible to open a website using the Devolutions Gateway that is already running without the workarounds because of the way Google Chrome is designed. An already opened Chrome cannot change the proxy settings dynamically.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Utiliser Devolutions Gateway avec un navigateur externe - Documentation Devolutions

Utiliser Devolutions Gateway avec un navigateur externe
=======================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Solution de contournement pour configurer sans avoir à fermer Chrome](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)
    
*   [PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#powershell)
    *   [Modifier en lot en utilisant PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#batch-edit-using-powershell)
        
    *   [Édition temporaire avec Avant d'Ouvrir](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#temporary-edit-with-before-open)
        
    *   [Supprimer le dossier](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#deleting-the-folder)
        

Il est possible d'utiliser Devolutions Gateway avec un navigateur externe, mais pour le moment il y a quelques limitations à prendre en compte en raison de la conception du navigateur :

*   Cela fonctionne uniquement avec Google Chrome.
    
*   Google Chrome doit être fermé lors de l'ouverture d'un site Web depuis Remote Desktop Manager. Une solution à cela peut être trouvée dans la [solution de contournement](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)
    .
    
*   Au cas où il y aurait d'autres paramètres de proxy avec Chrome (par objet stratégie de groupe, ligne de commande, paramètres, etc.), ils pourraient entrer en conflit les uns avec les autres et Devolutions Gateway ne fonctionnera pas.
    
*   Au cas où Google Chrome est fermé et n'a pas d'autres paramètres de proxy, configurer l'entrée pour ouvrir de manière externe comme toute autre entrée dans Remote Desktop Manager. Aucune installation ou addon supplémentaire n'est nécessaire pour cela.
    

Solution de contournement pour configurer sans avoir à fermer Chrome
--------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#workaround-to-set-up-without-having-to-close-chrome)

1.  Faire un clic droit pour accéder aux _**Propriétés**_ de l'entrée de _**navigateur Web**_ qui a le Devolutions Gateway défini.
    
2.  Dans la section _**Général**_, définir l'_**Affichage**_ sur _**Externe**_.
    
    ![Common – General – Display – External](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0019.png)
    
    Common – General – Display – External
    
3.  Aller à l'onglet _**Avancé**_.
    
    ![Advanced Tab](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0020.png)
    
    Advanced Tab
    
4.  Vérifier le chemin de _**données utilisateur**_.
    
    ![User Data Path Option](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0021.png)
    
    User Data Path Option
    
5.  Entrer un chemin pour le stockage des nouvelles données utilisateur de Chrome.
    
6.  Cliquer sur _**Ok**_ pour enregistrer les modifications.
    

PowerShell
----------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#powershell)

Cette section présentera plusieurs solutions en utilisant PowerShell.

### Modifier en lot en utilisant PowerShell

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#batch-edit-using-powershell)

Il est possible de [modifier en lot](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/commands/edit/batch-edit/)
 les entrées avec une commande PowerShell personnalisée pour toutes les faire utiliser un chemin différent (peut être le temporaire ou tout endroit où les utilisateurs sont autorisés à l'utiliser) :

    $connection.Web.UseUserDataPath = $true;
    $connection.Web.UserDataPath  = "C:\MyPath\" + $connection.ID;
    $RDM.Save();
    

### Édition temporaire avec Avant d'Ouvrir

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#temporary-edit-with-before-open)

Il est également possible d'[utiliser temporairement les propriétés](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/kb/how-to-articles/execute-powershell-connection)
 'Web.UseUserDataPath' réglé sur true et 'Web.UserDataPath' définir le chemin vers le temporaire ou tout endroit où les utilisateurs sont autorisés à l'utiliser, ce qui peut être dynamique avec un événement Before Open (en utilisant un script PowerShell).

    $RDM.Connection.Web.UseUserDataPath = $true
    $RDM.Connection.Web.UserDataPath = "C:\MyPath\" + $RDM.Connection.ID
    

### Supprimer le dossier

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-dgw-external-browser/#deleting-the-folder)

Ce code est utilisé pour supprimer le dossier lors de l'événement onClose :

    $connectionID = $RDM.Connection.ID
    Remove-Item -Path "C:\MyPath\$connectionID" -Recurse -Force
    

Il n'est pas possible d'ouvrir un site Web utilisant le Devolutions Gateway déjà en cours d'exécution sans les solutions de contournement à cause de la façon dont Google Chrome est conçu. Un Chrome déjà ouvert ne peut pas changer les paramètres du proxy de manière dynamique.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Launch an RDP session in a web client - Devolutions Documentation

Launch an RDP session in a web client
=====================================

On this page

*   [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Supported session entries](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [RDP session configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
    
*   [Launching the connection](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)
    *   [Supported features](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)
        
    *   [Session shadowing](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)
        
    *   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)
        

Launch RDP connections and other session types directly from the browser via the Devolutions Server web interface.

Based on [IronRDP](https://github.com/Devolutions/IronRDP)
 (Rust implementation of the RDP protocol) and its web assembly component, the web client, passing through a Devolutions Gateway, ensures a secure communication using the protocol directly. Unlike Apache Guacamole, no intermediate protocol is used and unlike RD Web Access, there is no redundant extra TLS layer. This ensures good performance.

Requirements
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)

To use this feature, certain requirements must be met, namely:

*   The browser must meet these minimal version requirements:
    
    *   Chrome: 102
        
    *   Firefox: 102
        
    *   Safari: 16.4
        
*   Windows 10 or 11.
    
*   Windows Server 2016 and later.
    
*   Have a [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   Have a [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     version 2023.1.3 or later.
    
*   Have an [RDP type connection](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)
     with a gateway type VPN configured.
    
*   Have the _**View password**_ permission if you are the one to use the session.
    
    *   When using IronRDP, a call is generated to the tool, and the password can be seen when the developer tools are enabled.
        
*   Have a Remote Desktop Manager or Devolutions Launcher license assigned to the user who will launch the session.
    

If HTTPS is used for Devolutions Gateway communications, it is highly recommended to use Subject Alternative Name (SAN). In most cases, a Common Name (CN) is only used as fallback and typically ignored when SAN is set. It is best security and compatibility practice, however, to make the CN match one of the SAN entries.

Supported session entries
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

Other session entry types can be launched via the Devolutions Server web interface:

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (remote)
    
*   RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)
    
*   SSH terminal
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

RDP session configuration
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#rdp-session-configuration)

Follow the steps below to properly configure your RDP session to launch it in a browser:

The steps below assume that you already have an RDP session entry. If you have not yet created it and want to learn how, see [Create entries manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web interface, go to the _**Properties**_ of your RDP entry.
    
2.  In the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ section, select _**Devolutions Gateway**_ in the _**VPN type**_ drop-down list.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2046_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – VPN type
    
3.  In the _**Connect**_ drop-down list, select _**Connect if unable to ping/port scan**_.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2047_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Connect – Connect if unable to ping/port scan
    
4.  Under _**Settings**_, select the _**Devolutions Gateway**_ to use for this connection, then click on _**Check health**_ to make sure the Gateway is functional. Its version must be 2023.1 or later.
    
    ![VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2048_2024_3.png)
    
    VPN/Tunnel/Gateway – Settings – Check health
    
5.  In the _**Session recording**_ section, set the recording _**Mode**_.
    
    ![Session recording – Mode](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2049_2024_3.png)
    
    Session recording – Mode
    
6.  Click _**Update**_ to save your changes.
    

Launching the connection
------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#launching-the-connection)

Once all the conditions are met, you can press the _**Open in web client**_ button to launch the connection from the web client.

![Open in web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0069_2024_3.png)

Open in web client

If the session recording mode was set to _**Optional**_ in the entry properties, you will be asked if you want to record this session.

![Do you want to record your session?](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2052_2024_3.png)

Do you want to record your session?

A new browser tab should open and your session should start.

![RDP session opened in a web client](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2053_2024_3.png)

RDP session opened in a web client

If the connection does not work, check the [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#requirements)
 again or visit [RDP Web client not showing](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/ "RDP web client not showing")
.

### Supported features

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#supported-features)

The tools menu in the RDP web interface contains what is currently supported. Note that the copy/paste feature (including the clipboard) is also supported.

![Supported features](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS2051_2024_3.png)

Supported features

| Icon | Option | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_fullscreen.png) | Full screen | Displays the content of the session, making sure to always occupy the maximum space on the screen. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_smallscreen.png) | Fit to screen (default) | Adapts the size to best fit the available space so that the entire session is always visible. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_screen.png) | Real size | Conforms to the resolution of the target host. |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_windows.png) | Windows key | Sends the signal of the Windows key (however, the key must also work). |
| ![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_icons_gear.png) | Ctrl + Alt + Del | Sends the command to the host system. |

### Session shadowing

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#session-shadowing)

With Devolutions Gateway session shadowing support, it is possible to watch an in-progress session recording to assist or audit in-process work. Navigate to the recording tab of an entry to see a pulsing icon indicating an in-progress recording, then click to watch in real-time.

1.  Launch a web-based RDP session in the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
2.  The Gateway automatically starts recording the session in the background.
    
3.  Run a stopwatch script to show the elapsed time.
    
4.  Go back to the Devolutions Server web interface.
    
5.  Select the RDP entry.
    
6.  Open the RDP entry's recording tab to view the session in real time.
    

### See also

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub](https://blog.devolutions.net/2024/08/spotlight-on-web-based-rdp-ard-ssh-in-devolutions-server-and-hub/ "Devolutions Blog - Spotlight on: Web-based RDP, ARD, SSH in Devolutions Server & Hub")
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Launch an SSH session in a web client - Devolutions Documentation

Launch an SSH session in a web client
=====================================

On this page

*   [Requirements](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)
    
*   [Supported session entries](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)
    
*   [SSH terminal session configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)
    
*   [See also](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)
    

Launch SSH session directly from your favorite web browser via the Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub web interface.

Requirements
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#requirements)

To use this feature, certain requirements must be met, namely:

*   Windows 10 or 11.
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   [Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/upgrade-server/)
     version 2023.1 or later.
    
*   An [SSH terminal session](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
     entry with a Devolutions Gateway VPN type configured must be created.
    
*   A Remote Desktop Manager or Devolutions Launcher license must be assigned to the user launching the session.
    

Supported session entries
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#supported-session-entries)

Other session types can be launched via the Devolutions Server web interface:

*   Active Directory
    
*   Apple Remote Desktop (ARD)
    
*   PowerShell (remote)
    
*   [RDP (Microsoft Remote Desktop)](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   SSH terminal
    
*   Telnet
    
*   VNC
    

SSH terminal session configuration
----------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#ssh-terminal-session-configuration)

Follow the steps below to properly configure your SSH terminal session to launch it in a browser:

The steps below assume that you already have an SSH terminal session entry. If you have not yet created it and want to learn how, see [Create entries manually](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/vault/entries/create-entries-manually/)
.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web interface, go to the _**Properties...**_ of your SSH terminal entry.
    
2.  In the _**VPN/Tunnel/Gateway**_ section, select _**Devolutions Gateway**_ in the _**VPN type**_ drop-down list.
    

!\[Set Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type for your connection\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4191\_2025\_1.png "Set Devolutions Gateway as the VPN type for your connection")

3.  In the _**Connect**_ drop-down menu, select _**Always connect**_.
    

!\[Devolutions Gateway connect mode\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4192\_2025\_1.png "Devolutions Gateway connect mode")

4.  Under _**Settings**_, select the Devolutions Gateway to use for this connection, then click on _**Check health**_ to make sure the Gateway is functional. Its version must be 2023.1 or later for this to work. Click on _**Update**_ to save your changes.
    

!\[Select the correct Devolutions Gateway instance and test if the connection functions properly\](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4193\_2025\_1.png "Select the correct Devolutions Gateway instance and test if the connection functions properly")

5.  Once all the conditions are met, you can press the _**Open in web client**_ button.
    

![Launch the SSH terminal connection](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS4194_2025_1.png)

Launch the SSH terminal connection

See also
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-ssh-session-web-client/#see-also)

*   [Launch an RDP session in a web client](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/launch-rdp-session-web-client/)
    
*   [SSH terminal entry options](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/entry-settings/ssh-session-entry/)
