# Type de connexion de tunnel Devolutions Gateway - Documentation Devolutions

Type de connexion de tunnel Devolutions Gateway
===============================================

Sur cette page

*   [Écouteurs](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)
    *   [Règles d'autorisation](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)
        
    *   [Utiliser le Devolutions Gateway Tunnel en dehors de Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)
        

Le _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ peut répondre à des besoins similaires au transfert de port SSH/Tunnel SSH, mais il ne nécessite rien d'autre que Devolutions Gateway lui-même. Il est utile lors de l'utilisation de connexions qui n'ont pas de support intégré dans Remote Desktop Manager via le Devolutions Gateway. L'entrée se trouve sous _**Nouvelle entrée**_ – _**Session**_ – _**Connexions à distance**_.

Devolutions Gateway doit être configuré dans la source de données de Remote Desktop Manager, puis configuré via [héritage](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/inheritance/)
 ou sur la connexion elle-même. L'option est sous **_Propriétés_** – **_Connexion_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_Général_**.

![Tunnel](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0116.png)

Tunnel

Écouteurs
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)

Si le **_Écouteur_** est réglé sur 0.0.0.0, il acceptera les connexions de toute source au sein du réseau. En raison de la difficulté de suivre la responsabilité, il est recommandé de **_NE PAS_** faire cela pour plusieurs raisons de sécurité.

*   Dans presque tous les scénarios, l'écouteur (adresse de liaison) doit être réglé sur l'adresse de retour (127.0.0.1) de la machine locale.
    
*   _**TCP Forward**_ : C'est l'équivalent du transfert de port.
    
*   _**HTTP**_ et _**SOCKS5**_ proxies : Ces écouteurs sont configurés comme des proxy ce qui rend possible l'utilisation d'un navigateur autre que Google Chrome. Cela signifie également qu'ils utilisent une destination dynamique.
    
    Dynamic ports can be used with all three listener types. If the value is 0, it will automatically find an available port.
    

### Règles d'autorisation

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)

Les écouteurs _**HTTP**_ et _**SOCKS5**_ utiliseront également les _**Règles d'autorisation**_ pour spécifier les destinations autorisées, tout ce qui n'est pas sur la liste blanche sera refusé.

Les _**Filtres de cible**_ peuvent être spécifiés en utilisant des adresses IP ou des noms d'hôtes. Les deux peuvent contenir des caractères génériques. Chaque _**Filtre de cible**_ doit spécifier explicitement un port de destination. Laisser le port par défaut à '0' entraînera une erreur lors de la tentative de sauvegarde du filtre.

![Default](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0163.png)

Default

#### Exemples de filtres de cible valides

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#examples-of-valid-target-filters)

| Filtre de cible | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `windjammer.net:80` | Permettre le trafic HTTP vers le nom d'hôte windjammer.net. |
| `*.windjammer.net:443` | Permettre le trafic HTTPS vers tout sous-domaine de windjammer.net mais pas vers windjammer.net directement. |
| `192.168.0.*:22` | Permettre le trafic SSH vers toute adresse IP entre 192.168.0.0 et 192.168.0.255. |
| `*:3389` | Permettre le trafic RDP vers tout point de terminaison accessible par le Devolutions Gateway. |

Il est possible d'ajouter plusieurs _**Filtres de cible**_ à votre entrée adaptée à l'utilisation souhaitée du tunnel. Par exemple, il se peut que vous ajoutiez le même nom d'hôte plusieurs fois mais avec des ports différents, comme 80 et 443, pour permettre le trafic HTTP et HTTPS.

### Utiliser le Devolutions Gateway Tunnel en dehors de Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)

Une fois ouvert, il est possible d'utiliser un _**Devolutions Gateway Tunnel**_ à partir d'une application externe à Remote Desktop Manager. Vous pourriez, par exemple, l'utiliser avec un navigateur web ou toute autre application qui supporte le type de proxying (TCP, HTTP, ou SOCKS5) que vous avez spécifié dans la connexion.

#### Exemple : Utiliser le tunnel avec l'outil en ligne de commande cURL

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#example-using-the-tunnel-with-the-curl-command-line-tool)

Il est possible d'ajouter votre point de terminaison de proxy ainsi que le port spécifié ou celui qui a été généré par l'entrée _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ avec l'argument -x.

    curl -x socks5h://127.0.0.1:65535 windjammer.net
    

Si vous avez défini vos filtres cibles à l'aide des noms d'hôtes, il est important de s'assurer que votre application ne résout pas le nom d'hôte avant de l'envoyer au tunnel ; sinon, le trafic sera refusé. Les applications ont généralement des paramètres pour activer ou désactiver ce comportement. Par exemple, dans le navigateur Web Firefox, il faut activer l'option **_Proxy DNS lors de l'utilisation de SOCKS v5_** dans le panneau de configuration du proxy pour que ce scénario fonctionne correctement.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Devolutions Gateway tunnel connection type - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway tunnel connection type
==========================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Listeners](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)
    *   [Allow Rules](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)
        
    *   [Using the Devolutions Gateway Tunnel oustide of Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)
        

The _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ can fulfill similar needs to SSH port forwarding/SSH tunneling, but it requires nothing other than Devolutions Gateway itself. It is useful when using connections that do not have built-in support in Remote Desktop Manager through the Devolutions Gateway. The entry can be found under _**New Entry**_ – _**Session**_ – _**Remote Connections**_.

Devolutions Gateway needs to be set up in the Remote Desktop Manager data source and then configured through [inheritance](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/inheritance/)
 or on the connection itself. The option is under **_Properties_** – **_Connection_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_General_**.

![Tunnel](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0116.png)

Tunnel

Listeners
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)

If the **_Listener_** is set to 0.0.0.0, it will accept connections from any source within the network. Due to the difficulty in tracking accountability, it is recommended **_NOT_** to do this for multiple security reasons.

*   In almost every scenario, the listener (bind address) should be set to the loopback address (127.0.0.1) from the local machine.
    
*   _**TCP Forward**_: It is the equivalent to port forwarding.
    
*   _**HTTP**_ and _**SOCKS5**_ proxies: These listeners are set up as proxies which makes it possible to use a browser other than Google Chrome. This also means they use a dynamic destination.
    
    Dynamic ports can be used with all three listener types. If the value is 0, it will automatically find an available port.
    

### Allow Rules

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)

The _**HTTP**_ and _**SOCKS5**_ listeners will also make use of the _**Allow Rules**_ to specify authorized destinations, anything not on the allow list will be denied.

_**Target filters**_ can be specified using IP addresses or hostnames. Both can contain wildcards. Each _**Target filter**_ must explicitly specify a destination port. Leaving the default port as '0' will result in an error when attempting to save the filter.

![Default](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0163.png)

Default

#### Examples of valid target filters

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#examples-of-valid-target-filters)

| Target filter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `windjammer.net:80` | Allows HTTP traffic to the hostname windjammer.net. |
| `*.windjammer.net:443` | Allows HTTPS traffic to any subdomain of windjammer.net but not to windjammer.net directly. |
| `192.168.0.*:22` | Allows SSH traffic to any IP address between 192.168.0.0 to 192.168.0.255. |
| `*:3389` | Allows RDP traffic to any endpoint reachable by the Devolutions Gateway. |

You can add multiple _**Target filters**_ to your entry tailored to your intended use of the tunnel. For example, you might add the same hostname several times but with different ports, like 80 and 443, to permit both HTTP and HTTPS traffic.

### Using the Devolutions Gateway Tunnel oustide of Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)

Once opened, it is possible to use a _**Devolutions Gateway Tunnel**_ from an applicaton that is external to Remote Desktop Manager. You could, for instance, use it with a web browser or any other application that supports the type of proxying (TCP, HTTP, or SOCKS5) that you specified in the connection.

#### Example: Using the tunnel with the cURL command-line tool

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#example-using-the-tunnel-with-the-curl-command-line-tool)

You can add your proxy endpoint along with the port specified or the one that was generated by the _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ entry with the -x argument.

    curl -x socks5h://127.0.0.1:65535 windjammer.net
    

If you have set your target filters using hostnames, it is important to ensure that your application does not resolve the hostname before sending it to the tunnel; otherwise, the traffic will be denied. Applications typically have settings to enable or disable this behavior. For example, in the web browser Firefox, you need to enable the **_Proxy DNS when using SOCKS v5_** option in the proxy configuration panel for this scenario to function correctly.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Use Windows certificate store for Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Use Windows certificate store for Devolutions Gateway
=====================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Importing the certificate into the Windows certificate store](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate-into-the-windows-certificate-store)
    *   [Converting an X.509 certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#converting-an-x509-certificate)
        
    *   [Importing the certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate)
        
*   [Giving the Devolutions Gateway service read permission on the certificate private key](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#giving-the-devolutions-gateway-service-read-permission-on-the-certificate-private-key)
    
*   [Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)
    
*   [Configuring Windows certificate store via PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-powershell)
    

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate.

It is possible to use the Windows certificate store as a TLS certificate source. Instead of using a file, store and manage your certificates with Windows. As of the time of writing, this functionality is not exposed in the Devolutions Gateway configuration console GUI. To configure, you must either directly modify the gateway.json file or use the Devolutions.PowerShell module.

With the new functionality, a [few additional parameters](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway#configuration)
 are available to configure the source of the certificate.

If you have a previously defined \`TlsCertificateFile\` and/or \`TlsPrivateKeyFile\` configuration, removal is unnecessary as \`TlsCertificateSource\` tells Devolutions Gateway where to search for the certificate.

*   **TlsCertificateSource** (string): Source for the TLS certificate, possible values shown below.
    
    *   **External** (default): Retrieve a certificate stored on the file system. See the options `TlsCertificateFile`, `TlsPrivateKeyFile`, and `TlsPrivateKeyPassword`.
        
    *   **System**: Retrieve the certificate managed by the system certificate store. See the options `TlsCertificateSubjectName`, `TlsCertificateStoreName`, and `TlsCertificateStoreLocation`.
        
*   **TlsCertificateSubjectName** (string): Subject name of the certificate for TLS when using System source.
    
*   **TlsCertificateStoreName** (string): Name of the System Certificate Store to use for TLS (default is My).
    
*   **TlsCertificateStoreLocation** (string): Location of the System Certificate Store to use for TLS, possible values shown below.
    
    *   **CurrentUser** (default)
        
    *   **CurrentService**
        
    *   **LocalMachine**
        

Importing the certificate into the Windows certificate store
------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate-into-the-windows-certificate-store)

First, import your certificate into the Windows certificate store. Windows supports the following certificate formats:

*   X.509 certificate - \*.cer, \*.crt
    
*   Personal Information Exchange - \*.pfx, \*.p12
    
*   Microsoft Serialized certificate Store - \*.sst
    
*   PKCS #7 Certificates - \*.spc, \*.p7b
    

If using the \`External\` method via \`TlsCertificateSource\`, then Devolutions Gateway only supports bundling the public and private key in a PFX (PKCS#12) file. Otherwise, you will need to define the \`TlsPrivateKeyFile\` parameter as well.

### Converting an X.509 certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#converting-an-x509-certificate)

Devolutions Gateway requires a private key with the TLS certificate; therefore, you may need to combine the public key with its private key. Here are two methods: [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-remote-desktop-manager)
 and the built-in [Windows utility `certutil`](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-the-windows-certutil-utility)
.

#### Using Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-remote-desktop-manager)

The _**X.509 Certificate**_ entry can be used to import said certificate and export it in several different formats, including PFX.

1.  In Remote Desktop Manager click on _**New Entry**_ – _**Credential Management**_ – _**General**_ – _**X.509 Certificate**_.
    
    ![X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0180.png)
    
    X.509 Certificate
    
2.  Select the certificate and click _**Open**_.
    
    ![Open](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0164.png)
    
    Open
    
3.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Next](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0165.png)
    
    Next
    
4.  Click on the ellipsis and select the _**Private key**_.
    
    ![Ellipsis button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0166.png)
    
    Ellipsis button
    
5.  Click on _**Open**_.
    
    ![KEY file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0181.png)
    
    KEY file
    
    The **_Private key_** must be in the \`.key\` extension.
    
6.  Click _**Finish**_.
    
    ![Finish](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0168.png)
    
    Finish
    
7.  Fill in the information, then click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Information fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0167.png)
    
    Information fields
    
8.  Select the entry and click _**Save Certificate As**_ (also available in the right-click context menu).
    
    ![Save Certificate As](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0186.png)
    
    Save Certificate As
    
9.  In the _**Export Format**_ field choose _**Personal Information Exchange (pfx)**_.
    
10.  Choose where the file will be saved by clicking on the ellipsis.
    
11.  Enter a strong password, then click _**Export**_.
    
    ![Export X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0182.png)
    
    Export X.509 Certificate
    

#### Using the Windows certutil utility

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-the-windows-certutil-utility)

Use the built-in Windows `certutil` utility to combine a certificate (`.crt` or `.cer`) file and its private key (`.key`). Both files need to have the same name. `certutil -MergePFX file.crt file.pfx`

![certutil](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0169.png)

certutil

### Importing the certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate)

After acquiring the certificate and certificate private key file, import it into Windows.

1.  Install the certificate:
    
    *   If Windows auto-detects the certificate, double-click it and choose _**Install Certificate...**_; or
        
    *   Open `certmgr.msc` to the intended store location (`LocalMachine` or `CurrentUser`), right-click on the wanted location (ex: _**Personal/Certificates**_) and choose _**All Tasks**_ – _**Import**_.
        
        ![Install Certificate...](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0183.png)
        
        Install Certificate...
        
2.  Pick one of the following options and click _**Next**_:
    
    *   _**Automatically select the certificate store based on the type of certificate**_; or
        
    *   _**Place all certificates in the following store**_ and click _**Browse...**_ to pick a folder.
        
        ![X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0184.png)
        
        X.509 Certificate
        
3.  Complete the import by clicking on _**Finish**_.
    
    ![Certificate Import Wizard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0185.png)
    
    Certificate Import Wizard
    

Giving the Devolutions Gateway service read permission on the certificate private key
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#giving-the-devolutions-gateway-service-read-permission-on-the-certificate-private-key)

By default, Devolutions Gateway runs its service using the Network Service account. To use a certificate from the local certificate store, ensure the Network Service account has read permissions on the certificate's private key.

1.  Open the local certificate store and navigate to the certificate.
    
2.  Right-click on the certificate and select _**All Tasks**_ – _**Manage Private Keys**_.
    
    ![All Tasks – Manage Private Keys](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2079.png)
    
    All Tasks – Manage Private Keys
    
3.  Click to add a user name.
    
    ![Add a user name](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2080.png)
    
    Add a user name
    
4.  Write "NETWORK SERVICE" in the object names field then click _**OK**_.
    
    ![Add the NETWORK SERVICE user name](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2081.png)
    
    Add the "NETWORK SERVICE" user name
    
5.  Select the new _**NETWORK SERVICE**_ user name and allow the _**Read**_ permission on it.
    
    ![Allow the Read permission](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2082.png)
    
    Allow the "Read" permission
    
6.  Click _**Apply**_, the click _**OK**_.
    

Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json
------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)

The default location of the `gateway.json` file is in the **%ProgramData%\\Devolutions\\Gateway** directory.

Make sure the file is a valid `.json` by testing it with:

    $Config = ("{0}\Devolutions\Gateway\gateway.json" -F $Env:ProgramData)
    
    Try {
      Get-Content -Path $Config | ConvertFrom-JSON -ErrorAction 'Stop'
    } Catch {
      $PSItem[0].Exception.Message
    }
    

This works with PowerShell 5.1 and later versions (the recommended version to use is PowerShell 7.x).

![Get-Content](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0173.png)

Get-Content

A typical configuration is shown below. Your values may differ, especially the _**Subject Name**_, as that will reflect the domain name Devolutions Gateway responds to. The important values to change are:

*   `TlsCertificateSource` - `System`
    
*   `TlsCertificateSubjectName` - `gateway.ad.it-help.ninja`
    
*   `TlsCertificateStoreName` - `My`
    
*   `TlsCertificateStoreLocation` - `LocalMachine`
    

An example of the entire configuration file:

    {
      "Id": "c912b379-8c34-449d-8ff3-3aa20a9cc3e4",
      "Hostname": "gateway.ad.it-help.ninja",
      "TlsCertificateFile": "server.crt",
      "TlsPrivateKeyFile": "server.key",
      "TlsCertificateSource": "System",
      "TlsCertificateSubjectName": "gateway.ad.it-help.ninja",
      "TlsCertificateStoreName": "My",
      "TlsCertificateStoreLocation": "LocalMachine",
      "ProvisionerPublicKeyFile": "provisioner.pem",
      "Listeners": [\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "https://*:7171",\
          "ExternalUrl": "https://*:7171"\
        },\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "tcp://*:8181",\
          "ExternalUrl": "tcp://*:8181"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

1.  Run the above script.
    
2.  Open `services.msc`.
    
3.  Right-click on _**Devolutions Gateway Service**_ and select _**Restart**_.
    
    ![Restart](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0174.png)
    
    Restart
    
4.  Verify if Devolutions Gateway is running correctly by navigating to `https://{FQDN}:7171/jet/health` (replacing `{FQDN}` with your Gateway DNS address) with a web browser.
    

Configuring Windows certificate store via PowerShell
----------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-powershell)

The Devolutions Gateway can also be configured through PowerShell commands. The [Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/DevolutionsGateway/)
 exposes many commands to configure it. By default, an install of Devolutions Gateway includes the module in the installation directory. Import the module via the following:

    # Import the Module
    Import-Module -Name "C:\Program Files\Devolutions\Gateway\PowerShell\Modules\DevolutionsGateway"
    # View the imported Modules
    Get-Module
    

![Import-Module](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0175.png)

Import-Module

Another method to make the module easily accessible is to install it via the following:

    # Install the DevolutionsGateway module
    Install-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # Update the module if installed via the above method (will not update the bundled version installed with Gateway)
    Update-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # Import the Module
    Import-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # View the imported modules to verify the DevolutionsGateway module is available
    Get-Module
    

![Install-Module](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0176.png)

Install-Module

Once imported, you can see the current configuration via the following command:

    Get-DGatewayConfig
    

![Get-DGatewayConfig](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0177.png)

Get-DGatewayConfig

To tell Devolutions Gateway to use the Windows Store, use the following command:

    # Update the configuration; this will not remove any existing parameters, only configure those defined.
    # Replace the '{FQDN}` example with the fully-qualified DNS name of the Gateway address
    Set-DGatewayConfig -TlsCertificateSource "System" -TlsCertificateSubjectName "{FQDN}" -TlsCertificateStoreLocation "LocalMachine" -TlsCertificateStoreName "My"
    # Display the updated configuration
    Get-DGatewayConfig
    

![Set-DGatewayConfig](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0178.png)

Set-DGatewayConfig

Restart the service for the configuration to take effect.

    Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    

![Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0179.png)

Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'

Verify if Devolutions Gateway is running correctly by navigating to `https://{FQDN}:7171/jet/health` with a web browser.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway side-by-side installation method not found - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway side-by-side installation method not found
==============================================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Solution](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)
    

When installing Devolutions Gateway on the same machine as Devolutions Server (side by side installation), this error can trigger in the installation logs.

Method not found:'Void System.Management.Automation.Runspaces.InitialSessionState.set\_ExecutionPolicy(Microsoft.PowerShell.ExecutionPolicy)'.

Solution
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)

As Devolutions Gateway requires at least PowerShell version 5.1, please update PowerShell to that version to fix the issue. Then start over the Devolutions Gateway installation.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Méthode d'installation côte à côte Devolutions Gateway non trouvée - Documentation Devolutions

Méthode d'installation côte à côte Devolutions Gateway non trouvée
==================================================================

Sur cette page

*   [Solution](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)
    

Lors de l'installation de Devolutions Gateway sur la même machine que Devolutions Server (installation côte à côte), cette erreur peut se déclencher dans les journaux d'installation.

Method not found:'Void System.Management.Automation.Runspaces.InitialSessionState.set\_ExecutionPolicy(Microsoft.PowerShell.ExecutionPolicy)'.

Solution
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)

Comme Devolutions Gateway nécessite au moins la version 5.1 de PowerShell, merci de mettre à jour PowerShell vers cette version pour résoudre le problème. Puis recommencer l'installation de Devolutions Gateway.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Résolution des problèmes de Devolutions Gateway - Documentation Devolutions

Résolution des problèmes de Devolutions Gateway
===============================================

Sur cette page

*   [Vérifier l'état de santé d'un Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)
    
*   [Journal et diagnostics Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs-and-diagnostics)
    *   [Journaux de Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)
        
    *   [Diagnostics Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)
        
*   [Le service échoue à démarrer](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#service-fails-to-start)
    
*   [Compatibilité du certificat](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#certificate-compatibility)
    
*   [Connexion au serveur perdue](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#connection-to-the-server-lost)
    
*   [Problèmes de proxy](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)
    

Cette rubrique couvre des conseils sur la résolution de problèmes de Devolutions Gateway à travers plusieurs produits.

Si vous êtes incapable de télécharger les journaux via le web, vous pouvez aussi les trouver dans le dossier d'installation : `C:\ProgramData\Devolutions\Gateway`.

Vérifier l'état de santé d'un Devolutions Gateway
-------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)

Il est possible de vérifier si une passerelle particulière est active et en bonne santé.

1.  Ouvrir un navigateur web.
    
2.  Dans la barre d'adresse, taper `https://:/jet/health`. Selon la configuration, cela pourrait aussi être `` `http` ``.
    
3.  Appuyer sur Entrée.
    
    ![Health check](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0000_2024_1.png)
    
    Health check
    

Journal et diagnostics Devolutions Gateway
------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs-and-diagnostics)

Si vous avez des difficultés avec une passerelle, ces solutions peuvent faciliter la détection d'erreurs plus apparentes.

1.  Dans l'interface Web de Devolutions Server, accéder à _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
2.  Cliquer sur _**Plus**_ sur le portail désiré.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0001_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
3.  Choisir entre [_**Journaux**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)
     ou [_**Diagnostics**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)
    .
    

### Journaux de Devolutions Gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)

1.  Cliquer sur _**Journaux**_.
    
    ![Logs](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0002_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs
    
2.  Observer les journaux.
    
    ![Logs window](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0006_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs window
    

### Diagnostics Devolutions Gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)

1.  Cliquer sur _**Diagnostics**_.
    
    ![Diagnostics](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0004_2024_1.png)
    
    Diagnostics
    
2.  Observer les statuts.
    
    ![Gateway status](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway status
    

Le service échoue à démarrer
----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#service-fails-to-start)

Si le service ne démarre pas du tout, vérifier si un fichier nommé `boot.stacktrace` existe dans le même répertoire que le fichier de configuration `gateway.json`. Ce fichier peut contenir des informations de diagnostic pertinentes. Contacter notre [équipe d'assistance](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 si vous n'êtes pas en mesure d'identifier la cause de l'échec.

Compatibilité du certificat
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#certificate-compatibility)

Les problèmes liés aux certificats auto-signés manquant un SAN ou un EKU peuvent être résolus en mettant à jour vers la dernière version de Devolutions Gateway.

Il est recommandé de définir l'option `TlsVerifyStrict` sur `true` dans la mesure du possible. Configurer également cette option si vous rencontrez des problèmes de certificat sur macOS et Chrome.

Connexion au serveur perdue
---------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#connection-to-the-server-lost)

Si ce message d'erreur est reçu, s'assurer que le compte de service configuré sur le service Devolutions Gateway peut atteindre le dossier de destination de l'enregistrement et qu'il dispose des permissions requises pour créer les dossiers et fichiers d'enregistrement.

Problèmes de proxy
------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)

Si vous rencontrez des problèmes lors du chargement ou de l'utilisation des entrées Web dans Remote Desktop Manager lorsque Devolutions Gateway est configuré comme un proxy, vérifier les fichiers journaux pour plus de détails:

*   Chemin Windows: `C:\Users\\AppData\Roaming\jetsocat`
    
*   Chemin macOS: `/Users//Library/Application Support/jetsocat`
    

Si le problème persiste, veuillez contacter notre équipe d'assistance client pour obtenir de l'aide à [service@devolutions.net](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 et fournir les fichiers journaux pertinents.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway tunnel connection type - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway tunnel connection type
==========================================

On this page

*   [Listeners](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)
    *   [Allow Rules](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)
        
    *   [Using the Devolutions Gateway Tunnel oustide of Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)
        

The _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ can fulfill similar needs to SSH port forwarding/SSH tunneling, but it requires nothing other than Devolutions Gateway itself. It is useful when using connections that do not have built-in support in Remote Desktop Manager through the Devolutions Gateway. The entry can be found under _**New Entry**_ – _**Session**_ – _**Remote Connections**_.

Devolutions Gateway needs to be set up in the Remote Desktop Manager data source and then configured through [inheritance](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/kb/knowledge-base/inheritance/)
 or on the connection itself. The option is under **_Properties_** – **_Connection_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_VPN/SSH/Gateway_** – **_General_**.

![Tunnel](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0116.png)

Tunnel

Listeners
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#listeners)

If the **_Listener_** is set to 0.0.0.0, it will accept connections from any source within the network. Due to the difficulty in tracking accountability, it is recommended **_NOT_** to do this for multiple security reasons.

*   In almost every scenario, the listener (bind address) should be set to the loopback address (127.0.0.1) from the local machine.
    
*   _**TCP Forward**_: It is the equivalent to port forwarding.
    
*   _**HTTP**_ and _**SOCKS5**_ proxies: These listeners are set up as proxies which makes it possible to use a browser other than Google Chrome. This also means they use a dynamic destination.
    
    Dynamic ports can be used with all three listener types. If the value is 0, it will automatically find an available port.
    

### Allow Rules

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#allow-rules)

The _**HTTP**_ and _**SOCKS5**_ listeners will also make use of the _**Allow Rules**_ to specify authorized destinations, anything not on the allow list will be denied.

_**Target filters**_ can be specified using IP addresses or hostnames. Both can contain wildcards. Each _**Target filter**_ must explicitly specify a destination port. Leaving the default port as '0' will result in an error when attempting to save the filter.

![Default](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0163.png)

Default

#### Examples of valid target filters

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#examples-of-valid-target-filters)

| Target filter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `windjammer.net:80` | Allows HTTP traffic to the hostname windjammer.net. |
| `*.windjammer.net:443` | Allows HTTPS traffic to any subdomain of windjammer.net but not to windjammer.net directly. |
| `192.168.0.*:22` | Allows SSH traffic to any IP address between 192.168.0.0 to 192.168.0.255. |
| `*:3389` | Allows RDP traffic to any endpoint reachable by the Devolutions Gateway. |

You can add multiple _**Target filters**_ to your entry tailored to your intended use of the tunnel. For example, you might add the same hostname several times but with different ports, like 80 and 443, to permit both HTTP and HTTPS traffic.

### Using the Devolutions Gateway Tunnel oustide of Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#using-the-devolutions-gateway-tunnel-oustide-of-remote-desktop-manager)

Once opened, it is possible to use a _**Devolutions Gateway Tunnel**_ from an applicaton that is external to Remote Desktop Manager. You could, for instance, use it with a web browser or any other application that supports the type of proxying (TCP, HTTP, or SOCKS5) that you specified in the connection.

#### Example: Using the tunnel with the cURL command-line tool

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/knowledge-base/gateway-tunnel/#example-using-the-tunnel-with-the-curl-command-line-tool)

You can add your proxy endpoint along with the port specified or the one that was generated by the _**Devolutions Gateway tunnel**_ entry with the -x argument.

    curl -x socks5h://127.0.0.1:65535 windjammer.net
    

If you have set your target filters using hostnames, it is important to ensure that your application does not resolve the hostname before sending it to the tunnel; otherwise, the traffic will be denied. Applications typically have settings to enable or disable this behavior. For example, in the web browser Firefox, you need to enable the **_Proxy DNS when using SOCKS v5_** option in the proxy configuration panel for this scenario to function correctly.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Use Windows certificate store for Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Use Windows certificate store for Devolutions Gateway
=====================================================

On this page

*   [Importing the certificate into the Windows certificate store](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate-into-the-windows-certificate-store)
    *   [Converting an X.509 certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#converting-an-x509-certificate)
        
    *   [Importing the certificate](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate)
        
*   [Giving the Devolutions Gateway service read permission on the certificate private key](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#giving-the-devolutions-gateway-service-read-permission-on-the-certificate-private-key)
    
*   [Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)
    
*   [Configuring Windows certificate store via PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-powershell)
    

If your clients fail to connect with Devolutions Gateway, ensure the certificate contains the entire chain. This certificate chain includes any intermediate certificates. For example: Root Certificate Authority – Secure Certificate Authority – Purchased XYZ Certificate.

It is possible to use the Windows certificate store as a TLS certificate source. Instead of using a file, store and manage your certificates with Windows. As of the time of writing, this functionality is not exposed in the Devolutions Gateway configuration console GUI. To configure, you must either directly modify the gateway.json file or use the Devolutions.PowerShell module.

With the new functionality, a [few additional parameters](https://github.com/Devolutions/devolutions-gateway#configuration)
 are available to configure the source of the certificate.

If you have a previously defined \`TlsCertificateFile\` and/or \`TlsPrivateKeyFile\` configuration, removal is unnecessary as \`TlsCertificateSource\` tells Devolutions Gateway where to search for the certificate.

*   **TlsCertificateSource** (string): Source for the TLS certificate, possible values shown below.
    
    *   **External** (default): Retrieve a certificate stored on the file system. See the options `TlsCertificateFile`, `TlsPrivateKeyFile`, and `TlsPrivateKeyPassword`.
        
    *   **System**: Retrieve the certificate managed by the system certificate store. See the options `TlsCertificateSubjectName`, `TlsCertificateStoreName`, and `TlsCertificateStoreLocation`.
        
*   **TlsCertificateSubjectName** (string): Subject name of the certificate for TLS when using System source.
    
*   **TlsCertificateStoreName** (string): Name of the System Certificate Store to use for TLS (default is My).
    
*   **TlsCertificateStoreLocation** (string): Location of the System Certificate Store to use for TLS, possible values shown below.
    
    *   **CurrentUser** (default)
        
    *   **CurrentService**
        
    *   **LocalMachine**
        

Importing the certificate into the Windows certificate store
------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate-into-the-windows-certificate-store)

First, import your certificate into the Windows certificate store. Windows supports the following certificate formats:

*   X.509 certificate - \*.cer, \*.crt
    
*   Personal Information Exchange - \*.pfx, \*.p12
    
*   Microsoft Serialized certificate Store - \*.sst
    
*   PKCS #7 Certificates - \*.spc, \*.p7b
    

If using the \`External\` method via \`TlsCertificateSource\`, then Devolutions Gateway only supports bundling the public and private key in a PFX (PKCS#12) file. Otherwise, you will need to define the \`TlsPrivateKeyFile\` parameter as well.

### Converting an X.509 certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#converting-an-x509-certificate)

Devolutions Gateway requires a private key with the TLS certificate; therefore, you may need to combine the public key with its private key. Here are two methods: [Remote Desktop Manager](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-remote-desktop-manager)
 and the built-in [Windows utility `certutil`](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-the-windows-certutil-utility)
.

#### Using Remote Desktop Manager

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-remote-desktop-manager)

The _**X.509 Certificate**_ entry can be used to import said certificate and export it in several different formats, including PFX.

1.  In Remote Desktop Manager click on _**New Entry**_ – _**Credential Management**_ – _**General**_ – _**X.509 Certificate**_.
    
    ![X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0180.png)
    
    X.509 Certificate
    
2.  Select the certificate and click _**Open**_.
    
    ![Open](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0164.png)
    
    Open
    
3.  Click _**Next**_.
    
    ![Next](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0165.png)
    
    Next
    
4.  Click on the ellipsis and select the _**Private key**_.
    
    ![Ellipsis button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0166.png)
    
    Ellipsis button
    
5.  Click on _**Open**_.
    
    ![KEY file](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0181.png)
    
    KEY file
    
    The **_Private key_** must be in the \`.key\` extension.
    
6.  Click _**Finish**_.
    
    ![Finish](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0168.png)
    
    Finish
    
7.  Fill in the information, then click _**Add**_.
    
    ![Information fields](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0167.png)
    
    Information fields
    
8.  Select the entry and click _**Save Certificate As**_ (also available in the right-click context menu).
    
    ![Save Certificate As](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0186.png)
    
    Save Certificate As
    
9.  In the _**Export Format**_ field choose _**Personal Information Exchange (pfx)**_.
    
10.  Choose where the file will be saved by clicking on the ellipsis.
    
11.  Enter a strong password, then click _**Export**_.
    
    ![Export X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0182.png)
    
    Export X.509 Certificate
    

#### Using the Windows certutil utility

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#using-the-windows-certutil-utility)

Use the built-in Windows `certutil` utility to combine a certificate (`.crt` or `.cer`) file and its private key (`.key`). Both files need to have the same name. `certutil -MergePFX file.crt file.pfx`

![certutil](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0169.png)

certutil

### Importing the certificate

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#importing-the-certificate)

After acquiring the certificate and certificate private key file, import it into Windows.

1.  Install the certificate:
    
    *   If Windows auto-detects the certificate, double-click it and choose _**Install Certificate...**_; or
        
    *   Open `certmgr.msc` to the intended store location (`LocalMachine` or `CurrentUser`), right-click on the wanted location (ex: _**Personal/Certificates**_) and choose _**All Tasks**_ – _**Import**_.
        
        ![Install Certificate...](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0183.png)
        
        Install Certificate...
        
2.  Pick one of the following options and click _**Next**_:
    
    *   _**Automatically select the certificate store based on the type of certificate**_; or
        
    *   _**Place all certificates in the following store**_ and click _**Browse...**_ to pick a folder.
        
        ![X.509 Certificate](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0184.png)
        
        X.509 Certificate
        
3.  Complete the import by clicking on _**Finish**_.
    
    ![Certificate Import Wizard](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0185.png)
    
    Certificate Import Wizard
    

Giving the Devolutions Gateway service read permission on the certificate private key
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#giving-the-devolutions-gateway-service-read-permission-on-the-certificate-private-key)

By default, Devolutions Gateway runs its service using the Network Service account. To use a certificate from the local certificate store, ensure the Network Service account has read permissions on the certificate's private key.

1.  Open the local certificate store and navigate to the certificate.
    
2.  Right-click on the certificate and select _**All Tasks**_ – _**Manage Private Keys**_.
    
    ![All Tasks – Manage Private Keys](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2079.png)
    
    All Tasks – Manage Private Keys
    
3.  Click to add a user name.
    
    ![Add a user name](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2080.png)
    
    Add a user name
    
4.  Write "NETWORK SERVICE" in the object names field then click _**OK**_.
    
    ![Add the NETWORK SERVICE user name](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2081.png)
    
    Add the "NETWORK SERVICE" user name
    
5.  Select the new _**NETWORK SERVICE**_ user name and allow the _**Read**_ permission on it.
    
    ![Allow the Read permission](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/INTERFACE2082.png)
    
    Allow the "Read" permission
    
6.  Click _**Apply**_, the click _**OK**_.
    

Configuring Windows certificate store via gateway.json
------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-gatewayjson)

The default location of the `gateway.json` file is in the **%ProgramData%\\Devolutions\\Gateway** directory.

Make sure the file is a valid `.json` by testing it with:

    $Config = ("{0}\Devolutions\Gateway\gateway.json" -F $Env:ProgramData)
    
    Try {
      Get-Content -Path $Config | ConvertFrom-JSON -ErrorAction 'Stop'
    } Catch {
      $PSItem[0].Exception.Message
    }
    

This works with PowerShell 5.1 and later versions (the recommended version to use is PowerShell 7.x).

![Get-Content](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0173.png)

Get-Content

A typical configuration is shown below. Your values may differ, especially the _**Subject Name**_, as that will reflect the domain name Devolutions Gateway responds to. The important values to change are:

*   `TlsCertificateSource` - `System`
    
*   `TlsCertificateSubjectName` - `gateway.ad.it-help.ninja`
    
*   `TlsCertificateStoreName` - `My`
    
*   `TlsCertificateStoreLocation` - `LocalMachine`
    

An example of the entire configuration file:

    {
      "Id": "c912b379-8c34-449d-8ff3-3aa20a9cc3e4",
      "Hostname": "gateway.ad.it-help.ninja",
      "TlsCertificateFile": "server.crt",
      "TlsPrivateKeyFile": "server.key",
      "TlsCertificateSource": "System",
      "TlsCertificateSubjectName": "gateway.ad.it-help.ninja",
      "TlsCertificateStoreName": "My",
      "TlsCertificateStoreLocation": "LocalMachine",
      "ProvisionerPublicKeyFile": "provisioner.pem",
      "Listeners": [\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "https://*:7171",\
          "ExternalUrl": "https://*:7171"\
        },\
        {\
          "InternalUrl": "tcp://*:8181",\
          "ExternalUrl": "tcp://*:8181"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

1.  Run the above script.
    
2.  Open `services.msc`.
    
3.  Right-click on _**Devolutions Gateway Service**_ and select _**Restart**_.
    
    ![Restart](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0174.png)
    
    Restart
    
4.  Verify if Devolutions Gateway is running correctly by navigating to `https://{FQDN}:7171/jet/health` (replacing `{FQDN}` with your Gateway DNS address) with a web browser.
    

Configuring Windows certificate store via PowerShell
----------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/how-to-articles/use-windows-certificate-store/#configuring-windows-certificate-store-via-powershell)

The Devolutions Gateway can also be configured through PowerShell commands. The [Devolutions Gateway PowerShell module](https://www.powershellgallery.com/packages/DevolutionsGateway/)
 exposes many commands to configure it. By default, an install of Devolutions Gateway includes the module in the installation directory. Import the module via the following:

    # Import the Module
    Import-Module -Name "C:\Program Files\Devolutions\Gateway\PowerShell\Modules\DevolutionsGateway"
    # View the imported Modules
    Get-Module
    

![Import-Module](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0175.png)

Import-Module

Another method to make the module easily accessible is to install it via the following:

    # Install the DevolutionsGateway module
    Install-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # Update the module if installed via the above method (will not update the bundled version installed with Gateway)
    Update-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # Import the Module
    Import-Module -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    # View the imported modules to verify the DevolutionsGateway module is available
    Get-Module
    

![Install-Module](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0176.png)

Install-Module

Once imported, you can see the current configuration via the following command:

    Get-DGatewayConfig
    

![Get-DGatewayConfig](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0177.png)

Get-DGatewayConfig

To tell Devolutions Gateway to use the Windows Store, use the following command:

    # Update the configuration; this will not remove any existing parameters, only configure those defined.
    # Replace the '{FQDN}` example with the fully-qualified DNS name of the Gateway address
    Set-DGatewayConfig -TlsCertificateSource "System" -TlsCertificateSubjectName "{FQDN}" -TlsCertificateStoreLocation "LocalMachine" -TlsCertificateStoreName "My"
    # Display the updated configuration
    Get-DGatewayConfig
    

![Set-DGatewayConfig](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0178.png)

Set-DGatewayConfig

Restart the service for the configuration to take effect.

    Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'
    

![Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB0179.png)

Restart-Service -Name 'DevolutionsGateway'

Verify if Devolutions Gateway is running correctly by navigating to `https://{FQDN}:7171/jet/health` with a web browser.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway troubleshooting - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway troubleshooting
===================================

Auf dieser Seite

*   [Verify the health of a gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)

*   [Proxy issues](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)
    

This topic covers tips about troubleshooting Devolutions Gateway across multiple products.

If you are unable to download the logs from the web, you can also find them in the installation folder: `C:\ProgramData\Devolutions\Gateway`.

Verify the health of a gateway
------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)

It is possible to check if a particular gateway is alive and healthy.

1.  Open a web browser.
    
2.  In the address bar type `https://&lt;gateway.url&gt;:&lt;external port&gt;/jet/health`. Depending on the setup, it could also be `` `http` ``.
    
3.  Press Enter.
    
    ![Health check](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0000_2024_1.png)
    
    Health check
    

Devolutions Gateway Logs and diagnostics
----------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs-and-diagnostics)

If you are having trouble with a gateway, these solutions can make it easier to find more apparent errors.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web UI, go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
2.  Click _**More**_ on the desired gateway.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0001_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
3.  Choose between [_**Logs**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)
     or [_**Diagnostics**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)
    .
    

### Devolutions Gateway Logs

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)

1.  Click on _**Logs**_.
    
    ![Logs](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0002_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs
    
2.  Observe the logs.
    
    ![Logs window](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0006_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs window
    

### Devolutions Gateway Diagnostics

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)

1.  Click on _**Diagnostics**_.
    
    ![Diagnostics](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0004_2024_1.png)
    
    Diagnostics
    
2.  Observe the statuses.
    
    ![Gateway status](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway status
    

Service fails to start
----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#service-fails-to-start)

If the service does not start at all, verify whether a file named `boot.stacktrace` exists in the same directory as the `gateway.json` configuration file. This file may contain relevant diagnostic information. Contact our [support team](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 if you are not able to identify the cause of the failure.

Certificate compatibility
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#certificate-compatibility)

Issues related to self-signed certificates missing a SAN or an EKU can be resolved by updating to the latest version of Devolutions Gateway.

It is recommended to set the `TlsVerifyStrict` option as `true` whenever possible. You should also configure this option if you encounter certificate issues on macOS and Chrome.

Connection to the server lost
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#connection-to-the-server-lost)

If you receive this error message, make sure that the service account configured on the Devolutions Gateway service can reach the recording destination folder and has the required permissions to create the recording folders and files.

Proxy issues
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)

If you experience problems loading or using web entries in Remote Desktop Manager when Devolutions Gateway is configured as a proxy, check the log files for additional details:

*   Windows path: `C:\Users\&lt;user&gt;\AppData\Roaming\jetsocat`
    
*   macOS path: `/Users/&lt;user&gt;/Library/Application Support/jetsocat`
    

If the issue persists, please contact our customer support team for assistance at [service@devolutions.net](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 and provide the relevant log files.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway recording path - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway recording path
==================================

This topic serves as a reference for general information on Devolutions Gateway recording.

The recording format is WebM and the file size is around 15 kb/s, depending on compression.

The recording path can be set in the Devolutions Server Console only.

![Recording path in the Devolutions Server Console](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLSCONSOLE4010_2024_2.png)

Recording path in the Devolutions Server Console

Here are some important considerations:

*   If the new path is set to a network location, like a shared folder or a UNC path, be aware that this may impact network traffic, both incoming and outgoing.
    
*   Confirm that the account operating the gateway service has the necessary permissions to access both the gateway files and the file share.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Problèmes de certificat TLS invalide pour l'enregistrement de la session via Devolutions Gateway - Documentation Devolutions

Problèmes de certificat TLS invalide pour l'enregistrement de la session via Devolutions Gateway
================================================================================================

Si vous rencontrez des problèmes avec l'enregistrement de session via Devolutions Gateway, cela peut être dû à un certificat TLS invalide. Voici plusieurs raisons pour lesquelles un certificat TLS peut être considéré comme invalide. Voici les causes les plus courantes :

*   **Certificat mal configuré** : Configuration incorrecte ou installation du certificat TLS.
    
*   **Inadéquation du domaine** : Le certificat est délivré pour un domaine différent (par exemple, certificat délivré pour _exemple.loc_ mais l'adresse de destination de l'hôte est _pas-exemple.loc_).
    
*   **Rupture dans la chaîne de confiance** : L'identité de l'émetteur du certificat ne peut pas être vérifiée.
    
*   **Date/heure incorrecte sur la machine cliente** : Si la date/heure locale sur la machine cliente est incorrecte, le certificat peut être considéré comme expiré s'il dépasse la date d'expiration du certificat.
    
*   **Structure de certificat brisée** : Le certificat a une signature numérique invalide ou d'autres problèmes structurels.
    
*   **Algorithme de hachage obsolète** : Le certificat utilise uniquement l'algorithme de hachage SHA-1, qui est obsolète et n'est plus considéré comme sûr.
    
*   **Certificat révoqué** : Le certificat a été révoqué par l'autorité de délivrance.
    
*   **Certificat auto-signé et Sophos** : Lors de l'utilisation d'un certificat auto-signé, si le client utilise Sophos, le certificat peut être remplacé par un certificat non approuvé, contournant l'option d'autoriser les certificats auto-signés par Remote Desktop Manager.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Invalid TLS certificate issues for session recording via Devolutions Gateway - Devolutions Documentation

Invalid TLS certificate issues for session recording via Devolutions Gateway
============================================================================

If you encounter issues with session recording via Devolutions Gateway, it may be due to an invalid TLS certificate. There are several reasons why a TLS certificate could be considered invalid. Here are the most common causes:

*   **Misconfigured certificate**: Incorrect setup or installation of the TLS certificate.
    
*   **Domain mismatch**: The certificate is issued for a different domain (e.g., certificate issued for _example.loc_ but the host destination address is _not-example.loc_).
    
*   **Break in the chain of trust**: The certificate issuer's identity cannot be verified.
    
*   **Incorrect date/time on client machine**: If the local date/time on the client machine is incorrect, the certificate may be considered expired if it falls past the certificate's expiration date.
    
*   **Broken certificate structure**: The certificate has an invalid digital signature or other structural issues.
    
*   **Outdated hashing algorithm**: The certificate uses only the SHA-1 hash algorithm, which is outdated and no longer considered secure.
    
*   **Revoked certificate**: The certificate has been revoked by the issuing authority.
    
*   **Self-signed certificate and Sophos**: When using a self-signed certificate, if the client is using Sophos, the certificate may be replaced by an untrusted one, bypassing the option to allow self-signed certificates by Remote Desktop Manager.
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway side-by-side installation method not found - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway side-by-side installation method not found
==============================================================

On this page

*   [Solution](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)
    

When installing Devolutions Gateway on the same machine as Devolutions Server (side by side installation), this error can trigger in the installation logs.

Method not found:'Void System.Management.Automation.Runspaces.InitialSessionState.set\_ExecutionPolicy(Microsoft.PowerShell.ExecutionPolicy)'.

Solution
--------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/install-dgw-method-not-found/#solution)

As Devolutions Gateway requires at least PowerShell version 5.1, please update PowerShell to that version to fix the issue. Then start over the Devolutions Gateway installation.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Client web RDP ne s'affiche pas - Documentation Devolutions

Client web RDP ne s'affiche pas
===============================

Sur cette page

*   [Solutions](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#solutions)
    *   [Licences](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#licenses)
        
    *   [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#devolutions-gateway)
        
    *   [Autorisations de voir le mot de passe](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#view-password-permission)
        

Si vous ne parvenez pas à lancer le client web RDP dans l'interface web de Devolutions Server, vérifier si vous avez les exigences nécessaires en utilisant les solutions ci-dessous.

Solutions
---------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#solutions)

### Licences

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#licenses)

Une clé de licence qui inclut Devolutions Gateway doit être attribuée à l'utilisateur. Si vous n'avez pas cette clé, le bouton _**Ouvrir dans le navigateur**_, qui vous permet d'ouvrir l'entrée RDP dans un client web, n'apparaîtra pas.

![Open in browser](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6055_2025_3.png)

Open in browser

### Devolutions Gateway

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#devolutions-gateway)

Devolutions Gateway est requis pour ouvrir une session RDP dans le client web de Devolutions Server. Si vous avez bien une Gateway installée, vérifier sa [configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/server/server-configuration/)
.

### Autorisations de voir le mot de passe

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/rdp-web-client-not-showing/#view-password-permission)

Avoir l'_**autorisation de voir le mot de passe**_ pour lancer la session RDP.

Pour vérifier si ce droit vous a été octroyé, sélectionner votre entrée dans l'interface web de Devolutions Server, puis cliquer sur l'onglet _**Permissions**_. Si vous voyez _**Autorisée**_ sous la permission _**Voir mot de passe**_, vous avez les permissions appropriées. Si vous voyez _**Non autorisée**_, vous n'avez pas ce droit. Si vous pensez que vous devriez l'avoir, contacter votre administrateur.

![View password permission](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DVLS6057_2025_3.png)

View password permission

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Devolutions Gateway troubleshooting - Devolutions Documentation

Devolutions Gateway troubleshooting
===================================

On this page

*   [Verify the health of a gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)
    
*   [Devolutions Gateway Logs and diagnostics](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs-and-diagnostics)
    *   [Devolutions Gateway Logs](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)
        
    *   [Devolutions Gateway Diagnostics](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)
        
*   [Service fails to start](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#service-fails-to-start)
    
*   [Certificate compatibility](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#certificate-compatibility)
    
*   [Connection to the server lost](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#connection-to-the-server-lost)
    
*   [Proxy issues](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)
    

This topic covers tips about troubleshooting Devolutions Gateway across multiple products.

If you are unable to download the logs from the web, you can also find them in the installation folder: `C:\ProgramData\Devolutions\Gateway`.

Verify the health of a gateway
------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#verify-the-health-of-a-gateway)

It is possible to check if a particular gateway is alive and healthy.

1.  Open a web browser.
    
2.  In the address bar type `https://<gateway.url>:<external port>/jet/health`. Depending on the setup, it could also be `` `http` ``.
    
3.  Press Enter.
    
    ![Health check](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0000_2024_1.png)
    
    Health check
    

Devolutions Gateway Logs and diagnostics
----------------------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs-and-diagnostics)

If you are having trouble with a gateway, these solutions can make it easier to find more apparent errors.

1.  In the Devolutions Server web UI, go to _**Administration**_ – _**Devolutions Gateway**_.
    
2.  Click _**More**_ on the desired gateway.
    
    ![More button](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0001_2024_1.png)
    
    More button
    
3.  Choose between [_**Logs**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)
     or [_**Diagnostics**_](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)
    .
    

### Devolutions Gateway Logs

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-logs)

1.  Click on _**Logs**_.
    
    ![Logs](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0002_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs
    
2.  Observe the logs.
    
    ![Logs window](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0006_2024_1.png)
    
    Logs window
    

### Devolutions Gateway Diagnostics

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#devolutions-gateway-diagnostics)

1.  Click on _**Diagnostics**_.
    
    ![Diagnostics](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0004_2024_1.png)
    
    Diagnostics
    
2.  Observe the statuses.
    
    ![Gateway status](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/DGW0005_2024_1.png)
    
    Gateway status
    

Service fails to start
----------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#service-fails-to-start)

If the service does not start at all, verify whether a file named `boot.stacktrace` exists in the same directory as the `gateway.json` configuration file. This file may contain relevant diagnostic information. Contact our [support team](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 if you are not able to identify the cause of the failure.

Certificate compatibility
-------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#certificate-compatibility)

Issues related to self-signed certificates missing a SAN or an EKU can be resolved by updating to the latest version of Devolutions Gateway.

It is recommended to set the `TlsVerifyStrict` option as `true` whenever possible. You should also configure this option if you encounter certificate issues on macOS and Chrome.

Connection to the server lost
-----------------------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#connection-to-the-server-lost)

If you receive this error message, make sure that the service account configured on the Devolutions Gateway service can reach the recording destination folder and has the required permissions to create the recording folders and files.

Proxy issues
------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/kb/troubleshooting-articles/gateway-troubleshooting/#proxy-issues)

If you experience problems loading or using web entries in Remote Desktop Manager when Devolutions Gateway is configured as a proxy, check the log files for additional details:

*   Windows path: `C:\Users\<user>\AppData\Roaming\jetsocat`
    
*   macOS path: `/Users/<user>/Library/Application Support/jetsocat`
    

If the issue persists, please contact our customer support team for assistance at [service@devolutions.net](mailto:service@devolutions.net)
 and provide the relevant log files.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)
