# Workforce password management package - Devolutions Documentation

Workforce password management package
=====================================

The [**Workforce password management**](https://devolutions.net/solutions/#workforce-password-management)
 package simplifies credential management across teams and devices. Designed for business users and non-technical staff, it provides secure password storage, controlled sharing, and authentication policy enforcement while integrating with single sign-on and multiple platforms. Follow this checklist to set up your solutions securely and efficiently:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. Data sources are at the heart of Devolutions' ecosystem.<br><br>Discover the key differences between self-hosting and cloud-hosting in this blog article: [Decoding self-hosting vs. cloud-hosting](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |

### Companion tools

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/workforce-password-management-package/#companion-tools)

 that bring together Devolutions Hub Business and Devolutions Server into a single, centralized, cloud-based location. As for [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/)

# Forfait de Démarrage - Documentation Devolutions

Forfait de Démarrage
====================

Le **Forfait de Démarrage** octroie des fonctionnalités de mots de passe, accès à distance, connexion à distance, et gestion des accès privilégiés pour des équipes allant jusqu'à 5 utilisateurs. Profiter de toutes les solutions et outils de Devolutions—sans restrictions de fonctionnalités ou mises à niveau cachées.

[Contacter notre département des ventes](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 si vous souhaitez dépasser la limite de 5 utilisateurs.

La liste de contrôle ci-dessous contient toutes les étapes pour configurer correctement vos solutions :

| LISTE DE CONTRÔLE | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Étape 1 – Commencer avec une source de données**<br><br>*   Basé sur le nuage : [Créer un Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Auto-hébergé : [Créer une instance de Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Créer et configurer une source de données. Les sources de données sont au cœur de l'écosystème Devolutions.<br><br>Découvrir les principales différences entre l'hébergement local et l'hébergement sur le nuage dans cet article de blog : [Décoder l'auto-hébergement vs l'hébergement sur le nuage](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Étape 2 – Enregistrer une licence**<br><br>*   [Dans Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [Dans Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Gérez les licences en stockant leurs clés dans soit Devolutions Server, soit Devolutions Hub. |
| **Étape 3 – Installer Devolutions Gateway**<br><br>*   [Installation et configuration de Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/getting-started/) | [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/)<br> fournit un accès juste-à-temps (connexion JAT) autorisé aux ressources dans des réseaux segmentés, augmentant ainsi la sécurité. |
| **Étape 4 – Commencer avec Remote Desktop Manager**<br><br>*   [Liste de contrôle Remote Desktop Manager pour les entreprises](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/) | L'application Remote Desktop Manager est utilisée pour gérer et centraliser les technologies d'accès à distance, les mots de passe privilégiés, les documents et les informations partagées. |
| **Étape 5 – Commencer avec Devolutions PAM**<br><br>*   [Pour Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/pam/server/getting-started/)<br>    <br>*   [Pour Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/pam/hub/pam-service/) | Devolutions PAM est une solution de gestion des accès privilégiés robuste, facile à déployer et abordable qui équilibre productivité et sécurité. |

 apportent des fonctionnalités supplémentaires aux solutions principales de Devolutions, telles que l'injection des identifiants, la prise en charge de PowerShell, la messagerie sécurisée, et bien plus encore.

# Remote desktop management and IT operations package - Devolutions Documentation

Remote desktop management and IT operations package
===================================================

The [**Remote desktop management and IT operations**](https://devolutions.net/solutions/#remote-connection-management)
 package provides IT professionals, system administrators, and helpdesk technicians with a centralized platform for managing remote connections and IT infrastructure. It allows organizations to manage remote access, apply security policies, and standardize workflows across different environments.

Follow this checklist to set up your solutions:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. Data sources are at the heart of Devolutions' ecosystem.<br><br>Discover the key differences between self-hosting and cloud-hosting in this blog article: [Decoding self-hosting vs. cloud-hosting](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |
| **Step 3 – Install Devolutions Gateway**<br><br>*   [Devolutions Gateway installation and configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/) | [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/)<br> provides authorized just-in-time (JIT) access to resources in segmented networks, thus increasing security. |
| **Step 4 – Get started with Remote Desktop Manager**<br><br>*   [Remote Desktop Manager checklist for enterprises](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/) | The Remote Desktop Manager application is used to manage and centralize remote access technologies, privileged passwords, documents, and shared information. |

### Companion tools

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/remote-connection-and-it-management-package/#companion-tools)

[Companion tools](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/#companion-tools)
 bring additional features to Devolutions’ main solutions, such as credential brokering, PowerShell support, secure messaging, and much more.

#### Get started with Devolutions Workspace

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/remote-connection-and-it-management-package/#get-started-with-devolutions-workspace)

The Workspace app are [applications](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/)
 that bring together Devolutions Hub Business and Devolutions Server into a single, centralized, cloud-based location. As for [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/)
, it is a free browser plugin to be used in conjunction with Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub for secure password injection into websites.

*   [Workspace app](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/)
    
*   [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/)
    

#### Get started with Devolutions Launcher

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/remote-connection-and-it-management-package/#get-started-with-devolutions-launcher)

Devolutions Launcher is a companion tool for Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub. It can launch multiple remote sessions simultaneously while giving system administrators full control. Devolutions Launcher is only available for Windows.

*   [With Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/)
    
*   [With Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/)

# Security advisories - Devolutions Documentation

Security advisories
===================

On this page

*   [CVSS](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/security-advisories/#cvss)
    
*   [CVE](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/security-advisories/#cve)
    

_**Security Advisories**_ for all our products are available for consultation on our [Devolutions website](https://devolutions.net/security/advisories)
 It is a list to inform our users that a security vulnerability in our products was found. It will include remediation and workarounds, the severity level score from the [Common Vulnerability Scoring System](https://www.first.org/cvss/)
 (CVSS), and the [Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures](https://cve.mitre.org/index.html)
 (CVE) number. [Subscribe](https://devolutions.net/security/advisories)
 to receive our latest security advisories by email.

CVSS
----

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/security-advisories/#cvss)

![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4755.png)

The CVSS provides a way to capture the principal characteristics of a vulnerability and produce a numerical score reflecting its severity. The numerical score can then be translated into a qualitative representation (such as low, medium, high, and critical) to help organizations properly assess and prioritize their vulnerability management processes.

For more details and a description of the various equation components, please visit the [CVSS](https://www.first.org/cvss/)
 website.

CVE
---

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/security-advisories/#cve)

![](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/docs/docs_en_kb_KB4756.png)

The CVE mission program is to identify, define, and catalog publicly disclosed cybersecurity vulnerabilities. There is one CVE Record for each vulnerability in the catalog. The vulnerabilities are discovered then assigned and published by organizations from around the world that have partnered with the CVE Program. Partners publish CVE Records to communicate consistent descriptions of vulnerabilities. Information technology and cybersecurity professionals use CVE Records to ensure they are discussing the same issue and to coordinate their efforts to prioritize and address the vulnerabilities. It is a list of publicly disclosed computer security flaws. When someone refers to a CVE, it is a security flaw that has been assigned a CVE ID number.

For more details, please visit the [CVE](https://cve.mitre.org/)
 website.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# Remote access management package - Devolutions Documentation

Remote access management package
================================

The [**Remote access management**](https://devolutions.net/solutions/#remote-access-management)
 package provides a secure way to grant just-in-time (JIT) access to external users, vendors, and third-party IT professionals. It allows organizations to replace traditional VPNs with a more controlled alternative, enforce authentication measures such as MFA, and monitor remote connections without exposing their networks.

Follow the checklist below to get started:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. | **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |
| **Step 3 – Install Devolutions Gateway**<br><br>*   [Devolutions Gateway installation and configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/) | [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/)<br> provides authorized just-in-time (JIT) access to resources in segmented networks, thus increasing security. |
| **Step 4 – Get started with Devolutions Launcher**<br><br>*   [With Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/)<br>    <br>*   [With Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/devolutions-ecosystem/launcher/) | Devolutions Launcher is a companion tool for Devolutions Server and Devolutions Hub. It can launch multiple remote sessions simultaneously while giving system administrators full control. Devolutions Launcher is only available for Windows. |

# Securely send a file to our team - Devolutions Documentation

Securely send a file to our team
================================

To protect your information, we are using a third-party provider of a secure file exchange service, namely Sharefile.

To send us a file, visit [Sharefile](https://devolutions.sharefile.com/filedrop)
, fill in your basic information, and you will be able to upload file(s). These files are not accessible to all Devolutions employees, only to our customer support team.

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Privileged access management package - Devolutions Documentation

Privileged access management package
====================================

The [**Privileged access management**](https://devolutions.net/solutions/#privileged-access-management)
 package helps secure and manage administrative credentials by enforcing access controls and applying the principle of least privilege. It allows organizations to restrict access to critical resources, automate password rotation, and grant temporary privilege elevation when needed.

The checklist below contains all the steps to set up your solutions properly:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. Data sources are at the heart of Devolutions' ecosystem.<br><br>Discover the key differences between self-hosting and cloud-hosting in this blog article: [Decoding self-hosting vs. cloud-hosting](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |
| **Step 3 – Install Devolutions Gateway**<br><br>*   [Devolutions Gateway installation and configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/) | [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/)<br> provides authorized just-in-time (JIT) access to resources in segmented networks, thus increasing security. |
| **Step 4 – Get started with Remote Desktop Manager**<br><br>*   [Remote Desktop Manager checklist for enterprises](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/) | The Remote Desktop Manager application is used to manage and centralize remote access technologies, privileged passwords, documents, and shared information. |
| **Step 5 – Get started with Devolutions PAM**<br><br>*   [For Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/server/getting-started/)<br>    <br>*   [For Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/pam-service/) | Devolutions PAM is a robust, easy-to-deploy, and affordable privileged access management solution that balances productivity and security. |

# Starter Pack - Devolutions Documentation

Starter Pack
============

The **Starter Pack** grants password, remote access, remote connection, and privileged access management features for teams of up to 5 users. Leverage all of Devolutions’ solutions and tools—no feature restrictions or hidden upgrades.

[Contact our sales department](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 if you wish to go over the limit of 5 users.

The checklist below contains all the steps to set up your solutions properly:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. # Customer support - Devolutions Documentation

Customer support
================

Phone and chat hours: Monday to Friday 7:30 a.m. to 6:00 p.m. EDT

Languages: English, Français, Deutsch

Email: [service@devolutions.net](mailto:service@devolutions.net)

Forum: [https://forum.devolutions.net](https://forum.devolutions.net/)

Phone: +1 844 463.0419

### Support plans

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/technical-support/#support-plans)

Subscribers of a paid support plan receive an email address and a plan ID. You should send your support requests to the appropriate email address and provide your plan ID in the subject line.

The level of support provided, as well as the priority assigned to customer’s support requests, will depend on the specific support plan selected or purchased, and on the severity level of the issue reported.

The table below outlines the various support plans offered by Devolutions, each plan defining a distinct scope of customer support and technical assistance:

|     | Standard plan | Extended plan | Premium plan |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Support level priority** | Normal | High | Highest |
| **24/7 access to our community forum, documentation, and** **Devolutions Academy** | X   | X   | X   |
| **Online community forum support** | X   | X   | X   |
| **Email support** | X   | X   | X   |
| **Live chat support** | X   | X   | X   |
| **Phone support** |     | X   | X   |
| **24/7 online community forum and email support** |     |     | X   |
| **Dedicated customer success manager** |     |     | X   |
| **Consulting, security guidance, and training (6 hours per year)** |     |     | X   |

For more information, consult our full [Support Services Addendum](https://devolutions.net/legal/customer-agreements/)
.

# Integration levels - Devolutions Documentation

Integration levels
==================

On this page

*   [Integration level](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level)
    *   [Integration level 1 - High support](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-1-high-support)
        
    *   [Integration level 2 - Moderate support](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-2-moderate-support)
        
    *   [Integration level 3 - Limited support](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-3-limited-support)
        
    *   [Data sources](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#data-sources)
        
    *   [Sessions](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#sessions)
        
    *   [Credential management](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#credential-management)
        

Devolutions integrates a wide array of technologies and third-party software. Some session types such as RDP and SSH, are core features of Remote Desktop Manager and are used by hundreds of thousands of our users. We also integrate other types that are much less popular; those are typically added at the request of users on our forum and are maintained on a best effort basis.

The purpose of this document is to describe the level of maintenance and support you can expect from Devolutions for the sessions we integrate. The classification is based on a number of factors such as:

*   The amount of control we have on the integration
    
*   Whether the integration is a preview, an addon or is deprecated
    
*   The popularity of the types in our user base
    

**By default, session types that are not explicitly listed fall in Integration level 2.**

Integration level
-----------------

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level)

### **Integration level 1 - High support**

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-1-high-support)

This tier reflects our highest ability and commitment to resolve problems. This tier includes sessions based on popular and standardized protocols, as well as services developed by Devolutions directly. The session types most popular with our users are typically placed in this category.

### Integration level 2 - Moderate support

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-2-moderate-support)

This tier includes integrations where we have a moderate level of control. This typically includes integration based on an API or an SDK.

### Integration level 3 - Limited support

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#integration-level-3-limited-support)

Sessions in this tier are supported on a best effort basis. The following sessions fall under this tier:

*   Addons
    
*   Deprecated entries
    

Sessions that are integrated by launching an external program from the command line fall in this tier, as options with this type integrations are the most limited. Types with very low usage levels may also be placed in this category.

The following tables lists the tiers for data sources, sessions, and credential management types.

### Data sources

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#data-sources)

| Integration level | Data sources |
| --- | --- |
| **Integration level 1** | Devolutions Server, Devolutions Hub Business, SQL Server, Azure SQL, SQLite |
| **Integration level 2** | CyberArk, XML |
| **Integration level 3** | _**Deprecated data sources**_  <br>Google Drive, Dropbox |

### Sessions

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#sessions)

| Integration level | Session types |
| --- | --- |
| **Integration level 1** | RDP, SSH (SSH Tunnel, SCP, SFTP, SSH port forward), Telnet, Web browser, VNC (FreeVNC, IronVNC), FTP, Active Directory dashboard, Apple Remote Desktop, Microsoft Entra ID dashboard, Powershell, Devolutions Gateway |
| **Integration level 2** | Apple Remote Management, AWS dashboard, BeyondTrust, CyberArk (SIA, PSM), Citrix, DameWare Mini Remote Control, Dell iDRAC, DeskRoll, Google Workspace, HP iLO, IBM 5250, LogMeIn, Microtik Winbox, Microsoft Hyper-V dashboard, OpenVPN, Proxmox dashboard, Proxy Tunnel, RD Gateway console, Serial port, Supremo, TN3270, VMware dashboard, VMware remote console (VMRC), Windows Admin Center |
| **Integration level 3** | AnyDesk, ISL Light, MobaXterm, Nice DCV, Oracle Virtualbox, Radmin, RustDesk, Teamviewer, VMWare (Player, Workstation, vSphere), VNC (UltraVNC), XWindow  <br>  <br>_**Addons**_  <br>2XClient, Ammyy Admin, Anyplace Control, AWRC Pro, Axel Viewer, Barracuda NG Firewall, BeyondTrust Representative Console, Bitvise SSH Client, Check Point Smart Console, Cisco ASDM, Citrix NetScaler, Database .Net, Db Visualizer, DBeaver, Ericom Blaze Client, FastViewer, FlashFXP, FortiClient VPN, GateProtect Firewall Administration Client, HeidiSQL, HP Integrated Lights Out (iLO Application), IBM i Access, IBM Personal Communications, Impero Guest, Iperius Remote, Java Web Start, MS Telnet, MySQL GUI Tools, MySQLWorkbench, Navicat Premium, NetSupport Manager, NoMachine, NX Client, PenguiNet SSH client, PgAdmin 4, PowerTerm Pro, Proxy Networks - Proxy Master, RemoteAssistant365, Royal TS, RVTools, Sandboxie, SAP Frontend Server (SAP GUI), SAP Hana Studio, SAP MaxDB Database Studio, SAP NetWeaver, SCCM 2012 Remote Control, SecureCRT, SecureFX, SimpleHelp, SmartFTP, Splashtop, Splunk, SQL Server Management Studio, SuperMicro IPMI Utilities, Tera Term Pro, Teradici PCoIP Client, TOAD, Veeam, VMware Horizon View Client, X2Go Client, XMail Manager, XManager , Xshell, ZOC  <br>_**Deprecated sessions**_  <br>Box, Chrome Remote Desktop, Google Drive, GoToAssist, Intel AMT (KVM), Microsoft Azure Storage Explorer, Microsoft RD Gateway, Rebex (FTP, SSH, SCP), PuTTY, Spiceworks, XenServer |

### Credential management

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/integration-levels/#credential-management)

| Integration level | Credential management types |
| --- | --- |
| **Integration level 1** | SSH key, Devolutions Server privileged account, Devolutions Hub privileged account, RSA SecurID, X.509 certificate  <br>  <br>_**Generic entries**_  <br>username and password, password list, OTP, API key, access code, connection string |
| **Integration level 2** | 1Password, Bitwarden, Cerby, Dashlane, CyberArk, Delinea Secret Server, Dropbox Passwords, Hashicorp Vault, Hudu, IT Glue, IT Portal, Keepass, Keeper, LAPS, LastPass, Netwrix Password Secure, One Identity Safeguard, Passwordstate, Password Depot, Passbolt, Passwordstate, Pleasant Password Server, Proton Pass, Psono, Roboform, Sticky Password, TeamPass, Topicus KeyHub, True Key, Windows Credential Manager, Zoho Vault |
| **Integration level 3** | _**Addons**_  <br>  <br>_**Deprecated credential management types**_ |

# Workforce password management package - Devolutions Documentation

Workforce password management package
=====================================

The [**Workforce password management**](https://devolutions.net/solutions/#workforce-password-management)
 package simplifies credential management across teams and devices. Designed for business users and non-technical staff, it provides secure password storage, controlled sharing, and authentication policy enforcement while integrating with single sign-on and multiple platforms. Follow this checklist to set up your solutions securely and efficiently:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. Data sources are at the heart of Devolutions' ecosystem.<br><br>Discover the key differences between self-hosting and cloud-hosting in this blog article: [Decoding self-hosting vs. cloud-hosting](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |

### Companion tools

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/workforce-password-management-package/#companion-tools)

[Companion tools](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/devolutions-ecosystem/#companion-tools)
 bring additional features to Devolutions’ main solutions, such as credential brokering, PowerShell support, secure messaging, and much more.

#### Get started with Devolutions Workspace

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/support-resources/getting-started-packages/workforce-password-management-package/#get-started-with-devolutions-workspace)

The Workspace app are [applications](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/)
 that bring together Devolutions Hub Business and Devolutions Server into a single, centralized, cloud-based location. As for [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/)
, it is a free browser plugin to be used in conjunction with Remote Desktop Manager, Devolutions Server, and Devolutions Hub for secure password injection into websites.

*   [Workspace app](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-app/installation/)
    
*   [Workspace browser extension](https://docs.devolutions.net/workspace/workspace-browser-extension/installation/)

# Starter Pack - Devolutions Documentation

Starter Pack
============

The **Starter Pack** grants password, remote access, remote connection, and privileged access management features for teams of up to 5 users. Leverage all of Devolutions’ solutions and tools—no feature restrictions or hidden upgrades.

[Contact our sales department](mailto:sales@devolutions.net)
 if you wish to go over the limit of 5 users.

The checklist below contains all the steps to set up your solutions properly:

| CHECKLIST | DESCRIPTION |
| --- | --- |
| **Step 1 – Get started with a data source**<br><br>*   Cloud-based: [Create a Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/getting-started/create-hub/)<br>    <br>*   Self-hosted: [Create a Devolutions Server instance](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/getting-started/installation/create-server-instance/) | Create and configure a data source. Data sources are at the heart of Devolutions' ecosystem.<br><br>Discover the key differences between self-hosting and cloud-hosting in this blog article: [Decoding self-hosting vs. cloud-hosting](https://blog.devolutions.net/2025/03/decoding-self-hosting-vs-cloud-hosting)<br>. |
| **Step 2 – Register a license**<br><br>*   [In Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/server/web-interface/administration/security-management/licenses/)<br>    <br>*   [In Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/administration/management/licenses/) | Manage licenses by storing their serials in either Devolutions Server or Devolutions Hub. |
| **Step 3 – Install Devolutions Gateway**<br><br>*   [Devolutions Gateway installation and configuration](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/getting-started/) | [Devolutions Gateway](https://docs.devolutions.net/gateway/overview/what-is-gateway/)<br> provides authorized just-in-time (JIT) access to resources in segmented networks, thus increasing security. |
| **Step 4 – Get started with Remote Desktop Manager**<br><br>*   [Remote Desktop Manager checklist for enterprises](https://docs.devolutions.net/rdm/getting-started/checklist-enterprises/) | The Remote Desktop Manager application is used to manage and centralize remote access technologies, privileged passwords, documents, and shared information. |
| **Step 5 – Get started with Devolutions PAM**<br><br>*   [For Devolutions Server](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/server/getting-started/)<br>    <br>*   [For Devolutions Hub](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/pam-service/) | Devolutions PAM is a robust, easy-to-deploy, and affordable privileged access management solution that balances productivity and security. |

# API - Documentation Devolutions

API
===

Les administrateurs accèdent à l'API de Devolutions Hub Business principalement via le module Devolutions PowerShell, qui expose des applets de commande pour gérer les données du Hub depuis PowerShell. Utilisant des objets PSHubContext, les scripts authentifient avec un utilisateur d'application et un secret, puis appellent des commandes pour créer, mettre à jour ou supprimer des entrées, des coffres et des utilisateurs de manière automatisée.

Dans les opérations quotidiennes, cette surface d'API est utilisée pour intégrer le Hub avec des pipelines de déploiement, des CMDBs ou des systèmes de rapport. Par exemple, vous pouvez utiliser le type d'exportation de script PowerShell pour générer des données JSON ou CSV et les alimenter dans des analyses externes, ou provisionner automatiquement de nouveaux coffres de projet et attribuer des groupes en fonction d'un script standardisé.

### Sujets connexes

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/fr/hub/concepts/advanced-concepts/api/#related-topics)

*   [Devolutions Hub PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/hub-powershell/)
    
*   [Module PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/hub-powershell/powershell-module/)
    
*   [Type d'exportation de script PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/tools/export/powershell-script-export-type/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Partagez vos commentaires](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

---

# API - Devolutions Documentation

API
===

Administrators access the Devolutions Hub Business API primarily through the Devolutions PowerShell module, which exposes cmdlets for managing Hub data from PowerShell. Using PSHubContext objects, scripts authenticate with an application user and secret, then call commands to create, update, or remove entries, vaults, and users in an automated way.

In daily operations, this API surface is used to integrate Hub with deployment pipelines, CMDBs, or reporting systems. For example, you can use the PowerShell script export type to generate JSON or CSV data and feed it into external analytics, or automatically provision new project vaults and assign groups based on a standardized script.

### Related topics

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/de/hub/concepts/advanced-concepts/api/#related-topics)

*   [Devolutions Hub PowerShell](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/hub-powershell/)
    
*   [PowerShell module](https://docs.devolutions.net/powershell/hub-powershell/powershell-module/)
    
*   [PowerShell script export type](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/tools/export/powershell-script-export-type/)
    

 [![Devolutions Forum logo](https://cdnweb.devolutions.net/images/projects/forum/logos/forum-icon-shadow.svg) Share your feedback](https://forum.devolutions.net/forums/176/documentation--documentation-requests)

# Check-out approvals - Devolutions Documentation

Check-out approvals
===================

Check-out approvals add an authorization step before a privileged account or sensitive entry can be checked out and used. In Devolutions PAM, this means a designated approver must validate the business need and duration before credentials are released, strengthening oversight and enforcing least privilege.

When Devolutions PAM is enabled with Devolutions Hub Business, users request access to privileged accounts, approvers handle these requests, and resulting activity appears in Privileged access reports, including dedicated check-out requests views. A typical use case is requiring team leads to approve temporary access to domain admin accounts during maintenance windows.

### Related topics

[](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/concepts/advanced-concepts/check-out-approvals/#related-topics)

*   [Check-out approvals](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/concepts/checkout-approvals/)
    
*   [Approve access to a privileged account](https://docs.devolutions.net/pam/hub/privileged-accounts/approve-access-privileged-account/)
    
*   [Privileged access](https://docs.devolutions.net/hub/web-interface/reports/privileged-access/)
